# Tempahlah — Project Context for Claude Code

> **Brand**: Tempahlah (domain: `tempahlah.com`). The product was previously branded "HomestayMY" — historical entries below still use that name; all live code/config now uses Tempahlah.

> **READ THIS FIRST** at the start of every session. This file is the source of truth for project state, decisions, and what's left to do.

---

## 🎯 What we're building

A multi-tenant **SaaS + Marketplace** for Malaysian homestay operators.

- **SaaS side**: each tenant gets a private booking page (or custom domain on paid tier) where they take direct bookings. No commission on direct bookings.
- **Marketplace side**: paid tenants opt-in to list properties on `tempahlah.com`, where guests browse/book. Platform takes **3% commission** on marketplace bookings only.
- **Three clients**: Web (Blade), PWA (same Blade + service worker), Native mobile (Flutter, tenant + staff only — guests use PWA).
- **Pricing**: Free RM 0 (1 property / 3 rooms / 20 bookings per month), Paid **RM 49/month** (unlimited + Toyyibpay + custom invoices + WhatsApp + dynamic pricing + 5 staff + custom domain + marketplace listing). 7-day trial of paid.

---

## 🔒 Locked Tech Stack

| Layer | Choice | Reason |
|---|---|---|
| Framework | **Laravel 12.58** | Latest stable |
| PHP | 8.3+ (8.4 dev) | Laravel 12 requirement |
| Web templating | **Blade** | SEO + simplicity |
| Reactive UI | **Livewire 4** (tenant dashboard + Filament admin) | No SPA, Blade-first |
| Light interactivity | **Alpine.js + Tailwind** | Public marketplace, guest pages |
| Admin panel | **Filament 5.6** (super-tenant admin) | Note: design doc said "3", upgraded to 5 for Livewire 4 compat |
| Database | **MySQL 8** (prod) — SQLite (local dev — see "Database notes") | User specified MySQL |
| Auth (web) | Session + CSRF | Default |
| Auth (API) | **Laravel Sanctum 4.3** | Flutter mobile + paid-tier API access |
| RBAC | **Spatie Permission 7** | Roles: super_admin, owner, manager, cleaner, laundry, guest |
| Feature flags | **Laravel Pennant** | Free/paid tier gating |
| Email | **AWS SES** | User specified |
| Storage | **AWS S3 + CloudFront** | Photos, invoice PDFs, KYC docs |
| Push | **Firebase Cloud Messaging** | Tenant + staff Flutter app |
| PDF | **barryvdh/laravel-dompdf 3.1** | Invoices/receipts |
| Image | **Intervention Image 4** | Resize, watermark, EXIF strip |
| Guest payments | **Toyyibpay** | One-off bills (deposit, balance) |
| Subscription billing | **Manual v1** (monthly invoice + payment link) → Billplz recurring v2 | Toyyibpay doesn't support recurring |
| Channel sync | **Google Calendar 2-way at launch**, Airbnb/Booking iCal v1.5 | User confirmed |
| Search | MySQL full-text v1 → Meilisearch v2 if traffic warrants | |
| Queue | Redis (ElastiCache) prod / database driver dev | |
| Testing | Pest (TBD — to confirm in Phase 2) | |

### Database notes
- Local dev: `.env` uses `DB_CONNECTION=sqlite` (zero-setup, MySQL was returning Access denied for root)
- Production: `DB_CONNECTION=mysql` (template in `.env.example`)
- All migrations MUST be MySQL-compatible (no SQLite-specific features like `WITHOUT ROWID`)
- When user provides MySQL credentials: switch local `.env` and run `php artisan migrate:fresh --seed`

---

## 🧱 Multi-tenancy model

- **Row-level isolation** via `tenant_id` discriminator column on every tenant-owned table
- `BelongsToTenant` trait on Eloquent models adds global scope + auto-fills `tenant_id`
- **Tenant context middleware** resolves current tenant from session (web) or Sanctum token (API)
- **Cross-tenant tables** (no `tenant_id`): `users` (guests), `marketplace_listings`, `guest_blacklist_entries`, `disputes`, `super_admins`, `audit_logs`
- Why row-level not schema-per-tenant: marketplace requires cross-tenant queries

---

## 👤 Roles & permissions

| Role | Scope | Access |
|---|---|---|
| `super_admin` | platform-wide | Filament admin panel — KYC review, blacklist appeals, disputes, MRR |
| `owner` | per tenant | Full tenant access incl. finances, staff, subscription |
| `manager` | per tenant | Bookings, calendar, no finance |
| `cleaner` | per tenant | Own assigned cleaning tasks only |
| `laundry` | per tenant | Own assigned laundry tasks only |
| `guest` | global | Books, reviews, gets reviewed/blacklisted |

A user record can serve multiple tenants via `tenant_users` pivot with role.

---

## 💰 Free vs Paid tier

| Capability | Free | Paid (RM 49/mo + 3% marketplace commission) |
|---|---|---|
| Properties | 1 | Unlimited |
| Rooms / property | 3 | Unlimited |
| Bookings / month | 20 | Unlimited |
| Staff accounts | 1 owner | 5 (any role mix) |
| Private booking page | ✓ | ✓ + custom domain |
| Marketplace listing | ❌ | ✓ opt-in per property |
| Payment gateway | Manual only | Toyyibpay + manual |
| Auto reminders | ❌ | ✓ (X days before checkin) |
| Google Calendar sync | 1-way | 2-way |
| Airbnb/Booking iCal | ❌ | ✓ (v1.5) |
| WhatsApp | Click-to-WA link | Business API auto-send |
| Custom invoice/receipt PDF | ❌ basic on-screen | ✓ tenant-designed, auto-emailed + in-app |
| Email branding | Platform | Tenant logo |
| Cleaner/laundry auto-scheduling | Manual | Auto from bookings |
| Maintenance + inventory alerts | Basic | Full |
| Dynamic pricing | ❌ | ✓ |
| Reports & exports | 30 days, screen | Unlimited, CSV/PDF |
| Reviews + blacklist | ✓ | ✓ + public reply |
| API access (Sanctum) | ❌ | ✓ |
| Trial of paid | 7 days, no card needed | — |

---

## 🇲🇾 Malaysia-specific requirements

- **SST 8%** on accommodation if tenant exceeds threshold (configurable per tenant)
- **Tourism Tax RM 10/night** for foreign guests at registered accommodations
- **MOTAC license** field on properties — optional, with "MOTAC verified ✓" badge if filled and approved
- **PDPA compliance**: cookie consent, data export, right to be forgotten, audit log
- **Languages**: BM + EN at launch with toggle; URL-prefixed routes `/ms/...` and `/en/...` for SEO
- **Currency**: RM only at launch (USD/SGD auto-convert deferred to v2)
- **Geographic**: all Malaysia from day 1
- **Tenant persona**: user-friendly, mobile-first, BM-primary (must work for kampung homestay owners AND boutique operators)

## 🔐 Critical config notes

### Environment files
- `.env` — local dev (SQLite, no real credentials)
- `.env.example` — template (MySQL + all integration vars)

### Required external accounts (set when going to staging/prod)
- AWS account with SES, S3, RDS, ElastiCache provisioned (region `ap-southeast-1`)
- Toyyibpay merchant account (sandbox: `dev.toyyibpay.com`)
- Google Cloud project with Calendar API enabled + OAuth client
- Firebase project for FCM
- WhatsApp Business API approval (paid tier)
- Billplz merchant account (v2)

### Security baseline
- All KYC fields (MyKad, bank account) encrypted at app layer (AES-256 via Laravel cast)
- S3 buckets PRIVATE, signed URLs only (5-min expiry)
- Rate limits per `RateLimiter::for(...)` — see `app/Providers/AppServiceProvider.php` boot()
- Webhook signature verification required (Toyyibpay HMAC-SHA256)
- HTTPS only via CloudFront

---

## 📐 Conventions

### Code
- PSR-12 + Laravel default Pint config
- Eloquent over query builder unless perf-critical
- Models in `app/Models/`, traits in `app/Models/Concerns/`
- Form requests in `app/Http/Requests/{Web,Api}/`
- Policies in `app/Policies/`
- Livewire components in `app/Livewire/`
- Filament resources in `app/Filament/Admin/Resources/`
- Filament panel: route prefix `/super-admin`

### Multi-tenancy
- Every tenant-scoped model uses `BelongsToTenant` trait
- Never query `tenant_id` directly — let global scope handle it
- For super-admin cross-tenant queries: explicit `Model::withoutGlobalScope(BelongsToTenant::class)`

### Migrations
- Every tenant-scoped table starts with `tenant_id` foreign key
- Composite index `(tenant_id, ...)` on common query columns
- Use `ulid()` for public-facing IDs (bookings, properties), bigint auto-inc for internal
- Foreign keys: `cascadeOnDelete()` only when child can't exist without parent

### Naming
- Routes: `tenant.bookings.index`, `marketplace.search`, `admin.tenants.show`
- Permissions: `bookings.view`, `bookings.create`, `invoices.refund`, etc.
- Feature flags: `feature_paid_tier`, `feature_whatsapp_business`, `feature_marketplace_listing`

### 🎨 Brand colours & chart palette
**Always colour UI + charts with the CSS theme tokens, not raw hex.** Tokens live in `resources/css/app.css :root` and are **per-tenant** (a Pro/Ultra tenant's brand palette overrides `--primary/--secondary/--accent` at runtime via `Tenant::themeCssVariables()` injected in `layouts/app.blade.php`), so a hardcoded hex ignores the tenant's brand and drifts from the rest of the app. Platform defaults:

| Token | Default | Use for |
|---|---|---|
| `--primary` | `#2596c6` (brand blue) | primary actions, 1st chart series, active nav |
| `--secondary` | `#2cb8c4` (teal) | 3rd chart series, secondary accents |
| `--accent` | `#e8b94a` (**brand yellow/gold**) | 2nd chart series, the "Bookings"/revenue bars on the Reports chart |
| `--ok` | green (oklch 62% 155) | success, "paid", 4th chart series |
| `--warn` | amber (oklch 72% 75) | warnings, deposit state |
| `--err` | red (oklch 58% 25) | errors, blacklist alerts, "unpaid" |
| `--info` | blue (oklch 60% 250) | info |

Each token also has `-tint` / `-hover` / `-deep` variants. **Multi-series chart palette** (e.g. per-homestay lines in `Dashboard::revenueSeries()`): order **`var(--primary)` → `var(--accent)` → `var(--secondary)` → `var(--ok)`** (blue → yellow → teal → green — max adjacent contrast, all on-brand), then fall back to distinct hues `#8b5cf6` `#ec4899` `#ef4444` `#f59e0b` only for the rare 5th+ series. **Don't** put two blues adjacent (the old `#2563eb` line-2 clashed with the brand-blue line-1). `var(--…)` works in SVG `stroke=`/`fill=` presentation attributes here, so use tokens in inline charts too.

## 🚦 How to resume work in a new session

1. **Read this file first.**
2. Run `TaskList` to see current state.
3. Find the lowest-numbered `pending` or `in_progress` task.
4. Mark it `in_progress` if not already, then continue.
5. Update tasks as you complete them.
6. **Update this file** at the end of significant work — especially the "Current state" section below.

## 📊 Current state (update as you go)

> Last updated: 2026-07-19 — **"Send booking form" now lets the host set BOTH a custom stay price AND the pay-now / booking-fee amount (default RM 100 → e.g. RM 200) the guest pays to confirm — each tamper-proof via a purpose-bound HMAC.** The pay-now maps to `CreateBooking`'s `deposit_amount` (stay total unchanged; balance = total − pay-now); `App\Support\Booking\QuotedPrice` signs a `purpose` (`stay`|`paynow`) so the two amounts' signatures can't be swapped; `PublicBookingController::store` re-verifies on submit and forces the gateway bill to `TYPE_DEPOSIT` when a custom pay-now is set. Two independent optional toggles on the send-form. Verified end-to-end (purpose isolation + `deposit_amount=200` lands with total unchanged). See the top two "Recently shipped" entries. Prior: **"Send booking form" custom (agreed) stay price, tamper-proof via HMAC.** The sent link is a public URL, so a raw `?price=` would let the guest edit it down; instead the price rides in the link HMAC-signed (bound to tenant+property+dates+amount under `APP_KEY`, `App\Support\Booking\QuotedPrice`), auto-fetched from a new `POST /dashboard/bookings/sign-price` endpoint so the send-form's live link keeps working. `TenantHomeController::prefill()` verifies it for display and `PublicBookingController::store` re-verifies on submit before passing `base_amount` to `CreateBooking` (the accommodation subtotal, same semantics as the dashboard manual-booking override — SST/tax/fee added on top). A guest who edits the price or dates invalidates the signature → normal auto-pricing (never a silently-lowered total). Verified end-to-end (signer round-trips + rejects all tamper cases; a signed price sticks as `base_amount`/`total_amount` on a created booking with the original quote kept in `meta` for audit). Needs `view:cache` on deploy. See the top "Recently shipped" entry. Prior: **Fix: SecurePay balance payments (from the 7-day reminder) could stay unsettled — booking never auto-flipped to "Paid Full Payment".** The webhook dropped a genuinely-paid callback on any `invalid` checksum without consulting SecurePay's authoritative status API; now it falls back to `getPaymentStatus()` on any non-`verified` checksum (forgery-safe — a bad-checksum forgery still reports unpaid server-side), plus a new hourly `payments:reconcile-processing` safety-net command settles any stuck `processing` Toyyibpay/Billplz/SecurePay payment the gateway confirms paid. Verified via driven webhook (paid-settles / forgery-rejected / decline-still-fails) + reconcile dry-run. Needs **`queue:restart`** on deploy. See the top "Recently shipped" entry. Prior: **CONFIRMED trial policy: first-time tenants get a 30-day CARD-FREE Pro trial (no Stripe/card), reminder emails 3 days before it ends, then auto fall-back to Free.** All three pieces already shipped (registration `CreateTenantAndOwner` → `signup_trial_days=30`; `subscriptions:remind-trial-ending`; `subscriptions:process-lifecycle` downgrade) — this turn also bumped the subscription page + Stripe checkout trial 7 → 30 (`PAID_TRIAL_DAYS` default) so all copy reads 30. See the top "Recently shipped" entry. Trial length is `SIGNUP_TRIAL_DAYS` (30) / reminder lead `SIGNUP_TRIAL_REMINDER_DAYS` (3). 16 assertions pass; existing tenants untouched; DEPLOYED — needs **`queue:restart`** on deploy. Self-heals on the next View/Email/WhatsApp (renderPdf overwrites the stored file). Not yet deployed; see the top "Recently shipped" entry. Prior entry: **Direct purchase (skip the trial, pay today) added to Stripe checkout — a customer who wants Pro right now no longer has to go through the 7-day trial.** Previously the only way a fresh tenant reached Pro was the card-required 7-day trial (`StripeCheckoutController::checkout()` forced `trialDays = hasUsedTrial() ? null : trialDays()` — no way to skip). Now the checkout reads a `skip_trial` request flag: `trialDays = ($subscription->hasUsedTrial() || $request->boolean('skip_trial')) ? null : Subscription::trialDays()`. When `skip_trial=1`, no `subscription_data[trial_period_days]` is sent to Stripe, so Stripe **charges RM49 immediately** and starts auto-renew. The subscription page (`subscription/index.blade.php`) shows a secondary link-style CTA under the trial button — **"or subscribe now and pay today — skip the free trial"** — that POSTs to the *same* `tenant.subscription.stripe.checkout` route with a hidden `skip_trial=1`; only rendered when `$canStartTrial` (a fresh, never-trialed tenant), so a returning tenant's existing charge-now button is unchanged. **Verified** by driving the real `StripeBilling::createCheckoutSession()` with a faked Stripe API: trialDays=7 → payload **has** `trial_period_days`; trialDays=null (buy-now) → payload **omits** it (immediate charge). PHP + compiled Blade lint clean. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/StripeCheckoutController.php`, `resources/views/tenant/subscription/index.blade.php`. **Not yet deployed** (local change) — and, like the trial, only takes effect once Stripe keys + a recurring RM49 price are set. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; **do NOT `config:cache`**; no migration, no asset rebuild. Prior entry: **Reports & analytics is now Pro-only — free tenants can no longer access the reports dashboard or its PDF export.** The whole Reports feature was previously ungated (two flags `export_reports`/`reports_history_days` existed but were enforced nowhere). Added a new `reports` Pennant flag (`= isPaid()`) and gated it at the controller: `ReportController::index()` returns a new `tenant.reports.locked` upsell view (via `<x-pro-lock feature="reports">`) when the flag is inactive — building **no** report data for free tenants — and `exportPdf()` does `abort_unless(Feature::active('reports'), 403)` so a direct hit on `/dashboard/reports/export.pdf` is blocked too (crafted-request-proof). Bare `Feature::active('reports')` resolves against the current tenant via the default scope resolver. The sidebar Reports nav item is left in place — a free host clicking it lands on the upsell page. Files: `app/Providers/FeatureServiceProvider.php` (flag), `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/ReportController.php` (index gate + export abort), new `resources/views/tenant/reports/locked.blade.php`. **Verified** by driving the real controller in a rolled-back transaction: free tenant → `reports` flag NO → `index()` returns `tenant.reports.locked` + `exportPdf()` aborts 403; paid tenant → flag YES → full report. PHP + compiled Blade lint clean. **Not yet deployed** (local change). **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild. Prior entry: **AI Agent Pro now has a trainable Q&A knowledge base — auto-generated from the tenant's live info, editable/refinable by the host.** Extends the existing AI WhatsApp agent (shipped 2026-05-31) with a **Training Q&A** section on `/dashboard/integrations/agent`. On first visit (before the host has saved the FAQ) the panel **auto-seeds a starter set of question→answer pairs from the tenant's real data** — nightly rates, guest capacity, check-in/out times, booking fee + deposit policy, payment methods (bank details + gateway), cancellation/refund policy, location, facilities, SST/tourism-tax, house rules, and owner contact — each tagged `source: auto`. The host can **edit any answer, add their own questions, or delete pairs**; editing an auto pair promotes it to `source: custom`, and a **"Refresh from my info"** button rebuilds the auto pairs from the latest data while **keeping every custom/edited pair**. The saved FAQ is injected into the agent's system prompt as a `=== Trained answers (FAQ) ===` section (LLM keeps the owner's facts exact but rephrases in the guest's language; live tools still win for availability/quotes). **No migration** — stored as `training_qa` (+ `training_qa_seeded`) in the existing `tenant_integrations.config` blob (provider=`agent`, encrypted array), matching the `custom_knowledge` pattern; capped at 40 pairs. New `App\Services\Agent\TrainingQaGenerator` (only emits a pair when the data exists — never fabricates; dedupes identical check-in/out windows). Edits: `AgentSettings` (+`trainingQa`/`trainingQaSeeded` + `normalizeQa()`), `SystemPromptBuilder`, `AgentConnect` Livewire (mount seeding + `addQa`/`removeQa`/`regenerateQa`/`updatedTrainingQa` source-promotion + `save`), `config/agent.php`, `agent-connect.blade.php` (Training Q&A card). **Verified** by driving the real generator + prompt builder against the local DB (9 pairs generated; regenerate-merge keeps edited-auto + hand-written-custom pairs; prompt renders the FAQ, absent when empty; `normalizeQa` drops junk; check-times dedupe). PHP + compiled Blade lint clean. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + **`queue:restart`** (changed `SystemPromptBuilder`/`AgentSettings` are cached by the `agent` queue worker); no migration, no asset rebuild. Prior entry: **Setup checklist now gates a final "Share your booking link" step that dismisses the whole "Get set up" card when clicked.** A first-time host only finishes onboarding once the core steps are green — **Add your homestay · Add a room and set a nightly rate · Publish your homestay · Tell guests how to pay you** (+ **Connect WhatsApp** for paid tenants). Until every core step is done, the final **Share your booking link** step renders **locked** (a padlock chip, not a button). Once they're all ✓ the step unlocks into a filled **Share your booking link →** button; clicking it opens the public booking page in a new tab (a real user-gesture `window.open`, so it isn't popup-blocked) **and** fires a Livewire action (`Dashboard::shareBookingLink()`) that stamps `tenants.booking_link_shared_at` — which re-renders and makes the checklist `complete`, so the "Get set up" card **removes itself**. The share step is also satisfied by a real `Booking` existing (the honest proof the link works), so established tenants never see the card. The Livewire action **re-checks the lock server-side** before stamping (a crafted request can't skip setup). Prior entry: **Fix: the balance reminder can now ask for the FULL stay total (deposit kept as a refundable security deposit), not total−deposit.** A host reported that when a guest had paid the RM 100 deposit on an RM 1,600 booking, the auto "pay before check-in" reminder asked for the RM 1,500 balance — but the host wants the guest to pay the **full RM 1,600** and then **refunds the RM 100 deposit after check-out** (so the RM 100 is a separate security deposit, not a part-payment). This matches the platform's own default invoice terms ("Full payment must be made before check-in. Prior entry: **Two-way Airbnb + Booking.com calendar sync (iCal) — Pro feature, built & verified.** Hosts keep all three calendars in step so a booking on any channel blocks the dates everywhere (no double-bookings). **Per room, two directions:** (1) **Export** — each room gets an unguessable public busy-feed `GET /calendar/{token}.ics` (bookings + all blocks, all-day VEVENTs, checkout-exclusive) the host pastes into Airbnb + Booking.com; (2) **Import** — the host pastes each OTA's iCal URL; an hourly `channels:sync-ical` command (+ a "Sync now" button) fetches, parses and reconciles reservations into `CalendarBlock` rows (`source=airbnb|booking`, `source_uid`=iCal UID, idempotent upsert; events that vanish from the feed = cancellations → removed), which `AvailabilityService` already honours. **Reused dormant scaffolding**: `ChannelIntegration` table (ical import/export urls, last_sync_*), `CalendarBlock.source/source_uid`, the `ical_channel_sync` Pennant flag. **New**: `IcsWriter`/`IcsParser` (hand-rolled RFC 5545 — NO composer dep, since prod deploy never runs `composer install`), `ChannelCalendarSync` service, `ChannelSyncController` + a dedicated dashboard page with step-by-step Airbnb/Booking linking guidance, public `ChannelFeedController`, `SyncChannelCalendars` command, `rooms.ical_export_token` migration, `ical-feed` rate limiter. **Pro-gated** everywhere (`ical_channel_sync` = isPaid): free tenants get an Upgrade tile and the controller/command refuse to sync. **Verified — 45 assertions** on a throwaway migrated DB: export ICS shape (VCALENDAR, checkout-exclusive DTEND, no guest PII, stable UIDs), round-trip parse, import creates blocks + blocks availability, re-sync removes cancelled reservations while leaving manual/other-channel blocks untouched, a non-calendar response never wipes blocks, public feed returns `text/calendar` (bogus token → 404), the dashboard page renders for a paid tenant, free tenants redirect. ### 📌 Update protocol
**Whenever a feature is implemented, fixed, or removed**, update this section the same turn — don't defer. Bump the "Last updated" date and add a one-line entry to the "Recently shipped" log below. Move from "skeleton" to "completed" as work is fleshed out. Move blockers off the TODO list as they're resolved.

### 🆕 Recently shipped (newest first)
- **2026-07-19** — **Fix: a refundable booking fee no longer inflates the guest's "estimated total" — the `deposit_is_security` setting now properly excludes the deposit from the stay total (was left in, double-counting).** Host report (custom booking fee RM 200 on an RM 1,300 stay): the public page showed **Estimated total RM 1,500** (1,300 + 200) and — worse — with `deposit_is_security` ON the pre-checkin reminder chased the full RM 1,500 *plus* the RM 200 already paid, so the guest would pay RM 1,700 and the host would net RM 1,500. The host uses the fee as a **refundable deposit** (refunded after check-out), so the stay total should read **RM 1,300** with the RM 200 shown separately and returned → net RM 1,300. Root cause: `deposit_is_security` (added 2026-07-12, default ON) made the *reminder* treat the deposit as separate but **still added the booking fee to `total_amount`**, so the deposit was counted twice. **Fix — completed the setting's intended semantics**: in `CreateBooking`, when `Tenant::depositIsSecurity()` the booking fee is **NOT added to `total_amount`** (stay total = accommodation + SST + tourism only) and becomes the pay-now amount (a new deposit branch, wins over the last-minute "pay in full" rule); non-security tenants are **unchanged** (fee still added). New `Booking::securityDepositAmount()` (= `booking_fee_amount` in security mode, else 0) is the single source every surface reads. Display updated consistently: the **public page** (`PublicHomeBuilder` passes `depositIsSecurity`; Alpine `grandTotal()` excludes the deposit, new `securityDeposit()` renders a separate "Refundable deposit · returned after check-out" line below the estimated total, in both the summary card and the book-form recap) and the **invoice/receipt PDF** (booking fee stays in the total only in non-security mode; in security mode it's a "Refundable deposit" line below the grand total + a "not included in the total above" note). `reminderAmountDue()` already chases the full stay total in security mode (2026-07-12), so the balance is correct. **Verified** end-to-end (rolled back): security → total RM 1,300, deposit RM 200, reminder RM 1,300, guest pays RM 1,500 gross, refund 200 → **net RM 1,300**; non-security → total RM 1,500, net RM 1,500 (unchanged); real invoice render shows total RM 1,300 + separate refundable-deposit line, no stray RM 1,500; all PHP lints clean, all Blades compile. Files: `app/Actions/Booking/CreateBooking.php`, `app/Models/Booking.php` (+`securityDepositAmount`), `app/Services/Public/PublicHomeBuilder.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`, `resources/views/pdf/invoice.blade.php`. **Note**: `deposit_is_security` defaults ON, so every tenant with a booking fee now shows it as a refundable deposit excluded from the total — a host who treats the fee as a kept, non-refundable charge should untick "Deposit is a refundable security deposit" in Settings → Payment & refund policy (their total then includes the fee as before). **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild.
- **2026-07-19** — **Fix + rename: the "Send booking form" custom amount now overrides the actual BOOKING FEE (fee line + total + pay-now all update), and the toggle is renamed "Set booking fee manually".** Host report: after ticking the custom-amount toggle and entering e.g. RM 200, the public page's **Booking fee line still showed RM 100** (unchanged). Root cause: the previous cut overrode only the *pay-now* (`deposit_amount`), which the guest sees as "Pay now", but the separate **"Booking fee" line** (`feeAmount()` = the property's `booking_fee_amount`, RM 100) — which is also added to the total — was untouched, so it stayed RM 100. Since the host thinks of this amount AS the booking fee, the override now targets the booking fee itself: **`CreateBooking` gained a `booking_fee` override** (added to the total + becomes the pay-now, exactly like the property default); `PublicBookingController::store` passes the verified agreed amount as BOTH `booking_fee` and `deposit_amount` (so it holds even on a last-minute booking) and still forces the gateway bill to `TYPE_DEPOSIT`; the public page's `feeAmount()` returns the signed fee while the guest keeps the quoted dates, so the **fee line, the total (= subtotal + fee), and the pay-now all reflect it consistently**. Renamed the send-form toggle **"Set the pay-now amount" → "Set booking fee manually"** (+ field "Booking fee (RM)", updated hints + WhatsApp message wording). Signing path unchanged (still purpose-bound HMAC, `purpose=paynow` internally; guest can't edit it in the URL, changing dates drops it → property default). **Verified**: driving the real `CreateBooking` with `booking_fee=200` → fee line RM 100→200, total = base + 200, pay-now RM 200, balance = base (rolled back); all PHP lints clean, both Blades compile, no leftover renamed-var references. Files: `app/Actions/Booking/CreateBooking.php` (booking_fee override), `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php` (feeAmount override + signedFee state), `resources/views/tenant/bookings/send-form.blade.php` (rename + copy). **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild.
- **2026-07-19** — **"Send booking form": host can also set the pay-now / booking-fee amount (default RM 100) the guest pays to confirm — e.g. RM 200 — tamper-proof.** Follow-up to the custom-stay-price change (same day): the host confirmed they wanted to set the **pay-now / deposit** amount (the RM 100 booking-fee default the guest pays immediately), not just the stay total. That maps cleanly to `CreateBooking`'s existing `deposit_amount` override (flat pay-now amount, balance = total − this; **stay total unchanged**). Generalised `App\Support\Booking\QuotedPrice` to sign a **purpose** (`stay` | `paynow`) folded into the HMAC payload, so a signature minted for one amount can never be replayed as the other. The **send-form** now has two independent optional toggles — "Set a custom stay price" (existing) and "Set the pay-now amount" (new) — each debounce-fetches its own signed value (`signPrice` gained a `purpose` param) and appends `&price/&psig` and/or `&fee/&fsig` to the live link (WhatsApp message notes both). `TenantHomeController::prefill` verifies each with its purpose; the **public page** shows the host-set pay-now (`depositAmount()` returns it while the guest keeps the quoted dates, capped at the grand total) via hidden `fee`/`fsig`; `StoreBookingRequest` accepts them; `PublicBookingController::store` **re-verifies on submit** (purpose=`paynow`) → passes `deposit_amount` to `CreateBooking`, and forces the gateway bill to `TYPE_DEPOSIT` (never `TYPE_FULL`) when a custom pay-now is set so a last-minute booking isn't mislabeled fully-paid on settlement. Editing the amount or dates invalidates the signature → falls back to the property's booking fee. The Alpine send-form logic was refactored to a generic per-field structure (`fields.stay` / `fields.paynow`, shared `scheduleSign(key)`/`refreshSign(key)`/`has(key)`) — the shipped stay-price behaviour is unchanged. **Verified**: signature purpose-isolation (stay/paynow sigs differ, each only verifies under its own purpose, cross-purpose + tamper rejected); driving the real `CreateBooking` with `deposit_amount=200` → pay-now RM 200, **total unchanged**, balance = total − 200 (rolled back); all 5 PHP files lint clean, both Blades compile, no stale renamed-var references. Files: `app/Support/Booking/QuotedPrice.php` (purpose), `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php` (`signPrice` purpose), `resources/views/tenant/bookings/send-form.blade.php` (two toggles + generic Alpine), `app/Http/Controllers/Public/TenantHomeController.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`, `app/Http/Requests/Public/StoreBookingRequest.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild.
- **2026-07-19** — **"Send booking form": the host can now set a custom (agreed) price the guest pays — tamper-proof.** Host request: when sending a guest a prefilled booking-form link (`/dashboard/bookings/send-form`), let the host set the exact agreed price (a discount / special whole-house rate) instead of the calendar rate. **The wiring was already half-there** — `CreateBooking` honours a `base_amount` accommodation override (used by the dashboard manual-booking "Accommodation price" field), but the public "send form" flow never passed it and always recomputed via `PricingEngine`. The catch: the sent link is a **plain public URL the guest can edit**, so a raw `?price=` would let a guest lower what they pay. **Built HMAC-signed** so the agreed price is tamper-proof while keeping the live-link UX (signature auto-fetched, no extra button). **Pieces**: new `App\Support\Booking\QuotedPrice` (`sign`/`verify`/`normalizeAmount`, HMAC-SHA256 over `tenant|property|check_in|check_out|amount` under `APP_KEY`, `hash_equals`); new `POST /dashboard/bookings/sign-price` (`BookingController::signPrice`, tenant-scoped, returns `{price, sig}` for the exact stay); the **send-form** gains an optional "Set a custom price" toggle → RM field that debounce-fetches a signature and appends `&price=…&psig=…` to the live link **only when the sig matches the current property + dates** (a stale sig is never emitted; the WhatsApp message total reflects the custom price too); `TenantHomeController::prefill()` **re-verifies** the sig and only surfaces the price when it checks out (display-only); the **public booking page** shows the agreed price (`subtotal()` returns the signed amount while the guest keeps the quoted dates — change a date and it cleanly falls back to per-night calendar pricing), with a "✓ Price agreed with the host for these dates" note + hidden `price`/`psig` fields; `StoreBookingRequest` accepts `price`/`psig`; and `PublicBookingController::store` **re-verifies server-side on submit** (the real security boundary — the GET-time check is only for display) and passes `base_amount` to `CreateBooking` only when valid. A guest who edits the price, the dates or the property invalidates the signature → normal auto-pricing, never a silently-tampered lower total. The override is the **accommodation subtotal** (SST / tourism tax / booking fee still added on top, deposit still the booking fee) — identical semantics to the dashboard manual-booking override. **Verified**: `QuotedPrice` round-trips and rejects every tamper case (edited price / dates / tenant / missing sig); driving the real `CreateBooking` with a verified signed price → `base_amount = RM 1,550`, `total_amount = RM 1,550`, `price_overridden = true`, original PricingEngine quote (RM 600) preserved in `meta.quoted_accommodation` for audit (rolled back, dev DB untouched); all 5 changed PHP files lint clean; both Blades compile; the new route resolves. Files: new `app/Support/Booking/QuotedPrice.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php` (+`signPrice`), `routes/web.php`, `resources/views/tenant/bookings/send-form.blade.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/TenantHomeController.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`, `app/Http/Requests/Public/StoreBookingRequest.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild, no `queue:restart`. **⚠️ Do NOT `config:cache` in a way that changes `APP_KEY`** — the signature is keyed on `APP_KEY`, so a key rotation invalidates in-flight (already-sent) links; prod's key is stable, so this is a non-issue in practice.
- **2026-07-19** — **Fix: a SecurePay balance payment (from the 7-day reminder) could stay unsettled — booking never auto-flipped to "Paid Full Payment".** Host report: a customer paid the booking fee **manually**, the daily lifecycle reminder minted a SecurePay **balance** link, the customer paid it — but the booking stayed showing an outstanding balance. Root cause: a `TYPE_BALANCE` SecurePay payment only auto-settles via **(a)** the gateway webhook (`SecurePayWebhookController`) or **(b)** the return-page reconcile, and BOTH have a gap that this exact booking hits. **The webhook dropped a genuinely-paid callback whenever its checksum verified as `invalid`** — it flagged and returned WITHOUT consulting SecurePay's authoritative server-side status API (unlike the `missing` branch, which already falls back to `getPaymentStatus()`). This booking is the perfect trap: the fee was paid manually, so the SecurePay checksum path was **never exercised for the deposit** — the balance is the **first real SecurePay FPX callback**, and real callbacks carry a broader `fpx_*` field set than the synthetic verification, so a checksum divergence surfaces here for the first time and the paid balance is silently discarded. The return-page backup only fires if the customer returns to it (FPX users routinely close the tab at the bank success screen), and there was **no scheduled sweep** re-reconciling stuck `processing` payments — so once both triggers missed, the payment stayed `processing` forever. **Fix (two parts)**: **(1)** `SecurePayWebhookController` now falls back to the authoritative server-side `getPaymentStatus()` on **any** non-`verified` checksum (invalid *or* missing) before giving up — a genuinely-paid order settles even when our checksum computation diverges; a forged callback with a bad checksum still can't settle because SecurePay's status API (Basic-auth'd, server-to-server) reports it unpaid. **(2)** New hourly command **`payments:reconcile-processing`** (`ReconcileProcessingPayments`, scheduled in `routes/console.php`) — a safety net that asks the gateway directly about every stuck `processing` Toyyibpay/Billplz/SecurePay payment (older than `--minutes=10`, newer than `--days=14`) and settles any the gateway confirms paid, via the shared `SettlePaymentSuccess`. Idempotent + authoritative (only ever CONFIRMS payment → can never wrongly settle an unpaid booking). **Verified** by driving the real webhook in rolled-back transactions on the local DB with `Http::fake` for the status API: **(A)** bad checksum + server-confirms-paid → payment `succeeded` + `balance_paid_at` stamped + booking reads `paid_full` ✅; **(B)** bad checksum + server-says-unpaid → NOT settled, `invalid_signature` (forgery-safe) ✅; **(C)** verified genuine decline → still `markAttemptFailed`, not settled (no regression) ✅; the reconcile command dry-runs clean and is scheduled hourly. PHP lint clean on all 3 files. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Webhooks/SecurePayWebhookController.php`, new `app/Console/Commands/ReconcileProcessingPayments.php`, `routes/console.php`. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + **`queue:restart`** (the changed webhook controller + new command class are class-cached by workers); the hourly scheduler already runs; no migration, no view/asset change. **Unstick the affected customer now**: on the booking detail page → **Edit → "Mark fully paid"** (the money already reached the tenant's SecurePay account — verify in the SecurePay dashboard first). **Follow-up**: if the real-callback checksum keeps diverging, capture one real callback's field set (now logged as `invalid` in `payment_transactions`) and align `verifyChecksum`.

Both public surfaces already prefer per-locale fields (`public-tenant/home` + `marketplace/show` read `description_bm ?: description_en`), so guests see the right language with no view change. **Verified — 17 assertions** driving the real `store()` in a rolled-back transaction (tenant comped to Ultra in-test to lift the free 1-property cap): whole-house EN/BM carry name, "Kluang, Johor", "3-bedroom/3 bilik tidur", RM250 flat-rate phrasing, 8 guests, facilities list, "3:00 PM"/"3:00 petang" check-in; typed description kept verbatim with BM left null; per-room + minimal inputs (no amenities/bathrooms) renders "books separately" with the facilities + bathroom sentences correctly absent; create form renders the collapsed toggle + hint with the old always-open label gone. PHP + compiled Blade lint clean. Files: new `app/Services/Properties/DescriptionGenerator.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/PropertyController.php` (store: blank → generate), `resources/views/tenant/properties/create.blade.php`. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild, no `queue:restart`. **Note**: existing properties are untouched (create-flow only); a host can still hand-edit both language fields on the property edit page.
- **2026-07-16** — **Fix: the AI agent still offered a deleted homestay (Waiz) and asked customers "which homestay?" after the host deleted it.** Root cause: deleting a property (`PropertyController::destroy`) **soft-deletes** it (recoverable by design) and leaves `status=active` on the row — but every AI-agent property query used **`withoutGlobalScopes()`**, which strips not only the tenant scope (the intended part — the WhatsApp webhook/queue run without tenant context) but **also the `SoftDeletingScope`**. So the deleted homestay kept appearing in the agent's system-prompt catalogue and its tools, and with 2 "active" properties the agent naturally asked which one. Same bug class as the 2026-07-14 marketplace-listing fix. **Fix**: all 7 query sites — `SystemPromptBuilder` (catalogue), `TrainingQaGenerator`, and the `ListProperties`/`GetPropertyInfo`/`CheckAvailability`/`ShareLocation`/`GetQuote` tools — now use `->withoutGlobalScope(BelongsToTenantScope::class)` instead, so SoftDeletes stays applied (the CLAUDE.md convention for cross-context queries). The explicit `where('tenant_id', …)` each already carries keeps tenant isolation. A **restored** property reappears automatically. **Verified** in a rolled-back transaction driving the real classes: before delete → prompt + `list_properties` include the 2nd homestay; after soft-delete → prompt, `list_properties`, `get_property_info` (on the deleted id) and the training-QA generator all exclude it. PHP lint clean on all 7 files. Files: `app/Services/Agent/SystemPromptBuilder.php`, `app/Services/Agent/TrainingQaGenerator.php`, `app/Services/Agent/Tools/{ListPropertiesTool,GetPropertyInfoTool,CheckAvailabilityTool,ShareLocationTool,GetQuoteTool}.php`. **DEPLOYED 2026-07-17** (`042f204`, push → auto-deploy → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + `queue:restart`) and **verified live on prod**: the real built system prompt for tenant 1 now lists exactly **1** property, zero "Waiz" mentions, and the stored Training QA is clean too — so no host action was needed (no "Refresh from my info" required; Custom knowledge unaffected). **Note**: soft-deleting Waiz did NOT remove its `demo:waiz` seeded data — the tenant's grand-total earnings may still include the fake RM 11,600; run `sudo -u www-data php artisan demo:waiz --remove --property=9` on prod if the host wants those purged.
- **2026-07-16** — **Fix: editing a booking's customer name didn't change the name on its invoice/receipt PDF (host report, booking BK-260709-Z9K2P).** The host renamed the guest ("Mohd Zul Fadzli bin Marzuki" → "… / Muhammad Hariz bin Musa") in the booking Edit form — which correctly syncs the lead `BookingGuest` + linked `User` — but View PDF still printed the old name. Root cause: `GenerateInvoice` snapshots the guest contact into `invoices.billed_to` at issue time, and the PDF's bill-to block (`pdf/invoice.blade.php`) **preferred that snapshot** (`$invoice->billed_to['name'] ?? $booking->guestName()`), so even though `BookingDocumentController::renderPdf()` re-renders the PDF fresh on every View/Email/WhatsApp (the 2026-07-04 fix), it re-rendered with the stale name. Fix (view-only): **flipped the precedence for the contact block** — live booking guest first (`guestName()`/`guestEmail()`/`guestPhone()`), snapshot as fallback for old bookings whose guest rows are gone/incomplete; placeholder-email filtering (`Booking::isRealEmail`) still applies to both sources. The invoice **number, line items and amounts stay snapshotted as-issued** — only the contact block goes live. No data migration: every existing document self-heals the next time the host clicks View PDF / Email / WhatsApp (renderPdf overwrites the stored file). **Verified** by rendering the real `pdf.invoice` view against a fixture in a rolled-back transaction: stale snapshot + edited guest → the new combined name renders and the stale-only name is gone; deleting the live guest rows → falls back to the snapshot name; a real snapshot email prints when the booking has none (an `example.com` snapshot email is correctly suppressed as a placeholder). Compiled Blade lint clean. File: `resources/views/pdf/invoice.blade.php`. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild, no `queue:restart`. **Host tip**: after deploy, just open the invoice/receipt again (View PDF or re-send) — the document regenerates with the corrected name.

The host didn't want that opener. - **2026-07-15** — **Housekeeping: auto start/complete of forgotten tasks + a typical-cost assumption (host request).** Two asks: (1) auto-tick cleaning/laundry the host forgets, via a toggle; (2) record a typical price so those jobs still count toward cost history/reports even when no cost was typed — plus a way to edit those prices. Confirmed decisions: **one flat cleaning price + one flat laundry price** (not per-type), cost **applied at completion** (keeps future/unfinished tasks + reports honest — matches the "price the past, leave the future blank" rule), and auto-complete **available on every plan** (auto-*scheduling* from bookings stays Pro).
  - **New command `housekeeping:auto-complete {--dry-run}`** (`app/Console/Commands/AutoCompleteHousekeepingTasks.php`, hourly in `routes/console.php`, mirrors `AutoCheckoutBookings`' `withoutGlobalScopes()->with('tenant')`→chunk pattern). **Cleaning**: past `scheduled_at + duration` (duration defaults 180 min) → **completed** + typical cost applied; inside the window (`now >= scheduled_at`, still pending) → **auto-started** (in_progress, no cost). **Laundry**: past `expected_return_at` (or `pickup_at + 24h` when none) → **returned** + typical cost; between pickup and return → **picked_up**. Gated per task by `Tenant::autoCompleteHousekeepingEnabled()`. Never touches completed/skipped/cancelled/returned tasks; explicit host-entered cost always wins (only null is filled). **Timezone-correct**: housekeeping datetimes carry MYT wall-clock face values (the same convention the `DispatchCheckoutReminders` fix addressed), so the due-check reinterprets each stored value in `Asia/Kuala_Lumpur` before comparing — a plain UTC `now()` compare would fire ~8h off.
  - **Typical prices**: `Tenant::defaultCleaningCost()` / `defaultLaundryCost()` (column value if set incl. 0, else platform default `DEFAULT_CLEANING_COST = 60.00` / `DEFAULT_LAUNDRY_COST = 130.00` — Wafa's figures) + `autoCompleteHousekeepingEnabled()` (defaults ON). New reusable `CleaningTask::applyTypicalCostIfMissing(Tenant)` / `LaundryTask::applyTypicalCostIfMissing(Tenant)` — the single cost rule, used by both the command and the manual paths.
  - **Manual completion also applies the typical cost** (`HousekeepingController`): the `complete`/`return` action buttons and the edit-form status→completed/returned paths now fill a null cost with the tenant default (via `applyTypicalCostIfMissing`), so a manual tick behaves identically to the auto path.
  - **Settings**: new **"Auto-complete & typical costs"** card (`settings/index.blade.php`, right after "Housekeeping automation") — the `auto_complete_housekeeping` toggle + **Typical cleaning cost (RM)** / **Typical laundry cost (RM)** inputs (pre-filled from the accessors). Deliberately **not** wrapped in the Pro-disabled fieldset (available on all plans). `SettingsController::update()` validates the three keys and writes the boolean unconditionally (cost keys flow through the existing `fill($validated)`; blank → null → platform typical).
  - **Schema**: migration `2026_07_15_120000_add_housekeeping_auto_complete_and_default_costs.php` (idempotent) adds `tenants.auto_complete_housekeeping` (nullable bool) + `default_cleaning_cost` / `default_laundry_cost` (nullable decimal 10,2).
  - **Verified** (rolled-back txns on the migrated local DB, `Carbon::setTestNow`): the command auto-completes an overdue cleaning (+RM60), auto-starts an in-window one (no cost), returns an overdue laundry (+RM130), picks up an in-window one, preserves an explicit cost, `--dry-run` writes nothing, toggle-off skips everything — and the MYT reinterpretation proven (real MYT 20:00 while `now()`=12:00 UTC still completes a "12:30"-scheduled task). Manual `updateCleaning`/`updateLaundry` complete/return apply the typical cost (explicit cost preserved). `/dashboard/settings` renders 200 with the toggle + both pre-filled price fields; a real `update()` round-trips the values (unchecked box saves OFF). All PHP + compiled Blade lint clean; migration applied locally. Files: the migration, `app/Models/{Tenant,CleaningTask,LaundryTask}.php`, `app/Console/Commands/AutoCompleteHousekeepingTasks.php`, `routes/console.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/{HousekeepingController,SettingsController}.php`, `resources/views/tenant/settings/index.blade.php`. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy runs the migration) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + **`queue:restart`** (new command class is cached by workers); the hourly scheduler already runs. - **2026-07-15** — **Fix: the property Edit form had no "Bedrooms" field — a whole-house homestay's bedroom count couldn't be changed after creation.** The create form asks for `bedrooms` (required) and `store()` stores it on the single "Whole house" `Room`'s `beds` column (whole-house properties have exactly one synthetic room; `Property::bedroomCount()` reads `rooms->first()->beds` for whole-house, `rooms->count()` for per-room). - **2026-07-15** — **Bookings list: the "Upcoming" filter now includes a currently-active stay at the top (was hidden), so it reads current-at-top → future-at-bottom just like "All".** A host noted the Upcoming list didn't lead with the current date the way All does. **The ordering was already identical** (both `BookingController::index` filters sort `check_in` ascending — today/nearest at top, far-future at bottom; verified live: All and Upcoming both ascending). The real gap was the **filter**: Upcoming used `check_in >= today`, which **excludes an in-progress stay** — a pending/confirmed booking that started *before* today but hasn't ended yet — so All showed that ongoing booking at the top while Upcoming skipped straight to the next future arrival. Fixed by keying the Upcoming filter on **`check_out >= today`** instead (pending/confirmed stays that haven't ended = current + upcoming); the existing ascending order then places the ongoing stay at the very top, matching All. **Verified on live prod data** (read-only): the new Upcoming leads with the ongoing `2026-07-13 → 07-17` stay then `07-25, 07-26, …` ascending (identical to All's top); zero already-ended stays leak in (`check_out < today` count = 0); total moved 18 → 19 (the one previously-hidden current stay). The `checked-in` tab still owns `checked_in`-status guests, so there's no overlap. PHP lint clean. - **2026-07-14** — **Cross-tenant customer blacklist — hosts report problem guests in the Guests menu; super admin verifies; a verified guest triggers a red alert at every other homestay before a booking is accepted.** Full feature over the previously-dormant `guest_blacklist_entries` scaffolding (table + `GuestBlacklistEntry` model + a Filament resource existed but were never wired to any tenant/in-app flow). **Trust model**: a tenant files a report (**pending**) → a platform admin **verifies** it → an **approved** entry is the platform-wide mark. Nothing flags other homestays until verified. **(1) Tenant side (Guests menu)**: each guest row links to a new **guest profile page** (`/dashboard/guests/{guest:id}`, `GuestController@show` — bound `{guest:id}` because User's route key is `public_id` via `HasUlidPublicId`) showing stay history + verified platform-wide flags + this tenant's own reports + a **report form** (severity: note/warning/blacklist · reason: property damage / unpaid / **rude behaviour (kurang ajar)** / noise / overcapacity / house rules / fraud / other · description). `GuestController@report` creates the entry **pending**, snapshotting the guest's **normalized phone + email + name** (cross-tenant matching needs these — a returning guest at a different homestay is often a *different* User row, since `resolveGuest()` dedupes on email only). Guarded: only a homestay that has actually hosted the guest can report them (`abort_if(! $lastBooking, 403)`). Sidebar gains a "Guest blacklist" item (alert icon). **(3) Alert on booking**: `GuestBlacklistEntry::approvedFlagsFor(userId, phone, email)` matches **verified** entries by user id OR normalized phone OR case-insensitive email — surfaced as a **red banner** on the booking detail page (the surface where a host confirms/marks-paid, i.e. "before accepting") with a "View guest profile" link, plus a **⚠ Flagged** badge in the bookings list (desktop + mobile) and on the guests list. Deliberately a **warning, not a hard block** (so it can't break public gateway auto-confirm bookings) — the host sees it and decides. **Schema** (`2026_07_14_140000_extend_guest_blacklist_entries`, idempotent): adds `guest_name`/`guest_phone`/`guest_email`/`reviewed_by_user_id` + a `(guest_phone, review_status)` index. **Verified — 21 assertions, 0 failures** (rolled-back txns on the migrated local DB, driving the real models + real `PlatformAdminController@reviewBlacklist` + real `GuestController@report`/`@show`): pending flags nobody; verify → approved + reviewer stamped → matches by user_id / raw phone / intl phone / case-insensitive email; **CROSS-TENANT: a different User row with the same phone is matched** (the returning-guest case); null identity never match-alls; topFlag picks most-severe; revoke lifts the flag; reject rejects without flagging; report() creates a pending entry with the normalized-phone snapshot; show() renders + **404s for a guest with no booking at this homestay** (can't report a stranger). - **2026-07-14** — **Fix: Platform Admin → Email marketing "Onboarding series" Sent counts kept counting deleted homestays (step 1 showed "Sent 5" when only 3 subscribers exist).** Same class of bug as the overview stat-cards + marketplace-listing fixes the same day. `PlatformMarketingController::index()` builds each step's `sent_total`/`skipped_total`/`failed_total` via `withCount(['sends as sent_total' => fn ($q) => $q->where('status','sent')])` — with **no check that the tenant still exists**. Deleting a homestay in Platform Admin only **soft-deletes** the tenant; its `onboarding_email_sends` rows survive, so a welcome email sent to a since-deleted host kept counting as "sent" while the "Total tenants / new subscribers" figure (soft-delete-scoped) dropped — hence "Sent 5" vs 3 live subscribers. **Fix**: each count closure now also `->whereHas('tenant')`, which applies Tenant's SoftDeletes global scope (`deleted_at IS NULL`) and drops orphaned rows whose tenant was hard-deleted — so the counts reflect only **live** tenants. Display-only; **self-corrects on next page load** (no data change, no migration). PHP lint clean. File: `app/Http/Controllers/PlatformMarketingController.php`. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (PHP-only; no migration, no view/asset change).
- **2026-07-14** — **Fix: the AI agent DM'd someone (Waheeda) out of nowhere after they posted a WhatsApp STATUS/STORY — the sidecar had no chat-type filter, so status/group/channel/broadcast messages were forwarded as if they were customer DMs.** A host reported the agent replying to a contact who had only updated their WhatsApp story, not messaged the business. Root cause: the Node sidecar's `messages.upsert` `'notify'` handler (`wa-sidecar/src/session-manager.js`) filtered `fromMe`, empty-text and stale messages, but **never checked the message's chat context**. WhatsApp delivers **status/story updates through the same `messages.upsert` event** with `remoteJid = 'status@broadcast'` and the poster's phone JID in `key.senderPn`. A **text status** therefore had non-empty text, passed the freshness gate, and `resolvePhoneNumberJid()` resolved `key.senderPn` → the poster's real number — so the sidecar forwarded it as a normal inbound and Laravel's agent replied to their story. The identical hole also exposed **group chats** (`@g.us`), **channels** (`@newsletter`) and **broadcast lists** (`@broadcast`). (Confirmed there's still no proactive/broadcast send path — every agent send only ever fires off an inbound, so this status-flush was the sole trigger.) **Fix**: new `isDirectChat(jid)` helper + a **hard guard at the top of the message loop** — only genuine 1:1 DMs (`remoteJid` ending `@s.whatsapp.net`, or `@lid` for multi-device LID-routed senders) are forwarded; `status@broadcast`, `@g.us`, `@newsletter` and `@broadcast` are dropped **before** JID resolution, before they can reach Laravel — so this protects the agent reply, the out-of-hours auto-reply and every other inbound path at once. **Verified**: `node --check` clean; an 8-case table proves status/story/group/channel/broadcast/undefined/empty all drop while `@s.whatsapp.net` + `@lid` DMs pass. File: `wa-sidecar/src/session-manager.js` only. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy pulls the file) → **restart the Node sidecar** (`systemctl restart <wa-sidecar unit>`) — the sidecar change ONLY takes effect on process restart, NOT php-fpm; no migration, no `view:cache`, no `queue:restart`.

- **2026-07-14** — **Fix: the property page's "🛏️ N rooms" under the homestay name was hardcoded to 1 for whole-house homestays (ignored the bedroom count the host entered).** A host reported the room/bathroom/toilet counts on `/dashboard/properties/{id}` looking hardcoded. - **2026-07-14** — **Fix: the AI agent WhatsApp'd a customer (Erwan) “out of the blue” the moment the host activated/connected the Wafa session — it was replying to an OLD message WhatsApp only just delivered.** Root cause: when a WhatsApp linked device reconnects, WhatsApp flushes every message that queued while it was offline; Baileys surfaces these as `messages.upsert` `type:'notify'` (new to the fresh socket, so the existing `type!=='notify'` history-sync filter didn't catch them). The sidecar forwarded them with `receivedAt=now` and Laravel stamped `WhatsappMessage.created_at=now`, so a weeks-old message looked brand-new. The existing stale-inbound guard (`agent.max_inbound_age_minutes`, 5) measured age from **`created_at`** (= webhook-receipt time ≈ now) → age ~0 → guard passed → the LLM replied (the *“maaf, saya ni AI assistant untuk urusan tempahan Wafa Homestay je…”* deflection). Confirmed there's **no** proactive/broadcast send path — every agent send only fires off an inbound — so the trigger was purely this stale-flush. **Fix (real send-time, end-to-end + defense-in-depth):** **(1) Sidecar** (`wa-sidecar/src/session-manager.js`): extract WhatsApp's true send time `m.messageTimestamp` (epoch **seconds**; handles protobuf-Long via `.toNumber()` and plain number), and **drop any inbound older than `MAX_INBOUND_AGE_SECONDS`** (new `config.js` key, default **300**, aligned with Laravel) right at the source — before it ever reaches Laravel, so it protects the agent reply, the out-of-hours auto-reply and every inbound path at once. **Fails open** when the timestamp is missing/0 (never swallows a genuine new message). Also now forwards `sentAtUnix` in the `message.inbound` payload. **(2) Laravel** (`WhatsappWebhookController`): parse `sentAtUnix` → real `$sentAt` Carbon; store it as `delivered_at`; add a **central freshness gate at the top of `maybeDispatchAgent`** (before conversation bookkeeping AND the out-of-hours reply — the out-of-hours path previously had NO stale guard) that returns early when `$sentAt` is older than the cutoff; pass `$sentAt->timestamp` to the job. **(3) `ProcessAgentReply`**: new `int $sentAtUnix` ctor arg; its stale guard now measures from the **real send time**, not `created_at` (falls back to `created_at` only when unknown) — so a queue backlog can't reply to a long-past message either. **Verified**: PHP + JS lint clean; drove the real `maybeDispatchAgent` (queue faked) — a 3h-old message **SKIPS** (dispatched=0), a 30s-old message **REPLIES** (dispatched=1) with `sentAtUnix` threaded to the job; proved the job guard now SKIPs a row whose `created_at` age is ~0 but real-send age is 180min (the exact offline-flush shape); node-tested the sidecar extraction/drop across number/Long/missing/zero shapes (8/8 pass, fails open on missing). Files: `wa-sidecar/src/{session-manager.js,config.js,.env.example}`, `app/Http/Controllers/Api/WhatsappWebhookController.php`, `app/Jobs/Agent/ProcessAgentReply.php`. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + **`queue:restart`** (changed `ProcessAgentReply` job class is cached by the `agent` worker) + **restart the Node sidecar** (`systemctl restart tempahlah-wa-sidecar` or its unit name — the sidecar change only takes effect on process restart, NOT php-fpm) and add `MAX_INBOUND_AGE_SECONDS=300` to the sidecar's `.env`. No migration, no asset rebuild.

- **2026-07-14** — **Fix: Platform Admin overview stat cards (Free / Subscribed / On trial / Past due / MRR) kept counting deleted tenants.** After a super admin deleted homestays, **Total tenants** dropped (correct) but Free/Subscribed/MRR stayed inflated. Root cause: `PlatformAdminController::stats()` derives every subscription figure from `Subscription::query()->groupBy('plan','status')`, but `Subscription` has **no** SoftDeletes/tenant scope and `destroyTenant` only **soft-deletes** the tenant (its `subscriptions` row is left intact) — so those rows kept counting, while `totalTenants` (`Tenant::count()`, which IS soft-delete-scoped) already excluded them → the mismatch (e.g. "Total 2" but "MRR RM49 · 2 active paid" from a deleted RM49 tenant). Fix: the stats query now `->whereHas('tenant')`, which applies Tenant's SoftDeletes global scope (and drops orphaned subs whose tenant was hard-deleted), so Free/Subscribed/On-trial/Past-due/MRR count only **live** tenants — consistent with Total tenants + the list. **Verified** by driving the real `stats()` in a rolled-back transaction: adding an active PRO RM49 tenant bumps paidActive/subscribed/MRR, and **soft-deleting it returns them to baseline**. PHP lint clean. File: `app/Http/Controllers/PlatformAdminController.php`. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (PHP-only; no migration, no view/asset change). **Note**: the numbers self-correct on the next page load after deploy — no data backfill needed (the deleted tenants' subscription rows are simply no longer counted).

- **2026-07-13** — **Fix: a new host's welcome email waited up to ~24h for the next scheduled batch — now it sends within seconds of registering.** Reported live: a host (mohd.eddie91@gmail.com) registered but received nothing; diagnosis on prod found the tenant fully eligible (active, day 0, email resolvable, not suppressed) — the daily `marketing:send-onboarding` batch (01:30 UTC/09:30 MYT) had simply already run *before* he signed up, so he was waiting for tomorrow's run. **Fix**: new `App\Jobs\SendOnboardingWelcomeEmail` dispatched from `CreateTenantAndOwner::execute()` right after the DB transaction commits (never from inside it — avoids a queue worker racing an uncommitted tenant row) — sends the day-0 step **immediately** at signup instead of waiting for the batch. Covers every registration path (manual `/register`, Google onboarding, referral signups) since they all funnel through this one action. **Self-healing on failure, by design**: if the immediate send throws (mail outage etc.), the job deliberately records **no** row — the existing daily command's "already handled" check is a blanket `exists()` over a tenant's send history, so a permanent failure row would silently block step 1 forever; leaving no row means tomorrow's scheduled batch retries automatically. A genuinely dead mailbox (bounce/complaint-suppressed) still records `skipped` immediately, matching the daily command's behaviour. The daily batch is otherwise unchanged — it still owns every step after day 0, still enforces one-email-per-tenant-per-day, and simply no-ops for step 1 on a tenant the immediate job already reached (checked by the same idempotent unique `(step, tenant)` row). **Verified — 9 assertions**: registration action dispatches the job; the job actually sends + records `sent`; re-running the job is a no-op (no duplicate); same-day daily batch doesn't double-send; **a forced real mail failure (invalid mailer, no network) leaves zero rows**, and the next daily-batch run recovers it automatically; a suppressed address at signup records `skipped` and is never mailed; a suspended tenant is untouched. - **2026-07-13** — **⚠️ Deploy-timing gotcha found the hard way: run `view:cache` only AFTER the auto-deploy has FULLY finished, and if `filemtime(): stat failed` 500s appear use `systemctl restart php8.4-fpm` (a graceful `reload` is NOT always enough).** After pushing the testimonial commit (`06f79b1`), a `view:cache` + reload was run the moment the commit appeared in prod's `git log` — the page served 200 once, then went **500 site-wide** with the documented `filemtime(): stat failed for storage/framework/views/….php` (OPcache `enable_file_override=On` + deleted compiled views). Root cause: the Hostiqo auto-deploy pipeline **keeps running after the commit is visible** (its later steps clobber/clear compiled views), so caching immediately after `git log` shows the new commit is a race. **Fix that worked**: `view:clear` + `view:cache` + **`systemctl restart php8.4-fpm`** (full restart) → 6 consecutive 200s. **Procedure going forward**: after a push, wait until the deploy is genuinely done (give it ~30–60s after the commit lands, or re-run the cache a second time), then `view:cache` + reload — and reach for `restart` instead of `reload` at the first `filemtime` error.

- **2026-07-13** — **Fix: resolving a maintenance ticket wiped the repair cost the host entered when creating it.** A host reported that a maintenance ticket's Repair cost showed empty in the table. Root cause: `HousekeepingController::updateMaintenance()` `resolve` branch did `'cost' => $cost` unconditionally, and the inline "Cost RM" box on the Resolve action is **blank by default** (placeholder only, no pre-filled value). So the common flow — create a ticket **with** a repair cost (saved as `open`, cost shows), then click **Resolve** leaving that small box empty — **overwrote the cost with null**. Fix: on resolve, only write `cost` when the box actually carries a value (`$costProvided`), otherwise keep the existing figure; a typed value still wins (host setting/correcting it at resolve time). The **create** store + the full **edit** form were already correct (edit's cost field is pre-filled, so a blank there is a deliberate clear). **Verified — 6 checks** on a migrated DB: create with cost 80 → resolve with empty box → cost STILL 80 (not wiped) + resolved/stamped; resolve with cost 130 typed → 130 wins; create with no cost → resolve sets 25. PHP lint clean. File: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/HousekeepingController.php`. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (PHP-only; no migration, no view/asset change). **Note**: existing tickets whose cost was already wiped by a prior resolve must have the cost re-entered via the ticket's **Edit** form.
- **2026-07-13** — **Fix: the Airbnb & Booking.com (iCal) integration tile stayed on "Set up" forever, even after the host pasted OTA calendar URLs — now flips to Connected / Manage.** A host added their Airbnb + Booking.com iCal URLs but `/dashboard/integrations` still showed "Set up". Root cause: the integrations index tile looks up its status in the **`tenant_integrations`** table (keyed by provider), but the channel-sync feature stores its iCal URLs in a **separate `channel_integrations`** table (per room, per channel) — so there was never a `channel_sync` row and the tile was permanently "Set up" (the exact same table-mismatch the WhatsApp tile had, which was special-cased). **Two fixes**: (1) `IntegrationController::index()` now **synthesizes a `channel_sync` record** (mirroring the WhatsApp synth) when the tenant has ≥1 **active** `ChannelIntegration` with a non-null `ical_import_url` — so the tile shows the green **Connected** pill + "since <when>". (2) The index view's button branch for **route-based tiles** (channel sync + Google Calendar) ran *before* the connected check, so it always said "Set up"; it now shows **"Manage"** once connected (still linking to that feature's own page, not the generic `integrations.show`). **Verified — 5 checks** on a migrated DB: no URL → "Set up"; after an active Airbnb import URL is saved → "Connected" pill + "Manage" (and "Set up" gone); an inactive channel → back to "Set up". PHP + compiled Blade lint clean. - **2026-07-13** — **Fix: installed PWA opened on the marketplace, not the dashboard, for a signed-in host — plus a latent Blade `@push`-in-CSS-comment bug on the same page.** A tenant opening the home-screen app (still logged in) landed on the traveller marketplace. Root cause is two-fold: **(1)** a PWA freezes its `start_url` at install time — installs made before 2026-06-10 are frozen on `/` (the manifest now says `/dashboard`, but that only helps NEW installs); **(2)** when the apex root became the marketplace search page, the old "authenticated → redirect to dashboard" behaviour on `/` was deliberately dropped, so those frozen installs now open the marketplace. **Fix** (in `marketplace/search.blade.php` head, inside `@auth`): a tiny inline script that redirects to `route('tenant.dashboard')` **only when** the page is running as an installed app (`matchMedia('(display-mode: standalone)')` or iOS `navigator.standalone`) **and** it's a cold launch (`document.referrer === ''`) — so a host browsing to the marketplace from inside the app, or any normal browser tab, is never bounced. Old installs self-heal with no reinstall. **Second bug found during verification**: the same view's WARM-PALETTE CSS comment contained a literal **`@push('head')`** — Blade compiles directives even inside CSS comments (same class as the documented 2026-07-04 `<x-…>`-in-comment incident), so the compiled view opened a real `startPush` output buffer that **swallowed the entire `<head>`** (DOCTYPE → title → manifest → my new script). Prod only rendered correctly by accident: the leaked buffer flushes to the client in the right order at request shutdown — fragile (any Content-Length/response-caching middleware would break it) and it made direct `->render()` verification impossible. Fixed by rewording the comment (no literal directive). **Verified** by driving the real `MarketplaceController::search()` in separate processes: anonymous → script absent; authed (`owner@demo.test`) → script present with the standalone + referrer guards and `replace('/dashboard')`; full document now renders from `<!DOCTYPE html>` with title + manifest intact; compiled Blade `php -l` clean, 0 stray `startPush`. Files: `resources/views/marketplace/search.blade.php` only. **Not yet deployed.** **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no migration, no asset rebuild. **Tenant tip**: reinstalling the home-screen app also picks up the new `/dashboard` start_url, but is no longer required.

- **2026-07-13** — **Bookings list: payment-method indicator (Online · <gateway> / Manual) + date-ordered (today at top, far-future at bottom).** Two host asks. **(1)** A host was confused that a gateway-paid booking still showed "direct" in the **Channel** column — because Channel is the booking *source* (direct / marketplace / walk-in), not how they paid. Past tab → most-recent stay first; deposit-due → nearest deadline first. **Also fixed a latent bug**: the Upcoming filter compared the `check_in` date column against a Carbon *datetime* (`$today`), so a booking whose check-in **is today** was bound against `…00:00:00` and wrongly excluded — now compares against a `Y-m-d` string (`$todayStr`), correct on MySQL + SQLite. **Verified — 8 checks** with `Carbon::setTestNow` (noon MYT): ALL → today→soon→far then past-recent→old; Upcoming → today included, at top, far at bottom; Past → recent first; plus the 3 payment-badge cases (gateway→Online·Billplz, manual→Manual, unpaid→none). - **2026-07-13** — **AI Agent no longer auto-replies to the host's own staff (cleaners, laundry, technicians) — only to guests.** A host worried the AI would answer their cleaner/laundry/maintenance crew as if they were a customer when those staff WhatsApp the connected number. Added an **internal-number guard** in `WhatsappWebhookController::maybeDispatchAgent()`: before creating a conversation or dispatching a reply, new `isInternalPhone()` checks whether the inbound number (E.164-normalized via `PhoneNumber::normalize`) matches any **Directory** `Cleaner` / `LaundryVendor` / `MaintenancePerson` phone for that tenant, or the tenant's own `business_phone` / agent `handoff_phone`. If so → **skip entirely** (no LLM call, no conversation row, logged). Directory models are `BelongsToTenant` and the webhook has no tenant context, so queried `withoutGlobalScopes()` with an explicit `tenant_id`. Phone matching is format-agnostic (`012-345 6789`, `0198887777`, `+60177776666` all normalize + match). Genuine guest numbers are unaffected — they still get a reply. Also (same session) **strengthened auto-detect language mirroring** in `SystemPromptBuilder`: the agent replies in the guest's language every message and switches if they switch (Malay→Malay, English→English). **Verified — 7 checks**: cleaner/laundry/technician + business/handoff numbers all resolve internal (agent skipped) regardless of stored format; a random guest number resolves NOT internal (agent replies). PHP lint clean. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Api/WhatsappWebhookController.php`, `app/Services/Agent/SystemPromptBuilder.php`. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + **`queue:restart`** (agent worker caches `SystemPromptBuilder`); no migration, no asset rebuild. **Host tip**: register crew in **Directory** (cleaners / laundry / maintenance) with their phone so the agent knows to skip them.

- **2026-07-13** — **Fix: calendars' "today" landed on the previous day between 00:00–08:00 MYT (app runs in UTC).** A host reported the booking calendar's date pointer/selection falling on 12 July when Malaysia was already on 13 July. Root cause is the standing `config/app.php` `'timezone' => 'UTC'` (Malaysia is UTC+8): every **server-side** `Carbon::today()` / `now()->toDateString()` used to seed a calendar returns the previous calendar day during the 00:00–08:00 MYT window. (The public booking page's Alpine calendar uses the browser's `new Date()`, which is already correct for a Malaysian guest — so only the server-computed calendars were wrong.) Fix: derive calendar "today" in the display timezone via the established `now(config('homestay.timezone', 'Asia/Kuala_Lumpur'))` pattern (same helper the invoice/booking-ref date stamps already use) — **storage stays UTC**, only the *calendar-date* derivations change. Spots fixed: `BookingController` (all three `$today` — bookings index filters, sendForm booked-warning, **new-booking calendar** `today`/min/prefill), `CalendarController` (dashboard calendar `todayIso`/`todayCursor`/default cursor, via a new `today()` helper), `MarketplaceController::searchDates()` past-guard, `marketplace/search.blade.php` date-picker `min`, `TenantHomeController::prefill()` guard, `PublicHomeBuilder` (60-day rate window start + booked-dates `check_out >=` cutoff). **Verified** with `Carbon::setTestNow('2026-07-12 17:30 UTC' = 01:30 MYT 13 Jul)`: old `Carbon::today()` → `2026-07-12` (bug reproduced), new derivation → `2026-07-13`; and driving the real controllers, the new-booking calendar `today` + dashboard calendar `todayIso` both emit `2026-07-13`. PHP + compiled Blade lint clean. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/{BookingController,CalendarController}.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Marketplace/MarketplaceController.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/TenantHomeController.php`, `app/Services/Public/PublicHomeBuilder.php`, `resources/views/marketplace/search.blade.php`. **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; **do NOT `config:cache`**; no migration, no asset rebuild. **Note**: left `config/app.php` on UTC deliberately — an app-wide timezone flip would reinterpret every stored timestamp and is the documented-risky path; this is the contained per-calendar fix.

- **2026-07-12** — **Marketplace availability filter: with both dates set, only homestays actually free for the range are shown.** Follow-up to the search redesign. `MarketplaceController::search()` now adds a SQL `whereExists` (only when `check_in` + `check_out` are both valid) that keeps a listing only if its property has **at least one room free** for the half-open range. Built as **raw correlated subqueries** (`from('rooms')` → `whereNotExists` bookings → `whereNotExists` calendar_blocks), NOT `whereHas`, so Room/Booking/Block **tenant + soft-delete global scopes never apply** (the marketplace is cross-tenant and may be browsed by a signed-in host). Overlap logic mirrors `AvailabilityService` exactly: bookings in `pending|confirmed|checked_in` with `check_in < checkOut AND check_out > checkIn`, plus room-specific OR property-wide (`room_id IS NULL`) blocks; `rooms.deleted_at IS NULL`. **Verified** against a migrated DB with a real listing + booking (dates inserted raw to sidestep the documented SQLite `date`-cast `H:i:s` quirk, i.e. MySQL-equivalent): exact/overlapping/enclosing ranges EXCLUDED; a free range INCLUDED; both half-open boundaries (check-in on a prior booking's checkout day, checkout on its check-in day) INCLUDED; a property-wide `CalendarBlock` EXCLUDES its range. **Note**: pure SQLite dev shows the checkout-day boundary wrong due to the `date` cast writing `Y-m-d H:i:s` (same quirk `AvailabilityService` has) — **prod MySQL stores clean DATE columns, so it's correct there**.
