- **2026-07-12** — **Fix: super-admin `/dashboard/admin/tenants/{id}/edit` 404'd (route-key binding by public_id).** The new tenant-editor route used `{tenant}` binding, but **Tenant's route key is `public_id` (ULID) via the `HasUlidPublicId` trait** — so binding looked for a tenant with `public_id="3"`, found none, and threw ModelNotFound → 404 (the overview link correctly passes the numeric `id`). Fixed by binding `{tenant:id}` on both `platform.tenants.edit`/`.update`. **Diagnosed on prod**: router matched `platform.tenants.edit` fine, but `(new Tenant)->resolveRouteBinding("3")` returned NULL while `Tenant::find(3)` worked → `getRouteKeyName()` = `public_id`. **Lesson: any admin route taking a numeric id for a model that uses `HasUlidPublicId` (Tenant, Property, Booking…) MUST use `{model:id}` or it 404s.** Deployed `3941c89` (push → auto-deploy → `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`); verified `/dashboard/admin/tenants/3/edit` → **200** with the form. **Also fixed a broader prod breakage the same session**: the earlier auto-deploys (`4446f25`/`4e84c46`) never had `view:cache` + php-fpm reload run, so OPcache (`enable_file_override=On`) was serving **stale compiled views** (`filemtime(): stat failed …`) and **stale PHP classes** (`Call to undefined method App\Models\Tenant::bookingLinkShared()`) site-wide — ran `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` to clear it. **Standing reminder: after EVERY push/auto-deploy, run `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (never leave prod on a bare deploy) — a bare deploy without the fpm reload 500s pages under OPcache.**

- **2026-07-12** — **Fix: invoices/receipts (and document numbers/booking refs) showed the previous day between 00:00–08:00 MYT — app runs in UTC.** Host reported an invoice sent "today" (12/7 MYT) printing the day before. **Root cause**: `config/app.php:83` hardcodes `'timezone' => 'UTC'` (ignores `APP_TIMEZONE=Asia/Kuala_Lumpur` in `.env`), so `now()` is UTC; Malaysia is UTC+8, so any Malaysian *calendar date* derived from `now()` between midnight and 8 AM MYT lands on the previous UTC day. Confirmed reproduction: at `2026-07-12 01:30` MYT, `now()->toDateString()` = `2026-07-11`.
  - **Approach (contained, not an app-wide flip)**: kept storage in UTC — stored `datetime` timestamps (`paid_at`, `checked_out_at`, …) are correct absolute moments and were **not** touched (an app-wide `config('app.timezone')` flip would reinterpret all historical UTC rows 8h off — the documented-risky path, deliberately avoided again). Instead, every **Malaysian-calendar-date stamp** and every **guest-facing date display** now converts to MYT via a new central config `config('homestay.timezone')` (default `Asia/Kuala_Lumpur`, override `APP_DISPLAY_TIMEZONE`).
  - **Key insight**: `check_in`/`check_out` are `date` casts (no time → never shift), and the guest **emails + WhatsApp only ever print those**, so they were already correct and needed no change. The only real shift is `datetime`-derived dates, which all live on the invoice/receipt path.
  - **Fixes**: business-date **stamps** — `GenerateInvoice` `issued_on`, `Booking` reference `BK-ymd`, `InvoiceTemplate`/`SubscriptionInvoice` number year, `SettingsController` sample-invoice preview; guest-facing **display** — `pdf/invoice.blade.php` receipt "Paid on" (`paid_at`) + the `issued_on` fallback; plus host-facing dashboard timestamps for consistency (`bookings/show` payment time, `payments/index`, `livewire/tenant/dashboard` published date, `platform/overview` + `platform/testimonials` join dates). `diffForHumans()` displays left as-is (relative → tz-agnostic).
  - **Verified**: all 6 PHP files + all compiled Blade lint clean; a `Carbon::setTestNow('2026-07-12 01:30 MYT')` harness proves the exact bug (UTC → `11.07.2026`) now renders `12.07.2026`, booking ref `BK-260712`, and the receipt Paid-on date shows `12 Jul 2026`. **Not yet deployed** (local working tree). **Deploy**: push (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; **do NOT `config:cache`** (prod runs config uncached; `WhatsAppService` still calls `env()`). No migration, no asset rebuild. Note: the `2027` the host mentioned has no code path for the issue date (renders `d.m.Y`); the confirmed defect is the day-off (11 vs 12) — a screenshot would clarify if a stray `2027` genuinely appears anywhere.

- **2026-07-11** — **Stripe recurring subscriptions (true auto-renew) for the RM 49/mo Pro plan — built, DEPLOYED, ships DORMANT** (`efbdcef`). The recurring rail going forward; **supersedes the Billplz card-tokenization work** built earlier today (left dormant, not ripped out). Migration ran on prod; with no Stripe keys `enabled()=false`, the Stripe UI is hidden, the webhook 409s — `/dashboard/subscription` renders 200, nothing changed for any tenant.
  - **Why Stripe over Billplz**: Stripe **auto-charges every cycle and runs its own dunning/retries**, so there is **no daily charge command** for Stripe-managed subs — the webhooks drive state. Billplz never had native recurring (its Tokenization is card-only, off by default, can't tokenize FPX).
  - **Approach**: hosted **Checkout** (`mode=subscription`) + **Customer Portal** (manage/cancel/update-card) + **webhooks**. **Raw `Http::` + manual webhook-signature verification** — **NO `stripe/stripe-php` dependency**, because prod auto-deploy is `git reset --hard + migrate`, **not `composer install`**, so a new package would fatal on deploy; and all 4 existing gateway clients already use raw Http + manual HMAC. Keys in prod **`.env`** (platform-owned, per Stripe's own best-practices — never the DB).
  - **Webhook signature** (`StripeBilling::verifyWebhookSignature`): parse `Stripe-Signature: t=…,v1=…`, compare `hash_hmac('sha256', "{t}.{rawBody}", whsec)` via `hash_equals`, reject if `|now-t|>300s`. **Must read `$request->getContent()` (raw body), never the parsed array.**
  - **Files**: config `platform_billing.stripe` block; migration `2026_07_11_140000` (adds `stripe_customer_id/stripe_subscription_id/stripe_price_id`); `Subscription::isStripeManaged()`; new `StripeBilling` service + `StripeException` (implements the `PaymentGatewayException` marker); `SubscriptionBillingService::applyStripeSubscription()` (single owner of Stripe→local state); `StripeCheckoutController` (checkout/portal/return) + `StripeWebhookController` (`POST /api/webhooks/stripe`, idempotent via `WebhookEvent` **`stripe:` prefix**); routes; `SubscriptionController::index` passes `stripeEnabled`; card-first `subscription/index.blade.php` ("Subscribe with auto-renew" → Stripe; "Manage subscription" → portal; Billplz FPX pay-link kept as fallback).
  - **Status map** (`applyStripeSubscription`): `active|trialing`→paid+active; `past_due|unpaid`→past_due + grace (isPaid stays true mid-retry); `canceled|incomplete_expired`→downgrade to free; `incomplete`→ignore. Comped-safe, idempotent. **Both daily commands (`bill-cycle`, `process-lifecycle`) skip subs with a `stripe_subscription_id`** — Stripe drives them.
  - **Real bug caught in verification**: the status branches first used `$updates += [...]` (array-union), which does **NOT overwrite existing keys** — so the canceled branch's `stripe_subscription_id => null` was silently ignored (the key was already set in the base array). Switched all three branches to `array_merge`. **Lesson: `+=` on arrays keeps the left value for duplicate keys; use `array_merge` when a later block must overwrite.**
  - **Verified — 25 assertions** against a throwaway migrated SQLite DB in a rolled-back transaction, Stripe faked via one URL-routing `Http::fake` closure: created→paid/active + ids/period stored + `ai_agent` flag active; idempotent replay (`stripe:` WebhookEvent); **forged signature → 400, changes nothing**; `payment_failed`→past_due+grace (still `isPaid()`); `deleted`→free with the stripe id cleared; `checkout.session.completed` resolves via `retrieveSubscription` + activates; comped keeps its comp; commands exclude stripe subs; request shapes (basic auth `secret:`, `mode=subscription`, `line_items[0][price]`, customer, `client_reference_id`). **Plus** `SubscriptionController::index()` rendered for stripe on/off + free-tenant — **the exact path that 500'd on the last feature; this time I drove the real controller, not just a compiled-Blade lint.** All 13 PHP files + compiled Blade `php -l` clean. Two harness snags were tinker-scoping only (`global $WH`/counters not populating the global symbol table; `Illuminate\Support\Str` is not a `Facades\Str`) — not code.
  - **NOT verified end-to-end** — no live Stripe keys in this env (outbound HTTP faked). A **real test-card Checkout + a genuine signed webhook** (Stripe CLI / dashboard) is a required follow-up before switching on.
  - **To switch on** (Stripe Dashboard, sandbox first): (1) create a **recurring Price** MYR 49.00/mo → `price_…`; (2) configure the **Customer Portal** (allow cancel + card update); (3) add a **webhook endpoint** `https://tempahlah.com/api/webhooks/stripe` subscribed to `checkout.session.completed`, `customer.subscription.created|updated|deleted`, `invoice.paid`, `invoice.payment_failed` → copy the `whsec_…`; (4) put `STRIPE_SECRET_KEY` (`sk_test_…` first), `STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, `STRIPE_PRICE_ID` (+ `STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`) in prod `.env`; (5) test a card, then swap to live keys. **Deploy of the code itself is done**: migration ran, `view:cache` + fpm reload + `queue:restart` applied. **Do NOT `config:cache`** (WhatsAppService still calls `env()`).
- **2026-07-11** — **Billplz card auto-renew (Tokenization, Visa/Mastercard) for the RM 49/mo Pro subscription — built, DEPLOYED, ships DORMANT** (`6a877d5`, + fixes `f05c0f8`, `75724dc`). Layers true auto-charge on top of the existing pay-link cycle. Migration ran on prod (batch adds the card columns); with no `BILLPLZ_API_KEY` + `BILLPLZ_TOKENIZATION` off, nothing changed for any tenant — `/dashboard/subscription` renders 200, feature inert. **Two post-deploy fixes** — both from the SAME root cause worth remembering:
  - **`f05c0f8`** — `SubscriptionController::index()` called `$billing->tokenizationEnabled()`, but I'd added that method to `PlatformBillplz`, not the injected `SubscriptionBillingService` → **`/dashboard/subscription` 500'd** ("Call to undefined method"). My verification drove `SubscriptionCardController` + the service directly and **never called `SubscriptionController::index()`**, and a compiled-Blade `php -l` can't catch a runtime method call. Fix: a `tokenizationEnabled()` passthrough on the service, mirroring `configured()`. **Lesson: exercise every controller that renders the changed view, not just the new one.**
  - **`75724dc`** — the view referenced `<x-btn-submit>`, a component from **another session's uncommitted working-tree edits**. `subscription/index.blade.php` was already ` M` (dirty) at session start; when I `git add`ed it I **swept in the other session's `x-btn-submit` swaps** and committed a view depending on `components/btn-submit.blade.php`, which is **untracked and not on prod** → 500 "Unable to locate component [btn-submit]". Local checks passed only because the component exists in my working tree. Fix: reverted all 5 to plain `<button type=submit>` (prod-before-my-commit had zero x-btn-submit here). **Lesson (recurring): in this repo several sessions edit the same files at once — before `git add`ing a file that's already ` M`, diff it against HEAD and isolate your own hunks; don't assume your edit is the only change.**
  - **Why it's dormant**: gated on a new `homestay.platform_billing.tokenization` flag (`BILLPLZ_TOKENIZATION`, default **false**) **on top of** `configured()`. With creds set but the flag off (the prod default), `configured()=true` but `tokenizationEnabled()=false` — pay-link billing works exactly as before, the card UI is hidden, the daily command never auto-charges. **Verified inert.** Billplz keeps Tokenization off by default (paid plan, email support@billplz.com; **Visa/MC only, cannot tokenize FPX/Amex**), so this can't be switched on until they enable it on the platform account.
  - **Design (locked with the user)**: **card-first checkout** — "Subscribe with auto-renew (card)" is the primary Pro button, with a smaller "pay once by FPX" link (the existing `checkout` path) for bank users; and **enroll + charge now** — the enrollment callback immediately charges the outstanding cycle via the fresh token, so enabling auto-renew subscribes in one step.
  - **Billplz v4 flow (verified from docs)**: `POST /v4/cards` (name/email/phone/callback_url) → `{id, authentication_redirect_url}` → tenant does hosted 3DS → Billplz POSTs the token to `callback_url` with an **X-Signature computed the same way as bill callbacks**. Then each cycle: mint the bill (`/v3/bills`) → `POST /v4/bills/{id}/charge` (`card_id`+`token`) → **reconcile via `getBill` before settling** (never trust the sync charge body). **Reuses the existing `BILLPLZ_COLLECTION_ID` — no new collection.**
  - **Files**: migration `2026_07_11_120000` (adds `auto_renew, card_id, card_token(encrypted), card_last4, card_brand, card_status` to `subscriptions`; token **encrypted** cast per security baseline); `Subscription` (fillable/casts + `CARD_ACTIVE` + `hasChargeableCard()`); `PlatformBillplz` (+`tokenizationEnabled()`, `createCard()`, `chargeCard()` [**no auto-retry** — a charge isn't idempotent], `cardCallbackSignatureStatus()` delegating to `BillplzClient::verifySignature` verbatim); `SubscriptionBillingService` (+`storeCard()`, `chargeSavedCard()` reusing `settle()`/`reconcile()`/`issueInvoice()` — the single owner of "advance the period"); new `SubscriptionCardController` (`enroll` → 3DS redirect; public checksum-verified `callback` at `POST /api/webhooks/subscription-card`, idempotent via `WebhookEvent` **`card:` prefix**; `toggle` auto-renew); routes in web.php + api.php (api group has no CSRF — no `bootstrap/app.php` change); `ProcessSubscriptionBilling::issueDueBills` auto-charges a card-on-file sub and **falls back to the pay-link email on decline** (never uncharged AND un-notified); card-first UI in `subscription/index.blade.php` gated on `tokenizationEnabled`.
  - **Cardholder email trap avoided**: Tenant has **no `email` column** (it's `business_email`); `createCard` uses `owner?->email ?: business_email`, NOT the existing `createBill`'s `$tenant->email` which silently resolves null.
  - **Verified — 30 behaviours** against a throwaway migrated SQLite DB in a rolled-back transaction, Billplz faked via one URL-routing `Http::fake` closure (avoids the first-match-wins shadowing gotcha): valid+active callback stores the token (**ciphertext ≠ plaintext in the DB row**), charges once (basic auth `apiKey:`, `card_id`+`token`, `/v4/bills/{id}/charge`), settles the invoice and advances the period; **replay is idempotent** (`card:` WebhookEvent, no second charge); a **forged X-Signature stores nothing, charges nothing, 200** (not 401); a **declined** charge keeps the token but marks the invoice `failed` and doesn't advance; `bill-cycle` **auto-charges a card sub** and **leaves a no-card/FPX sub on the pay-link email** (regression guard, `SubscriptionInvoiceMail` asserted queued); a **comped** sub refuses billing; **flag off → `createCard` refused + UI hidden**; and `createCard`'s request shape (sandbox base, owner email, callback, 3DS redirect). All PHP + the compiled Blade `php -l` clean.
  - **NOT verified end-to-end** — no real Billplz Tokenization account exists yet (outbound HTTP faked). A **real sandbox 3DS card run is a required follow-up** before switching on.
  - **To switch on** (later): (1) email support@billplz.com to enable Tokenization on the platform Billplz account; (2) set platform `BILLPLZ_*` + `BILLPLZ_TOKENIZATION=true` in prod `.env`; (3) sandbox-test one card. **Deploy**: `php artisan migrate --force`, `view:cache`, `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`, **`queue:restart`** (touches the `ProcessSubscriptionBilling` command class). **Do NOT `config:cache`** (WhatsAppService still calls `env()`).
- **2026-07-11** — **SES bounce + complaint handling — the prerequisite for taking the account out of the SES sandbox.** Groundwork so that once production access is granted, a hard bounce or spam complaint can never drag Tempahlah's sender reputation down.
  - **Why now**: the 2026-07-10 finding that prod SES is still in **sandbox mode** (every guest address rejected, `81 × MessageRejected`). Getting out is an AWS request, and AWS reviewers reject accounts with no bounce/complaint plan — this is that plan.
  - **I could NOT submit the sandbox-exit request from here** — the server's only AWS key (`tempahlah-ses`, account `920876082929`) is send-only: `ses:GetAccount` returns `AccessDeniedException`, and `ses:PutAccountDetails` (the API that requests production access) is likewise denied. It's a **console action for the account owner**, and rightly so — it commits the business to AWS's sending-policy attestations. The owner was given exact console steps + a drafted, accurate use-case description (transactional only, triggered by the recipient's own booking).
  - **DNS pre-check (the #1 rejection reason) — mostly good**: `SPF` = `v=spf1 include:amazonses.com -all` ✓; `DMARC` present but `p=none` with `rua=mailto:rua@dmarc.brevo.com` (a **stray Brevo address** from a prior setup — reports go to Brevo, not us; flagged for a later one-line DNS fix); **no MX** (domain can't receive — fine, SES handles bounces itself); **DKIM** couldn't be confirmed blind (owner told to verify "Successful" in the SES console before requesting access).
  - **What shipped** (all new, no changes to existing behaviour): 
    - `email_suppressions` table (migration `2026_07_11_000000`, idempotent, MySQL+SQLite) — `email` unique+lowercased, `reason` (bounce|complaint), `subtype`, `diagnostic`, `suppressed_at`. **Deliberately NOT `BelongsToTenant`**: a mailbox belongs to a person, shared across every tenant they book with, and the webhook runs with no tenant context.
    - `App\Models\EmailSuppression` — `isSuppressed()` (10-min cache on the hot path, busted on write), idempotent `suppress()` (updateOrCreate, so SNS redelivery + repeat bounces don't duplicate).
    - `App\Support\Aws\SnsMessageVerifier` — **hand-rolled SNS signature verification**, because the AWS SDK's `Aws\Sns\MessageValidator`/`Message` classes are **absent from the installed pruned aws-sdk-php 3.383.1 build** (`class_exists` = false; it's only there transitively via flysystem-s3 for SnsClient). Validates the `SigningCertURL` is a genuine `sns.<region>.amazonaws.com` host (the anti-forgery guard), rebuilds the canonical string-to-sign in AWS's mandated field order per message Type, and `openssl_verify`s it (SHA1 for SignatureVersion 1, SHA256 for 2). Cert PEM cached 24h by URL.
    - `App\Http\Controllers\Webhooks\SesNotificationController` on `POST /api/webhooks/ses` (`throttle:webhook-ses`, 120/min) — reads the raw body (SNS posts `Content-Type: text/plain`, so `$request->json()` won't parse it), verifies the signature (bad → 403), auto-confirms `SubscriptionConfirmation`, and on `Notification` suppresses **Permanent** bounces + **Complaints** while **leaving Transient bounces alone** (mailbox-full is temporary; SES retries). Always 200 for authentic-but-uninteresting messages so SNS doesn't retry-storm. Optional `SES_SNS_TOPIC_ARN` pins the accepted topic.
    - `App\Listeners\HaltMailToSuppressed` on Laravel's `MessageSending` event (registered in `AppServiceProvider::boot`) — **one choke point for every mailable**, now and future. Returns false (aborts the send) only when every `To` is suppressed; a message with a live recipient still goes. So a bounced guest silently stops receiving email while WhatsApp (a separate path) is unaffected.
  - **Verified** end-to-end through the real HTTP kernel against a throwaway DB with a genuine openssl-signed SNS payload — **19 assertions, zero failures**: valid signature verifies / tampered payload + untrusted cert host both rejected; a forged webhook → 403 and suppresses nothing; a permanent bounce suppresses the (lowercased) address with its diagnostic; a transient bounce does **not**; a complaint suppresses; replay creates no duplicate; subscription confirmation auto-handled; and — driven through the actual mailer + array transport — a message to a suppressed address **never reaches the transport** while a clean one does.
  - **Owner still has two console tasks**: (1) request SES production access (the drafted content is ready); (2) create an SNS topic subscribed to `https://tempahlah.com/api/webhooks/ses` and point the SES identity's Bounce+Complaint notifications at it — the webhook auto-confirms the subscription. Optionally set `SES_SNS_TOPIC_ARN` in prod `.env` afterward to pin it.
  - Files: new `database/migrations/2026_07_11_000000_create_email_suppressions_table.php`, `app/Models/EmailSuppression.php`, `app/Support/Aws/SnsMessageVerifier.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Webhooks/SesNotificationController.php`, `app/Listeners/HaltMailToSuppressed.php`; edited `app/Providers/AppServiceProvider.php` (listener + rate limiter), `config/services.php` (`sns_topic_arn`), `routes/api.php`. **Migration runs on auto-deploy**; no asset rebuild, no view change. Deploy = push + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (new classes + provider change; do NOT `config:cache`).

- **2026-07-10** — **"Send booking form" — the host sends a guest a prefilled link to their own booking page, for a manual booking paid by bank transfer.** New page at **`/dashboard/bookings/send-form`** (button on the bookings list, beside "+ New booking"; on phones it sits under the filter strip since it has no floating counterpart).
  - **Deliberately no invite table and no signed token.** The tenant's booking page is *already public*, so a signed per-guest link would add a token, an expiry and a `booking_invites` migration while protecting nothing a guest couldn't reach anyway. The link is simply the public page with query params: `{slug}.tempahlah.com/?property_id=3&check_in=…&check_out=…&guests=5&pay=manual`. Zero migration, zero new persistence.
  - **The guest can still edit everything** (the host's explicit choice). Dates, guests and homestay are seeds, not a contract — the price is recomputed by `PricingEngine` and availability re-checked by `AvailabilityService` when they submit, exactly as for a walk-up booking. So the link can't be used to lock in a stale price.
  - **`TenantHomeController::prefill()`** parses the params and **drops anything unusable rather than 404'ing** — a stale link must still open a working booking page. Rejects a property that isn't this tenant's active one, a check-in in the past, a check-out on/before check-in (keeping the check-in), guests outside 1–20, and a `pay` that isn't `manual|gateway`. Dates are parsed **strictly** (`preg_match` + a `format() === $value` round-trip) so `2026-13-45` is rejected instead of Carbon silently rolling it to 2027-01-14. `marketplace.show` renders the same view, so the Blade reads `$prefill ?? null`.
  - **Client side**: a new Alpine `init()` on `wafa()` applies the seed. Order is load-bearing — `selectProperty()` resets the guest count to the new property's default, so the property is applied *before* the host's number. A quoted range whose nights have since sold is **dropped** (`rangeHasBookedNight()`, half-open `[ci, co)`), the calendar opens on the quoted month, `payMethod` honours `pay=manual` (falling back to manual if the tenant has since dropped their gateway), the booking form opens and scrolls into view.
  - **Generator page** (`BookingController::sendForm()` + `tenant/bookings/send-form.blade.php`): homestay picker, dates, guests, an optional guest WhatsApp number, and an **"Ask the guest to pay manually"** checkbox (on by default; the copy adapts when the tenant has no gateway at all). Builds the link live, with **Copy**, **Preview form**, and a **Send on WhatsApp** deeplink carrying a BM/EN message with the homestay, dates, nights and estimated total. It ships each property's booked nights so it **warns the host before they quote a range that's already sold** — matching submit-time semantics (it counts `pending` too, which is what `AvailabilityService` rejects on).
  - **⚠️ Behaviour worth knowing** (pre-existing, surfaced by this feature): a manual booking is created `pending` with **no Payment row**, and `PublicHomeBuilder` only greys out a date once the **booking fee is paid** (the 2026-06-05 rule). So the nights a manual guest just booked **still look available on the public calendar** until the host hits "Mark booking fee paid". They are *not* double-bookable — `AvailabilityService` counts `pending`, so a second guest is rejected at submit — but the calendar is misleading in the gap. Also, `ProcessPaymentLifecycle` never auto-cancels these (`fee_autocancel` is armed only by the guest online pay-now flow), so an abandoned manual booking holds its dates until the host cancels it.
  - **Verified: 38 assertions, zero failures**, driving the dashboard, the public page and a real booking POST through the **actual HTTP kernel** against a throwaway seeded DB inside a rolled-back transaction. Covers: the generator page renders and the bookings list links to it; a prefilled link seeds property/dates/guests/`pay=manual` into Alpine; no params → `prefill: null`; each junk param (bogus property, past date, `2026-13-45`, backwards check-out, `guests=999`, `pay=crypto`) is dropped while the page still renders; a guest submits the prefilled form and gets a `pending` booking with the quoted dates, the right nights, their name, **no gateway Payment row** and no `fee_autocancel`; the unpaid booking does **not** grey the calendar but a **second guest is rejected**; marking the fee paid *does* grey it; and the generator ships the booked nights so it can warn. Three initial failures were **harness artifacts, not code**: Blade's `@js()` escapes `"` to `"` (so naive `"key":val` assertions never match), the POST needs `APP_ENV=testing` to bypass CSRF, and a regex over the escaped HTML matched an empty `booked:[]` — the grey-out assertions were rewritten to call `PublicHomeBuilder` directly rather than scrape the page.
  - Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Public/TenantHomeController.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php` (+`sendForm`), new `resources/views/tenant/bookings/send-form.blade.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php` (Alpine `init()` + `prefill`), `resources/views/tenant/bookings/index.blade.php` (entry button). The route was committed ahead of the code in `c0d712e`, so `main` briefly carried a `bookings.send-form` route pointing at a method that didn't exist. **No migration, no asset rebuild.** Deploy = push + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-07-10** — **First-run setup checklist for new tenants + the tour's "replay from Settings" promise is finally real.** Shipped `4a37e7f`, deployed.
  - **What already existed** (and was *not* in this log until now): an 8-step anchored walkthrough modal, `resources/views/partials/onboarding-tour.blade.php` + `OnboardingController@complete`, added **2026-06-02 in `4fbef31`** and spotlight-anchored in `d3f0198`. BM+EN copy, renders from `layouts/app.blade.php` whenever `users.tour_completed_at IS NULL`, anchors to `[data-tour]` on each sidebar nav item (rendered dynamically from a `tour` key on the nav array — a literal grep for `data-tour="dashboard"` finds nothing and looks broken; it isn't).
  - **It toured the UI; it never told a host what had to be TRUE before they could take money.** New `App\Services\Onboarding\SetupChecklist` answers that with six steps, **all derived from live state** (nothing stored), so a step can't be ticked while the underlying thing is broken, and undoing the work un-ticks it: `property` (a Property exists) · `room` (a Room with `base_price > 0` — an **unpriced room doesn't count**, it can't be quoted) · `publish` (a Property is `active` — **a draft is invisible on the booking page**, the #1 "my link shows nothing" cause) · `payment` (a gateway resolves via `CreateGatewayBill::resolveProvider`, **or** `hasBankDetails()` / `manualPaymentInstructions()`) · `whatsapp` (session connected — **blunt on purpose: guest email is dead while SES is in sandbox, so no WhatsApp = guests receive nothing at all**) · `booking` (ticks itself on the first real booking — the only honest proof the public link works).
  - Rendered by `partials/setup-checklist.blade.php`, included from the Dashboard **above the stat cards** (which all read RM 0.00 for a new tenant), and it **removes itself entirely once all six pass**. That makes it a config diagnostic, not just a welcome mat.
  - **The broken promise**: the tour's final step said, in both languages, *"You can always replay this tour from Settings."* `tour_completed_at` was **write-once** — `complete()` was the only code that touched it, nothing ever cleared it, and Settings had no tour control (the only "tour" match there was "Tourism Tax"). New `OnboardingController@replay` + `POST /dashboard/onboarding/replay` nulls the flag; a **"Getting started" card in Settings** and a link in the checklist both hit it. **Per-user, not per-tenant** — a co-owner shouldn't have the tour forced back on them. The Settings card is load-bearing: once a tenant is 6/6 the checklist card is gone, so it's the *only* replay entry point (verified — prod `/dashboard` renders `replay-control:no` for Wafa, `/dashboard/settings` renders `yes`).
  - **Verified** against a throwaway tenant in a rolled-back transaction, driving the real service: `0/6` fresh → each step ticking **only** when genuinely satisfied (an `RM0` room stays unticked; pricing it flips it) → `6/6` hides the card → **un-publishing the property re-opens it** → no cross-tenant leak (an empty tenant reads 0/6 while the seeded one reads 3/6) → `replay()` nulls the flag so the tour renders again. On prod: **Wafa is 6/6 → card correctly hidden**; a rolled-back fresh tenant reads **0/6 → card shown**; `/dashboard` + `/dashboard/settings` both 200.

Their hunks were parked as patches, my changes committed alone (7 files, 312 insertions, zero foreign hunks), then their patches re-applied `--3way`. **Check `git diff --cached` before committing in this repo — several sessions edit it at once.**
