- **2026-07-10** — **Fix: a failed gateway payment left the guest on an endless "Confirming your payment…" page.** Reported against SecurePay: the gateway emails the guest that payment was unsuccessful, but Tempahlah's return page keeps loading forever. Three bugs, all on the money path.
  - **(1) The failure state was unreachable on two of three gateways.** `BillplzWebhookController` and `SecurePayWebhookController` both did `$newStatus = $paidConfirmed ? SUCCEEDED : PROCESSING` — a **declined** payment and one that simply **hasn't happened yet** were recorded identically. Nothing ever wrote `STATUS_FAILED` (only Toyyibpay did, via `3 => STATUS_FAILED`). `PaymentReturnController::reconcile()` then returned a plain `bool` — paid / not-paid — with no way to say "the gateway told us this failed", so `return.blade.php` fell into its `$pending` branch, which emitted `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="6">` **with no attempt limit**. The guest re-rendered "Confirming your payment…" every 6 seconds indefinitely. The "unsuccessful payment" email is the **gateway's own** — we have no failed-payment mailable — so the app never knew.
  - **(2) An unsigned Toyyibpay callback could settle a payment.** The `signatureStatus === 'missing'` branch (DuitNow QR, which carries no hash) fetched `getBillTransactions`, **logged it, and discarded it** — then decided on `$payload['status']`. Anyone who knew a billcode could POST `status=1` with no hash and flip the payment to `succeeded` + confirm the booking. It now **decides on the server-side answer**, which is what its own comment always claimed. Same block: `'paid_at' => $paid ? now() : null` **wiped `paid_at`** off an already-succeeded payment when a late non-success callback arrived (the Billplz/SecurePay twins used `: $payment->paid_at`); aligned.
  - **(3) Toyyibpay's `STATUS_FAILED` minted a second live bill.** `CreateGatewayBill`'s reuse guard looks for a `processing` payment; a `failed` one misses it, so a retry created a **new bill while the old one stayed payable** at Toyyibpay — two live links for one booking, both chargeable.
  - **Model**: at all three gateways the bill/session **stays payable after a decline** (Billplz leaves it `state: due`, Toyyibpay's billcode still works, SecurePay's session reopens). So a failed *attempt* must not close the *payment*. New `AttemptOutcome` enum (`Paid` / `Failed` / `Unknown`, `app/Services/Payments/`) is read out of each gateway's payload by a client method that sits next to that gateway's other protocol knowledge — `attemptOutcome()` on all three, plus `billOutcome()` (Billplz) and `transactionsOutcome()` (Toyyibpay) for server-side answers. `Payment::markAttemptFailed()` writes `meta.last_attempt` and **leaves status `processing`**, so the reuse guard, the fee-chase and auto-cancel all keep working; `attemptFailed()` also reads legacy `status = failed` rows so nothing on prod regresses.
  - **`Unknown` is the safe default — `Failed` is only ever returned on a positive failure signal.** This matters because the two are *not* distinguishable server-side on two gateways: a declined FPX transaction leaves a Billplz bill `due` and a SecurePay order `payment_status: false`, exactly like a bill nobody has opened. So Billplz's decline arrives via the callback's `transaction_status: failed`, SecurePay's via `payment_status: false` on a **checksum-verified** callback or redirect POST (`fpx_debit_auth_code: 99` = *pending approval*, deliberately **not** a failure — it's the B2B1 99→00 transition), and only Toyyibpay can report a decline server-side (`billpaymentStatus: 3`).
  - **Return page** rewritten: `reconcile()` → tri-state `resolveOutcome()`. Precedence is load-bearing — a **paid claim from the browser can't settle a payment** (forgeable, and even signed it can outrun the gateway's records) but it **must suppress a stale failure**, otherwise a guest who fails once, retries and succeeds gets told their payment failed while it settles. SecurePay's checksum-verified redirect POST is read so a decline shows *before* its webhook lands; Toyyibpay/Billplz redirects are unsigned or differently-signed, so theirs come from the server check or the webhook. Polling is now bounded (10 × 6s): a payment that stays `Unknown` lands on a **"Still waiting on your bank"** page that stops refreshing, warns **"do not pay twice"**, and offers Try again + Message the host — instead of spinning forever. Failure state gets a **Try payment again** button pointing at the stored `meta['payment_url']` (the *same* bill), plus the host's WhatsApp.
  - **Also**: `ProcessPaymentLifecycle::pendingUnpaidOnline()` whitelisted `['toyyibpay','billplz']` — **`securepay` was missing**, so abandoned/failed SecurePay bookings were never fee-chased or auto-cancelled and **held their dates forever**. Now that SecurePay is the primary live gateway, that was live. Added.
  - **Verified: 64 assertions, zero failures**, driving the real webhooks + return page through the **actual HTTP kernel** against a throwaway seeded DB inside a rolled-back transaction (0 residual rows). Covers, per gateway: a verified decline → payment stays `processing`, failure recorded, booking **not** confirmed, return page shows the failure with the same-bill retry link and **no** refresh tag; Billplz "unpaid but untried" → still pending (not a false failure); SecurePay `99` → not a failure; **forged unsigned Toyyibpay `status=1` does not settle** and the server's `3` is recorded instead; retry-succeeds → return page settles, booking confirms, stale failure suppressed; **signed redirect claiming paid while the gateway says not-yet → pending, never the stale failure**; unsigned forged paid POST → ignored, no 419/500; `poll=10` → stalled state, no refresh; the **reuse guard still returns the same bill** after a failure (exactly 1 payment row); securepay now selected by the lifecycle command. Plus a full happy-path regression: a successful payment still settles + confirms on **all three** gateways, the Toyyibpay DuitNow (unsigned + server-says-paid) path still settles, and a late pending callback no longer wipes `paid_at`. Two initial failures were **test artifacts, not code**: `Http::fake()` merges stubs and the first registered match wins (a stale `payment_status: false` shadowed a later `true`), and `CreateSecurePayBill::execute()` takes 3 args.
  - Files: new `app/Services/Payments/AttemptOutcome.php`; `app/Models/Payment.php`; `app/Http/Controllers/PaymentReturnController.php`; `app/Http/Controllers/Webhooks/{Toyyibpay,Billplz,SecurePay}WebhookController.php`; `app/Services/Payments/{Toyyibpay/ToyyibpayClient,Billplz/BillplzClient,SecurePay/SecurePayClient}.php`; `app/Console/Commands/ProcessPaymentLifecycle.php`; `resources/views/payments/return.blade.php`. **No migration** (`payments.meta` is an existing JSON column), no asset rebuild. **Deploy**: push to `main` (auto-deploy) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-07-10** — **Manual payment is now ALWAYS an option on the public booking page (the per-tenant toggle is removed), and the invoice email finally prints the host's bank details.** Reported as "customers can't pick manual payment on the booking link."
  - **Root cause was a setting, not a bug in the flow.** `public-tenant/home.blade.php` only rendered the "Pay online / Pay manually" chooser when `$toyyibpayConfigured && $manualPaymentEnabled`, and prod had `tenants.manual_payment_enabled = 0` for Wafa — set by a **direct DB write on 2026-07-07** when the ask was the opposite ("make it gateway-only so the booking fee auto-marks as paid"). The host never unticked it in Settings, so from their side the option had silently vanished.
  - **Fix (per the host's explicit choice: force it on platform-wide, not just flip their row).** Manual pay is now unconditional: the chooser renders whenever a tenant *also* has an online gateway, and with no gateway `payMethod` stays pinned to `manual`. Removed `Tenant::manualPaymentEnabled()`, `MANUAL_PAYMENT_ENABLED_DEFAULT`, the `manual_payment_enabled` fillable/cast, the Settings checkbox, and its `SettingsController` validation + `$request->boolean()` write. **The DB column is deliberately left in place but is now read by nothing** — so no data migration is needed and Wafa's `0` is simply inert. The Settings card keeps the free-text **instructions** textarea and now says the option is always on.
  - **Two dead paths fell out.** The public page's WhatsApp-only "Reserve on WhatsApp" fallback (shown when a tenant had neither gateway nor manual) and `PublicBookingController`'s `method === 'none'` → `whatsappFallbackUrl()` redirect are both **unreachable** once manual always exists, and were removed. Net effect: a free-tier tenant with no gateway now gets a **real booking form that records the booking**, instead of bouncing the guest into WhatsApp with nothing persisted. (`whatsappFallbackUrl()` itself stays — it's still the catch for a gateway bill that fails to mint.)
  - **Second, real defect fixed at the same time**: the manual-payment panel in `emails/bookings/invoice.blade.php` + `received.blade.php` read **only** `manual_payment_instructions`. Wafa has that blank but *does* have bank details saved, so the email told guests **"Please contact the host to arrange your payment"** while the booking-sent page, the WhatsApp message (`MessageTemplates::manualPayHow()`) and the invoice PDF all correctly showed the Maybank account. Turning manual back on without this would have shipped a dead end. New shared partial **`emails/partials/how-to-pay.blade.php`** renders bank name / account holder / account number as a markdown list, appends the free-text instructions when set, quotes the booking reference, and falls back to "contact the host" **only when both are genuinely empty**. (⚠️ Per the SES-sandbox entry below, **no guest actually receives these emails yet** — WhatsApp is the only channel that lands, and it was already correct. The email fix matters the day SES leaves sandbox.)
  - **Verified** end-to-end against a throwaway SQLite DB through the real HTTP kernel — **29 assertions, zero failures**: free tenant with no gateway renders the booking form (not the wa.me button) with `payMethod` pinned manual and no chooser; a guest POSTing `payment_method=gateway` at a tenant with no gateway **falls back to manual** (booking created `pending`, **no Payment row**, `fee_autocancel` not armed) instead of being redirected away; a paid tenant with Billplz shows **both** options; picking manual while a live gateway exists still mints no bill; the invoice email now carries `Maybank` / holder / account no. and no longer says "contact the host"; and a tenant with neither bank details nor instructions still gets the honest fallback. Plus the Settings page renders 200, the checkbox is gone, the textarea persists, and a save with the removed key no longer 500s. Blade compiled **and the compiled PHP linted** (`view:cache` alone doesn't lint — see the 2026-07-04 gotcha). Three "failures" during the run were harness artifacts, not code: `.wf-paymethod-opt` also appears in the page's `<style>` block (so it's a useless marker), the success route is `/book/sent/{ref}` not `/booking/`, and the app locale defaults to **BM** so the English copy never rendered.
  - **Trade-off the host accepted**: a guest who picks manual creates a **pending** booking that does **not** auto-confirm — the host must "Mark paid" in the dashboard, which then sends the receipt. Manual bookings are never auto-cancelled by `bookings:process-payment-lifecycle` (that only targets bookings carrying `meta.fee_autocancel`).
  - Files: `app/Models/Tenant.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/SettingsController.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`, `app/Services/Public/PublicHomeBuilder.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`, `resources/views/tenant/settings/index.blade.php`, `resources/views/emails/bookings/{invoice,received}.blade.php`, new `resources/views/emails/partials/how-to-pay.blade.php`. **No migration, no asset rebuild, no data op.** Deploy = push + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-07-10** — **Fix: an SES rejection killed the WhatsApp booking confirmation; SecurePay payments had no method label.** Found while confirming the SecurePay post-payment flow end-to-end. Shipped `30a059a`.
  - **⚠️ The big finding is NOT the code — prod AWS SES is still in SANDBOX MODE.** It refuses every address that isn't individually verified: `81 × MessageRejected`, **21 distinct guest addresses** refused with `Email address is not verified. The following identities failed the check in region AP-SOUTHEAST-1: …`. **No guest has ever received an email from Tempahlah** — not an invoice, not a receipt, not a reminder. `MAIL_MAILER=ses`, region `ap-southeast-1`, from `noreply@tempahlah.com`. **Getting out of the SES sandbox is an AWS support request with a lead time — start it now.** Until then WhatsApp is the *only* channel that actually reaches guests.
  - **Bug 1 — the rejection cascaded.** `SendBookingConfirmation` sent its email with `Mail::to()->send()` **inline and uncaught**, so the SES exception aborted the job *before* `WhatsappMessenger::dispatchConfirmation()` on the next line. `SendBookingReceipt` / `SendBookingInvoice` / `SendBookingCancellation` / `SendBookingInstructions` all already wrap `Mail` in `try/catch`, which is why guests still got the **invoice** and **receipt** on WhatsApp but never the **confirmation**. Visible in the data: every settled booking has `whatsapp: invoice:sent | receipt:sent` and **no `confirmation` row**, plus **13 dead-lettered `App\Jobs\SendBookingConfirmation`** in `failed_jobs`. Both arms are now isolated.
    - **`SendCheckInInstructions` + `SendPaymentReminder` were deliberately left alone**: they use `Mail::…->queue()`, so the mailable fails as its *own* job (hence they dead-letter as `App\Mail\CheckInInstructionsMail` / `App\Mail\PaymentReminderMail`, 4 + 3) and their WhatsApp arm already survives. Don't "fix" them by wrapping — nothing is broken there.
    - **Verified with a negative control**: a Symfony transport that throws SES's exact `MessageRejected`, driving the real job against a throwaway booking in a rolled-back transaction. **Old code**: `job THREW … / WhatsApp arm reached: NO`. **New code**: `job survived: yes / WhatsApp arm reached: yes`. The old code genuinely fails the test, so the test proves the fix.
  - **Bug 2 — SecurePay payments were unlabelled.** `MessageTemplates::paymentMethodLabel()` had no `METHOD_SECUREPAY` case → fell to `default => ''`, so a SecurePay receipt read `💳 Dibayar: RM 100.00` with **no method**; the invoice PDF's `$methodLabels` map had no `securepay` key → `ucfirst()` rendered **"Securepay"**. Both are on the live path now that SecurePay is Wafa's primary gateway. Fixed both; verified on prod against a real receipt: `💳 Paid: RM 100.00 via SecurePay`.
  - **Confirmed correct (no change needed)**: a settled gateway payment stamps `deposit_paid_at`, flips `pending → confirmed` **only if it was pending** (so a late/duplicate callback can't rewind a checked-out stay), and `Booking::paymentStatusKey()` then renders **"Paid Booking Fee"**. Live evidence: `BK-260623-1V3D2 → status=confirmed → label: Paid Booking Fee`, `docs: invoice(WAF-INV-26-0010), receipt(WAF-RCP-26-0006)`, `whatsapp: invoice:sent | receipt:sent`. **Caveat**: a booking made **within `full_payment_days_before` (7) days** of check-in is charged `TYPE_FULL`, which also stamps `balance_paid_at` → it reads **"Paid Full Payment"**, not "Paid Booking Fee". By design.
  - **Did NOT retry the 13 dead-lettered confirmations** — replaying them would WhatsApp guests about bookings from weeks ago. Leave them.
  - **Deploy gotcha**: this touched a Blade (`pdf/invoice.blade.php`) **and** a queued job class. Long-running queue workers cache PHP classes, so the deploy needed `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` + **`php artisan queue:restart`** — without the last one the workers keep running the old `SendBookingConfirmation` until `--max-time=3600` recycles them. Files: `app/Jobs/SendBookingConfirmation.php`, `app/Services/WhatsApp/MessageTemplates.php`, `resources/views/pdf/invoice.blade.php`.
- **2026-07-10** — **Two fixes found by driving the app as 10 tenant personas (261 assertions): new homestays were invisible to guests, and online bookings never charged tourism tax.**
  - **(1) A new property was created as a `draft`, and a draft is invisible.** `PropertyController::store` set `Property::STATUS_DRAFT`, but `TenantHomeController` lists only `STATUS_ACTIVE` properties and `StoreBookingRequest` rejects anything else. So a host created their homestay, shared `{slug}.tempahlah.com`, and **their booking page rendered empty**; any guest who reached the form was told *"Selected property is not available."* — which reads like the dates are taken. There is **no status field on the create form**, so no host ever chose draft. New properties are now created **`STATUS_ACTIVE`**; the status selector on the edit page still lets them archive or unpublish. **Marketplace behaviour deliberately unchanged**: `store()` called `autoListMarketplace($property)`, which was **dead code** (it early-returns on anything but active). With the property now live that call would have published a homestay to tempahlah.com before the host added a single photo — and `PublishListing` has **no paid-tier gate**, only an active check. So the call was removed from `store()`; listing still happens on the first save from the edit page, exactly where it did before (that's where the host used to flip the property to active).
  - **(2) Tourism tax (RM 10/night, foreign guests only) was never charged on an online booking.** `PublicBookingController` hardcoded `'guest_country' => 'MY', 'is_foreigner' => false`. The tax logic in `CreateBooking` was correct all along — it simply never received a `true`. A host typing a booking in by hand and ticking "foreigner" charged RM 20 on 2 nights; the identical booking made by the guest on the public page charged **RM 0**. Any Langkawi/Penang/Melaka operator taking online bookings silently under-collected a statutory tax. **Fix**: the public booking form now asks **Warganegara / Nationality** (a select reusing the dashboard form's 10-country list, `OT` = other, defaulting to Malaysia, with an inline RM-10/night hint when non-Malaysian). `StoreBookingRequest` gains `COUNTRY_LABELS`/`COUNTRIES` + `guestCountry()` + `guestIsForeigner()`, validated with `Rule::in` so a junk code is rejected rather than stored. Both `guest_country` and `is_foreigner` now derive from **the one answer**, so they can't contradict each other (the dashboard form still has a separate country select *and* a foreigner checkbox, which can). A missing field (an old cached form) defaults to Malaysian — never over-charges.
  - **Verified** end-to-end against a throwaway DB through the real HTTP kernel: property created `active`, **not** auto-listed, public page shows the homestay, nationality field renders, and a guest books immediately (previously impossible). Tourism tax: MY → RM 0, SG/GB/OT → RM 20 on 2 nights, each with `country` stored correctly and `is_foreigner` matching; field-absent → RM 0; bogus `ZZ` → rejected by validation. Tax lands in `total_amount`, and the free tier still mints no invoice. (One composite-run "failure" turned out to be the `booking-create-public` limiter doing its job — 5/min/IP, and the harness fired 6.)
  - Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/PropertyController.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`, `app/Http/Requests/Public/StoreBookingRequest.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php` (+ `select` added to the `.wf-book-form` input styling, kept at 16px so iOS Safari doesn't zoom on tap). PHP + one Blade; deploy = push + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`. No migration, no asset rebuild. **Existing `draft` properties are unaffected** — on prod that's only Wafa's soft-deleted property 2.
  - **Still open from the same sweep** (not fixed here): free-tier caps (1 property / 3 rooms / 20 bookings-per-month / staff) are **advertised but enforced nowhere** — the property guard lives in the never-rendered `⚡property-form.blade.php` while the real form posts to `PropertyController::store`; **no staff invite exists at all** (`TenantUser` is created once, for the owner) though Pro sells "5 staff accounts"; **no web tenant switcher** (the API's `switchTenant` is a no-op stub); **phone-only repeat guests duplicate `User` rows** (`resolveGuest` matches on email only); a **whole-house property holding >1 room can be sold twice** (availability is per-room — latent: no room-create route, but `update()` still accepts a `pricing_mode` change, and prod's soft-deleted property 2 is exactly this shape); and **no iCal import** exists for Airbnb/Booking.com despite the schema + flags (a live double-booking risk for cross-listing hosts). Also `AgentUsageDaily::todayFor()` 500s on the second call per day **under SQLite only** (the `date` cast writes `Y-m-d H:i:s`, the lookup searches `Y-m-d`); MySQL coerces it on a DATE column, so prod is unaffected — local dev is not.
- **2026-07-10** — **Fix: unticking "Use sandbox" never left sandbox mode — on ANY of the three gateways. SecurePay is now live on production for Wafa.** Reported as SecurePay's Test connection returning `{"error":"Unauthorized. Invalid or expired token."}` after entering real credentials.
  - **Root cause was NOT SecurePay and NOT the request shape.** `SecurePayClient::testConnection()` reproduces the documented curl in `docs.securepay.my/api/validate` byte-for-byte (POST form `checksum_token`, Basic auth `uid:auth_token`), and that error string is SecurePay's **own documented rejection** for that endpoint. The credentials were *production* credentials being sent to `sandbox.securepay.my`.
  - **Why**: an unchecked HTML checkbox posts **no value at all**, so `'is_sandbox' => 'sometimes|boolean'` dropped the key from `$request->validate()`'s return. `IntegrationController::update()` does `$integration->config = $validated`, so the key **vanished from config** rather than being stored as `false` — and all three clients read `$config['is_sandbox'] ?? true`. Unticking the box was a **silent no-op**. Prod proved it: the securepay row's config keys were `uid,auth_token,checksum_token,is_primary` with `is_sandbox` **absent**, and `SecurePayClient::forTenant(1)->baseUrl()` returned `https://sandbox.securepay.my`.
  - **Scope**: `BillplzClient` (line 65) and `ToyyibpayClient` (line 74) carry the identical `?? true` fallback, so **no tenant on any gateway had ever been able to leave sandbox mode through the UI**. The standing CLAUDE.md note telling hosts to "untick Use sandbox before taking real money" was never actionable. `is_primary` was unaffected (its fallback is `?? false`, which matches unticked).
  - **Live impact found while diagnosing**: the host had ticked "Use SecurePay as my main gateway" and disabled Billplz, so `resolveProvider(1)` returned `'securepay'` → a sandbox 401 on every real booking. `PublicBookingController` catches `PaymentGatewayException` and redirects the guest **away to a WhatsApp deeplink**, so bookings were still created but **nobody could pay online**. That was live.
  - **Fix** (`IntegrationController::update()`, one loop): after validation, every field the provider catalog declares as `type => 'checkbox'` is written explicitly via `$request->boolean($key)`. Catalog-driven, so it fixes SecurePay + Billplz + Toyyibpay together and can't drift as fields are added. **No view change** — deliberately fixed in the controller rather than by adding a hidden `value="0"` input, so the deploy is PHP-only (no `view:cache`).
  - **Verified** by driving the real `update()` against the dev DB inside a rolled-back transaction: ticked → `is_sandbox=true` → `sandbox.securepay.my`; unticked → `is_sandbox=false` → `securepay.my`; `is_primary` round-trips true/false both ways. Then **live on prod**: flipped tenant 1's `is_sandbox` to `false` and ran the real `testConnection()` against `https://securepay.my` → **HTTP 201 `{"credential":true,"api_name":"Default","merchant_name":"Tempahlah Enterprise"}`**. This closes the last unverified segment from the 2026-07-09 note — **SecurePay's own HTTP response is now confirmed against a real merchant account**, and all three credentials (UID / auth token / checksum token) are valid. `resolveProvider(1)` = `securepay`, `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com` + `tempahlah.com` both 200.
  - **Nothing was wrong on the SecurePay dashboard side.** The Interfaces → Default page's blank Callback/Redirect/Cancel/Timeout URLs are **correct to leave blank** — `CreateSecurePayBill` passes `callback_url` (`https://tempahlah.com/api/webhooks/securepay`) and `redirect_url` (`payments/return/{payment}`) per payment, so the interface-level defaults are never read. FPX B2C alone is right; B2B1 is safe to enable later (the webhook's idempotency key already handles its `99 → 00` transition). API credentials come from **Apps**, not Interfaces.
  - **Still not exercised**: a real SecurePay bill (`POST /api/apis/payments`) has never returned a live `payment_url`, and no real checksum has been verified — those need one genuine RM1 booking through the public page. SecurePay is **primary and live** right now, so the next real guest booking is that test.
  - Commit `b1c52ed`, pushed to `main` (auto-deploy). File: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/IntegrationController.php`. PHP-only; deploy = push + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-07-10** — **Fix: calendar "Nights booked" showed `6.9999999999884`, and every month-crossing stay was over-counted by one night.** Reported on `/dashboard/calendar?property_id=3&cursor=2026-04`. The float was the symptom; the real defect was the boundary. `CalendarController` clamped each booking's overlap against `$monthEnd->copy()->addDay()` — but `endOfMonth()` lands on `23:59:59.999999`, so that bound was **the 1st of the next month at 23:59:59.999999, a full day too late**. A stay crossing month-end therefore had its first night of the *next* month counted into this one, and `diffInDays()` (a **float** in Carbon 3, an int in Carbon 2) surfaced the leftover microsecond as `…9884`. Carbon 2 would have truncated it to a tidy-looking integer and hidden the over-count entirely. Real April 2026 data: `BK-260430-APDWG` (30 Apr → 2 May) contributed `1.9999999999884` nights to April instead of **1**, pushing April occupancy from the true **20%** to **23%** and over-allocating that booking's revenue into April (`overlap / nights` ≈ 1.0 instead of 0.5). **Fix**: clamp against `$monthStart->copy()->addMonthNoOverflow()` (the 1st of next month at 00:00), matching the half-open `[check_in, check_out)` rule `AvailabilityService` already uses, then `startOfDay()` both ends and cast the diff to `int`. Verified against the live April data (total `6.9999999999884` → **6**, occupancy 23% → 20%) and 8 boundary cases incl. the month-crossing stay seen from *both* months (nights conserve: 1 + 1 = the booking's 2), whole month, 28-day Feb, leap Feb, and a year-end crossing. **Not** a bug on Reports/Dashboard: their long decimals (`width: 94.029713585541%`) are CSS bar widths, not displayed text — the labels correctly read `94%`. File: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/CalendarController.php`. PHP-only; deploy = push + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-07-10** — **Phase 2: platform subscription billing — Tempahlah can now actually charge RM 49/mo.** Ships **switched off**: with no `BILLPLZ_API_KEY` in `.env` (prod has none), checkout is hidden and `subscriptions:bill-cycle` no-ops, so the deploy changes nothing until Tempahlah's own Billplz account is configured.
  - **Direction of money matters.** A tenant's own gateway (Toyyibpay / Billplz / SecurePay, credentials encrypted per tenant in `tenant_integrations`) charges their *guests*. This bills the *tenant* into **Tempahlah's own** Billplz account, credentials from `config('homestay.platform_billing.billplz')`. Deliberately separate classes — a bug that crossed the two would pay a guest's booking into the platform account, or bill a tenant into their own.
  - **`subscription_invoices`** (migration `2026_07_09_140000`): one row per cycle — `number` (`TPL-SUB-26-00001`, doubles as the gateway's `reference_1`), status `pending|paid|failed|void`, amount, `period_start`/`period_end`, `due_at`, `gateway_bill_id`, `payment_url`, `reminders_sent`/`last_reminder_at`. Unique `(subscription_id, period_start)` is the real guard against double-minting under concurrency. Model is **not** `BelongsToTenant` — the webhook, return page and command all run without tenant context.
  - **`PlatformBillplz`** — config-driven twin of `BillplzClient::forTenant()`. Only bill *creation* is reimplemented (the tenant one is shaped around a `Booking`); `getBill`, `isPaid` and the static `verifySignature` are reused verbatim. `configured()` is the master switch.
  - **`SubscriptionBillingService`** owns every state transition so checkout, webhook, return page and the daily command can't drift: `issueInvoice()` (get-or-create per cycle, refuses comped), `payUrlFor()` (mint-or-reuse the bill), `settle()` (idempotent, row-locked — the webhook and return page routinely race), `reconcile()` (ask Billplz server-side), `voidOpenInvoices()`, `nextPeriodStart()` (never bills for a month that already elapsed).
  - **Routes**: `POST /dashboard/subscription/checkout` → Billplz; `GET /subscription/billing/return` (public, any host — resolves the invoice from the bill id and **never trusts the redirect's `paid` flag**, it re-asks Billplz); `POST /api/webhooks/subscription-billing` (`throttle:webhook-subscription`, X-Signature verified against the platform key, idempotent via `webhook_events` with a `sub:` prefix so a platform bill id can never collide with a tenant's booking bill id). An unverifiable signature falls back to a server-side `getBill()` rather than trusting the body.
  - **`subscriptions:bill-cycle`** (daily 02:00, **before** `process-lifecycle` at 02:15, `--dry-run`): issues + emails the next bill `issue_lead_days` (3) before a trial or period ends; sends at most one dunning email a day while past_due inside grace; voids open invoices for anyone back on free. `process-lifecycle`'s downgrade now voids open invoices too, so nobody is chased for a cycle they no longer hold. New `SubscriptionInvoiceMail` (+ dunning variant naming the grace deadline).
  - **Subscription page**: the "Free trial already used" dead-end becomes a real **Upgrade to Pro — RM 49.00/mo** checkout when billing is configured; a past-due tenant sees a grace-countdown banner with **Pay now**; an open invoice surfaces its pay link. Comped accounts can't check out.
  - **Config**: new `homestay.platform_billing` block (api_key / collection_id / x_signature_key / sandbox, `issue_lead_days`, `invoice_due_days`). Removed the **orphaned `homestay.channels`** block — it held platform Toyyibpay/Billplz creds that **nothing in `app/` ever read** (verified) and was the source of the "billing looks half-built" confusion. `.env.example` rewritten to say plainly that `BILLPLZ_*` are the *platform's* keys, not a tenant's.
  - **Verified** against throwaway SQLite DBs with Billplz faked: **67 assertions, zero failures** (46 service/command/webhook + 21 HTTP). Covers: issue → mint bill → signed callback → invoice paid → period advanced → `ai_agent` active again; replay is idempotent; a **forged X-Signature is rejected** (200, not 401, so Billplz doesn't retry-storm) and settles nothing; an **unsigned callback claiming `paid=true` is not trusted** (server says due → noop) but **does** settle once Billplz itself says paid; `payUrlFor` reuses the bill (asserted via `preventStrayRequests`, so a second mint would throw); comped accounts refuse to be billed; dry-run writes nothing; dunning fires once per day; downgrade voids the open invoice. Two failures during the run were **test artifacts, not code**: `Http::fake()` accumulates stubs and the first registered match wins, so an earlier catch-all silently shadowed later `getBill` stubs; and a re-run against a dirty DB replayed already-processed webhook events.
  - **Not yet possible**: true auto-charge. Billplz has **no** recurring/subscription/mandate endpoint — recurring must be built on their **Tokenization** product, which is **off by default** (paid plan; email `support@billplz.com` for access), **Visa/Mastercard only**, and **cannot tokenize FPX** — the rail most Malaysian hosts want. So the monthly pay-link cycle built here is the foundation, not a stopgap; card auto-charge layers on top later. **Request tokenization access now** — it has a lead time.
  - **To switch billing on**: put Tempahlah's own `BILLPLZ_API_KEY` / `BILLPLZ_COLLECTION_ID` / `BILLPLZ_SIGNATURE` (+ `BILLPLZ_SANDBOX=false` when live) into prod `.env`, then reload php-fpm. **Do not run `config:cache`** (standing note — `WhatsAppService` still calls `env()`). Verify with `php artisan subscriptions:bill-cycle --dry-run`.
- **2026-07-09** — **Fix: two payment-settlement bugs affecting ALL THREE gateways (Toyyibpay, Billplz, SecurePay).** Both surfaced while end-to-end testing SecurePay; neither was introduced by it.
  - **(1) A late or duplicate gateway callback rewound a booking's status.** `SettlePaymentSuccess` wrote `'status' => Booking::STATUS_CONFIRMED` **unconditionally** on any succeeded `deposit`/`full` payment. So a callback arriving on an already-`checked_out` stay silently rewound it to `confirmed`; on a **`cancelled`** booking it **resurrected** it — even though `CancelBooking` had already freed the dates, so the calendar could then double-book. Reachable without malice: all three gateways retry callbacks, and `PaymentReturnController` *also* reconciles + settles whenever the guest re-opens the return URL. **Fix**: `status` is now only written when `$wasPending` (the same guard the confirmation/receipt/GCal/housekeeping side-effects already used, so the normal `pending → confirmed` path is unchanged). Paid dates (`deposit_paid_at`/`balance_paid_at`) are still stamped in every case — money really did arrive — and a new `Log::warning` fires when a payment settles against a `cancelled`/`no_show` booking, because the host probably owes a refund and that must never be swallowed silently.
  - **(2) A retried *rejected* callback 500'd on a unique constraint.** `payment_transactions` is `UNIQUE(provider, external_id)`. The rejected-callback branches in all three webhook controllers (bad signature/checksum, missing tenant creds) `return` early **without** stamping `webhook_events.processed_at`, so the controller's replay guard doesn't catch a retry of the same delivery — and every gateway retries. The audit insert then hit the constraint and threw. **Fix**: `recordWebhook()` in `ToyyibpayLog`, `BillplzLog` and `SecurePayLog` now uses `PaymentTransaction::withoutGlobalScopes()->firstOrCreate([provider, external_id], [...])` (withoutGlobalScopes because the webhook is unauthenticated — the tenant comes from the Payment row, not request context). Distinct deliveries carry distinct external ids, so genuine events still each get their own row. **Gotcha**: `ToyyibpayLog::recordWebhook()` takes **5** args and derives `external_id` from the payload's `refno`/`billcode`, unlike the Billplz/SecurePay twins which take it explicitly — don't assume the signatures match.
  - **Verified: 21/21 new assertions** (plus the 55 SecurePay ones re-run green — 76 total, dev DB rolled back): a `checked_out`/`checked_in`/`cancelled`/`no_show` booking each **stays** in its status when a deposit settles against it; `pending → confirmed` still works and still dispatches `SendBookingConfirmation` + `PushBookingToGoogleCalendar`; settling twice doesn't re-stamp `deposit_paid_at` or double-send the confirmation; and a retried rejected callback is idempotent for **all three** gateways (exactly 1 audit row, no exception) while a genuinely distinct delivery still records its own.
  - Files: `app/Actions/Payments/SettlePaymentSuccess.php`, `app/Services/Payments/{Toyyibpay/ToyyibpayLog,Billplz/BillplzLog,SecurePay/SecurePayLog}.php`. No migration, no asset rebuild. **Deploy**: `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (PHP-only, OPcache flush). **Billplz is the gateway Wafa is live on, so bug (2) was reachable in production today.**
- **2026-07-09** — **SecurePay verified end-to-end as far as possible without a merchant account; webhook proven live on prod.** Neither documented credential set works (`sandbox.securepay.my` returns `401` for both the docs' "Credentials" table and its PHP sample-code set), and no SecurePay creds are stored locally or on prod — so SecurePay's own two HTTP responses (a real bill returning `payment_url`; a real checksum) remain the **only** unverified segment. Everything on our side is proven. **Live against `https://tempahlah.com` (real HTTPS → nginx → php-fpm → route → controller → MySQL)**: a correctly-signed callback → `200 {"status":"ok"}` logged `verified`; a **tampered** payload (amount changed after signing) → `200 {"error":"invalid_signature"}`, logged `invalid` + `flagged`, payment **not** settled; an exact replay → `200 already_processed`; unknown order → `404 payment_not_found`; empty body → `400 missing_order_number`. The idempotency key proved itself live too — the unpaid and paid callbacks produced **two distinct `external_id`s** (`…:999001:unpaid` vs `…:999001:paid`), so a real B2B1 `99 → 00` transition can't be swallowed as a replay. Tested against a throwaway RM1 Payment on a past `checked_out` booking, with `resolveProvider(1)` asserted to stay `billplz` **before, during and after** (a non-primary SecurePay integration never displaced Wafa's primary Billplz); then fully torn down — 0 residual payments/integrations/webhook_events/payment_transactions, booking #66 back to `checked_out` with 0 payments, `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com` still 200 and still naming Billplz. The **paid → settle** path was deliberately NOT run on prod: it would have tripped bug (1) above and rewound booking #66. **Schema note**: prod MySQL has `payments.booking_id` **NOT NULL** while local SQLite allows null — a real divergence to remember when writing prod probes. **To finish**: register at `sandbox.securepay.my` → Apps → create an API credential → paste UID / Auth token / Checksum token into `/dashboard/integrations/securepay` (leave "Use sandbox" ticked) → **Test connection** validates all three at once via `merchants/validate` and creates nothing. To route a real booking through it, SecurePay must be ticked **primary** (Wafa's Billplz is primary today) — do that with a RM1 booking, then untick.
- **2026-07-09** — **Paid tier made enforceable (Phase 0) + free/paid boundary drawn (Phase 1). Shipped (`0c8ab7c`) + deployed to prod.** Groundwork for charging RM 49/mo.
  - **Phase 0 — the paid tier was not enforceable.** Three independent holes: (1) `POST /dashboard/subscription/change` granted `plan=paid, status=trialing` on a plain authenticated POST — no payment; (2) nothing ever expired a trial, and `Subscription::isPaid()` returned true for `status=trialing` **without checking `trial_ends_at`**, so a self-granted trial was permanent Pro; (3) Pennant runs on the **database** store and **nothing purged the cache on a plan change**, so upgrades never unlocked and downgrades never locked. A fourth found while fixing: downgrading cleared `trial_ends_at`, so a tenant could cycle paid→free→paid and **farm unlimited trials**.
    - `Subscription::isPaid()` rewritten: comped short-circuits true; lapsed trial → false; `active` stays paid until `current_period_end + grace` (derived, so a tenant is never cut off just because the daily command hasn't run); `past_due` paid only while `grace_ends_at` is future; `cancelled` never. New `isComped()`, `inGrace()`, `hasUsedTrial()`, `trialDays()`, `graceDays()`; dead `isOverdue()` fixed.
    - New `SubscriptionObserver` (`#[ObservedBy]`) purges **that tenant's** cached Pennant rows (`Feature::for($tenant)->forget(Feature::defined())` + `flushCache()`) on any flag-bearing write; skips non-flag writes; handles insert via `wasRecentlyCreated` (Eloquent leaves `$changes` empty on insert).
    - New **`subscriptions:process-lifecycle`** command (scheduled daily 02:15, `--dry-run`): trial expired → `past_due` + grace; paid period lapsed → `past_due` + grace **anchored to `current_period_end`, not `now()`** (else a command that misses a week silently gifts a week of grace); grace expired → downgrade to free. Comped rows skipped at every step.
    - `SubscriptionController::change()` no longer grants Pro. It starts the **one** free trial (length from `config('homestay.paid_trial_days')` = 7, was a hardcoded 14), stamps `trial_used_at` (survives downgrade), records the monthly/yearly intent in `meta.billing_preference`, and refuses a second trial. Comped accounts cannot self-change plan (would land on `plan=free` while `comped_at` forced `isPaid()` true). The subscription view never rendered `session('status')`/`session('error')` at all — added.
    - Migration `2026_07_09_120000_add_subscription_lifecycle_columns.php` adds `comped_at`, `grace_ends_at`, `trial_used_at` (+ index), and **backfills `comped_at` on every existing `plan=paid` row**. This is load-bearing: prod auto-deploys migrations and code together, and **Wafa's period ended 2026-07-01** — without the backfill the new `isPaid()` would drop Wafa out of Pro (killing `auto_operational_tasks`, its cleaning/laundry auto-scheduling) the instant it deployed. On prod that backfill is exactly one row.
    - New config `homestay.subscription_grace_days` (7). Filament: `comped_at`/`grace_ends_at`/`trial_used_at` on the Subscription form; **MRR now excludes comped accounts** (`SUM(CASE WHEN comped_at IS NULL …)`) so Wafa doesn't inflate revenue; trial label reads from config.
  - **Phase 1 — free = manual payments only, no invoice/receipt documents.** Note **17 of the 20 Pennant flags were defined but enforced nowhere** (only `ai_agent`, `auto_operational_tasks`, `multiple_properties` were live), so free tenants already had every integration.
    - New flags `payment_gateway` + `invoice_documents` (the old `toyyibpay_payment` and `custom_invoice_template` predate Billplz/SecurePay and were never enforced; kept resolvable).
    - Gateways gated at the **single choke point** `CreateGatewayBill::resolveProvider()` — free tenants resolve `null` even with an enabled integration row, so `PublicHomeBuilder`, `PublicBookingController`, `BookingController::payLink` and `ProcessPaymentLifecycle` all fall back to manual with no change. `execute()` now throws a new **`NoGatewayAvailableException` implements `PaymentGatewayException`** instead of silently falling through to Toyyibpay, so the three existing `catch (PaymentGatewayException)` sites handle it unchanged. `IntegrationController` blocks show/update/test for `toyyibpay|billplz|securepay` (disconnect deliberately stays open so a downgraded tenant can clear creds); the integrations index shows an Upgrade CTA on those tiles, and now renders `session('error')` (it only rendered `status`).
    - Documents gated: `GenerateInvoice` call sites (`PublicBookingController`, `SettlePaymentSuccess::dispatchReceipt`, `BookingController::applyManualPayment`), both `BookingDocumentController` routes, the `<x-booking.documents>` card (pro-lock; compact hint in the calendar), and `settings.invoice-preview` (403).
    - **The load-bearing bit**: the invoice email was the *only* thing a guest received at booking — it carries the pay link (gateway) or the bank details (manual). Gating `GenerateInvoice` outright would have left free tenants' guests with nothing, unable to pay, un-chased, and (on the gateway path) auto-cancelled. So free tenants now send new **`SendBookingInstructions`** → `BookingReceivedMail` (`emails/bookings/received.blade.php`, no attachment) + `WhatsappMessenger::dispatchBookingReceived()` → `MessageTemplates::bookingReceived()` (reuses `manualPayHow()`, never says "invoice"/"receipt"). New `WhatsappMessage::KIND_BOOKING_RECEIVED` + `auto_booking_received` pref (default on).
    - Branding settings: **bank name / holder / account number stay editable on every plan** (`manualPayHow()` reads them to tell a free tenant's guest where to pay). Only the invoice-PDF dressing — logo, tagline, payment QR, terms — is Pro, enforced server-side in `updateBranding()` and `@disabled` in the view.
  - **Verified** against throwaway SQLite DBs driving the real models/observer/command/controllers/jobs: Phase 0 **38 model+command + 22 HTTP** assertions, Phase 1 **32 + 27**, all passing, zero failures. Includes: lapsed trial denies Pro; day-3 of grace grants it, day-10 doesn't; downgrade purges the cache and `ai_agent` flips inactive on the next resolve while another tenant's rows survive; a non-flag write doesn't churn the cache; `--dry-run` writes nothing; a second command run is a no-op; a comped account 90 days lapsed keeps Pro; a second trial is refused; **free tenant with an enabled Billplz row still resolves no provider, `execute()` throws a catchable `PaymentGatewayException`, the public booking creates no Invoice and no Payment and dispatches `SendBookingInstructions` not `SendBookingInvoice`**; the free-tier email renders with the bank details and never says "invoice"; and a **paid control tenant still bills through Billplz and gets its Invoice + `SendBookingInvoice`**.
  - **Billplz reality check** (from their [API reference](https://support.billplz.com/api)): there is **no** subscription / recurring / mandate / direct-debit endpoint. Recurring must be built on **Tokenization** — which is **off by default (paid plan; email support@billplz.com to request access)**, **Visa/Mastercard only** (Senangpay vault, no Amex), and **cannot tokenize FPX** (single-transaction by design). So FPX hosts can never be auto-charged; a monthly pay-link cycle is a prerequisite, not an alternative. Sequence: build the one-off cycle first (works for everyone), layer tokenized auto-charge on top for card holders.
  - **Still to do (Phase 2)**: platform billing. `config/homestay.php` already defines `paid_tier_price` (49.00), `paid_trial_days` and platform-level Toyyibpay/Billplz creds — **nothing in `app/` reads the `channels` block**. Needs a `subscription_invoices` table, a `SubscriptionBillingService` minting RM 49 bills against **Tempahlah's own** Billplz collection (`CreateGatewayBill` can't be reused — it takes a `Booking`; `BillplzClient` can, with platform creds instead of `forTenant()`), a platform webhook that extends `current_period_end` → `active`, dunning inside the grace window, and a checkout replacing the trial button once the trial is used.
  - **Deployed 2026-07-09** (commit `0c8ab7c`, pushed to `main`, auto-deploy). **Verified live on prod**: migration ran (batch 32); Wafa is `comped_at=2026-07-09 13:53:11`, `isComped=true`, `isPaid=true`, `isOverdue=false`, and all seven checked flags (`payment_gateway`, `invoice_documents`, `ai_agent`, `whatsapp_business`, `two_way_calendar_sync`, `auto_operational_tasks`, `marketplace_listing`) resolve **true**, with `resolveProvider(1)` still `'billplz'`. `subscriptions:process-lifecycle --dry-run` reports 0/0/0 (comped rows skipped) and is scheduled daily at 02:15. Authenticated HTTP-kernel renders of `/dashboard`, `/dashboard/subscription` (shows "Complimentary Pro", no stale "14-day" copy), `/dashboard/integrations`, `/dashboard/integrations/billplz`, `/dashboard/settings`, `/dashboard/bookings`, a booking detail (shows "View PDF"), its **invoice PDF** (1.8 MB), `/dashboard/housekeeping`, `/dashboard/calendar` all 200, and the public `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com/` 200. No new errors in `laravel.log`. Deploy = push + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; no asset rebuild.
  - **Still unenforced** and still advertised on the landing page: the free-tier **20 bookings/month** and **3 rooms/property** caps. (Only the 1-property cap is enforced, via `multiple_properties`.)
- **2026-07-09** — **SecurePay added as a THIRD payment gateway (sandbox-first), alongside Toyyibpay + Billplz.** Tenants can connect **SecurePay** (their own account) at `/dashboard/integrations/securepay` and take FPX/card bookings through it. Built as a full mirror of the Billplz package, so the gateway-agnostic settlement path (`SettlePaymentSuccess`) is untouched.
  - **Which SecurePay API, and why.** SecurePay exposes two ways to start a payment. `POST /api/v1/payments` is the classic FPX endpoint: checksum-signed, designed for a **browser** POST (`redirect_post=true` auto-submits the shopper onto the bank page), and its success response body is **undocumented**. `POST /api/apis/payments` ("Payment Session", HTTP Basic auth `uid:token`) returns JSON with a durable **`payment_url`**. Tempahlah needs a *shareable* URL — pay links are emailed, WhatsApp'd, printed on invoices and re-opened days later by the balance reminder — so we use the **Payment Session** endpoint. It also matches the existing Toyyibpay/Billplz `{payment, payment_url, bill_code, reused}` contract exactly.
  - **New service package** `app/Services/Payments/SecurePay/`: `SecurePayClient` (per-tenant creds from `tenant_integrations` — `uid`, `auth_token`, `checksum_token`, `is_sandbox`, `is_primary`; `forTenant()`; `createPayment()` → `POST {base}/api/apis/payments` with `Http::withBasicAuth($uid, $authToken)`, **amount as a plain decimal string** (`150.00`, NOT cents — unlike Billplz), `order_number = payment.public_id`; `getPaymentStatus()` → `GET {base}/api/v1/payments/status/{order_number}` for server-side reconciliation; `testConnection()` → `POST {base}/api/v1/merchants/validate`, which validates **all three credentials in one call** and creates nothing to clean up; `formatPhone()` normalises `0127964501` → `+60127964501`; and the **checksum verifier** — `ksort($params, SORT_STRING)`, join the **values** with `|`, `hash_hmac('sha256', …, $checksumToken)`). Plus `SecurePayException` (implements the shared `PaymentGatewayException` marker) + `SecurePayLog`.
  - **Checksum correctness** — `verifyChecksum()` reproduces **byte-for-byte** the worked example in `docs.securepay.my/api/url.md` (expected `41712f0c…a40bbf`), and the create-payment checksum example in `api/merchant/payment.md` (`75b54e40…b78844`) also reproduces. Note `SORT_STRING`: PHP's default `ksort()` compares numeric-looking keys numerically, which would diverge from SecurePay's plain string sort. A payload carrying a **nested** value (the optional `params` bag) can't be flattened back into their pipe-joined source unambiguously → treated as `missing` → falls back to a server-side status check rather than guessing.
  - **Bases**: prod `https://securepay.my`, sandbox `https://sandbox.securepay.my` (per-tenant `is_sandbox`). Unlike the Billplz client these are **host roots without a version segment**, because the paths differ per endpoint family (`/api/apis/…` vs `/api/v1/…`).
  - **Actions/controllers**: `CreateSecurePayBill` (twin of `CreateBillplzBill`; `Payment::METHOD_SECUREPAY`, `gateway_provider='securepay'`, reuse guard on an open `processing` bill). **`gateway_ref` stores the `order_number` (= the Payment's `public_id`)** — the only merchant-owned key SecurePay echoes on the callback, and the key the status endpoint is addressed by; the session `slug` goes in `meta`. `SecurePayWebhookController@handle` on `POST /webhooks/securepay` (new `throttle:webhook-securepay`, 100/min): resolves the Payment by `order_number`, verifies the checksum with **that tenant's** token, falls back to a server-side `getPaymentStatus()` when unverifiable, and settles through the shared `SettlePaymentSuccess`.
  - **⚠️ SecurePay POSTs to `redirect_url`** (Toyyibpay + Billplz both GET). So `payments.return` became `Route::match(['get','post'], …)` and `payments/return/*` was added to a new **CSRF `except` list** in `bootstrap/app.php`. Safe: `PaymentReturnController` never trusts the posted body — it re-checks state with the gateway (verified by a test that POSTs a forged `payment_status=true` while the gateway says unpaid; the payment stays `processing`). Also gained a `securepay` reconcile branch.
  - **Idempotency**: `order_number` alone is NOT a safe webhook key — SecurePay legitimately calls back twice for one order (a failed attempt then a successful retry; or B2B1's `fpx_debit_auth_code` 99 *pending approval* → 00 *approved*). Keying on the order alone would make that second, **decisive** callback look like a replay and silently drop it. The key is `{order_number}:{payment_id|exchange_number}:{paid|unpaid}` — order first, because `webhook_events.external_id` is **globally unique across providers**.
  - **Bug found + fixed during verification**: `payment_transactions` is `UNIQUE(provider, external_id)`, and the rejected-callback branches (bad checksum, missing tenant creds) return early **without** stamping `processed_at` — so the replay guard doesn't catch a retry, and SecurePay *does* retry. The audit insert then blew up on the constraint → **500**. `SecurePayLog::recordWebhook` now uses `PaymentTransaction::withoutGlobalScopes()->firstOrCreate(...)` (withoutGlobalScopes because the webhook is unauthenticated — the tenant comes from the Payment row, not request context). **`BillplzLog` has the identical latent bug** and was left alone (out of scope).
  - **Gateway selection**: `CreateGatewayBill` generalised from 2 → 3 providers via a `PRECEDENCE` list (`toyyibpay, billplz, securepay`). One enabled → use it. Several → the one ticked `is_primary` wins (scanned in precedence order, so two "primary" ticks still resolve deterministically); with none ticked, **Toyyibpay stays the default** so every existing tenant keeps billing exactly as it does today. New `CreateGatewayBill::displayName()` centralises the provider→label map (was a ternary duplicated in `PublicHomeBuilder` + `book-sent.blade.php`).
  - **No migration** — `payments.method`/`gateway_provider` are plain `string` columns, and `webhook_events`/`tenant_integrations` are gateway-agnostic (`config` is `encrypted:array`).
  - **Verified: 55/55 assertions**, driven against the real actions/controllers with the webhook + return page dispatched through the **actual HTTP kernel**, inside a rolled-back transaction (dev DB left untouched — confirmed 0 residual rows). Covers: checksum vs SecurePay's own doc examples (+ tamper rejection); `createPayment` request shape (Basic auth = `uid:auth_token`, `transaction_amount=150.00` decimal, `order_number` = public_id, `+60` phone, callback/redirect URLs); reuse guard (no double-billing); a correctly-signed PAID callback → Payment `succeeded` + Booking `confirmed` + `deposit_paid_at`; replay ignored; **tampered checksum → 200 `invalid_signature`, payment NOT settled, attempt flagged**; unknown order → 404; the 99→00 transition NOT swallowed as a replay; POST-return works (no 419) and a **forged** paid body doesn't settle; GET-return still works for Toyyibpay/Billplz; and precedence regression guards (billplz `is_primary` still beats toyyibpay; all-three-none-primary → toyyibpay). Separately, the **live sandbox** was probed: `/api/apis/payments`, `/api/v1/merchants/validate` and `/api/v1/payments/status/{order}` all return **401** with bogus creds while a fabricated path returns **404** — confirming the endpoint paths and that the session endpoint uses HTTP Basic.
  - **Not yet exercised against a real SecurePay sandbox account** (needs a tenant to enter real credentials — outbound HTTP was faked). **⚠️ Sandbox-first**: `is_sandbox` defaults ON; untick "Use sandbox (sandbox.securepay.my)" with live keys before taking real money.
  - **Deploy**: no migration, no asset rebuild. `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`. **Do not run `route:cache`/`config:cache`** (apex `home` closure; `WhatsAppService` still calls `env()`) — prod runs both uncached, so the new routes appear on deploy. **Partial-commit note**: a concurrent session already committed + pushed the service package, `CreateSecurePayBill`, the webhook controller, `routes/api.php` and the rate limiter (`192202c`, `c2c2540`) — so prod already carries the **dormant** half (nothing calls it; no tenant has SecurePay enabled). The rest (dispatcher, CSRF/POST return, integrations UI, `SecurePayLog` fix) is **still uncommitted** in the working tree.
- **2026-07-09** — **New-booking page (`/dashboard/bookings/create`) — mobile redesign.** The page had **no media queries at all**: the Guest card was a hardcoded `1fr 1fr` and Booking details a `1fr 1fr 1fr`, both forced onto 360px phones; `.input` (`height:36px`, `font:inherit` = 14px) made **iOS Safari zoom the whole page on focus**; the calendar arrows were 30px (under the 44px touch-target min); and the footer was `justify-content:flex-end`, cramming tiny buttons into the right edge. Replaced the inline-style soup with a scoped `.nb-*` class system + a single `@media (max-width:640px)` block (matches the app shell's breakpoint) — **desktop is pixel-identical**. Mobile now: cards `20px → 16px 14px` padding, `.nb-grid-2`/`.nb-grid-3` collapse to 1 column, inputs `16px/44px` (no iOS zoom), calendar arrows 38px + tighter cell gaps, payment radio cards stack 1-up, and the footer stacks with **"Create booking" full-width under the thumb** and Cancel below it. Two latent bugs fixed on the way: (a) the inline `grid-column: 1 / 3` / `1 / 4` spans would have spawned an **implicit extra column** once the grid collapsed to 1 — now `1 / -1`; (b) **`input[type=date]` has a ~177px intrinsic min-width**, so the check-in/check-out `1fr 1fr` pair overflowed its card (16px at 390px, **86px at 320px**, silently clipped) — fixed with `.nb-grid > * { min-width: 0 }` + `minmax(0,1fr)` tracks, and the date pair now **stacks on mobile** (the availability calendar above is the primary picker). Adults/Children stay paired (number inputs shrink fine). Preserved the concurrently-added live **Price/quote** card verbatim (its inline styles moved to `.nb-price-*`/`.nb-money-*`). **Verified in headless Chrome over CDP** (system Chrome, no new deps) at 320/390/1280px logged in as the demo owner: `document.scrollWidth === innerWidth` and **0 overflowing elements inside the form** at every width (was 3, clipped, before the date fix); computed styles confirm 1-col grids + 16px/44px inputs + `flex-direction:column` actions on mobile and 2-col/3-col + 36px inputs + `row` actions on desktop; the live quote fetch returns RM 600 for 3 nights × RM 200 and the breakdown renders; 0 JS console errors. - **2026-07-07** — **Fix: switching a tenant from Toyyibpay to Billplz didn't move the public booking page onto Billplz — the online-pay option vanished (defaulted to manual).** A host connected + enabled Billplz (and *disabled* Toyyibpay), but the public link (`{slug}.tempahlah.com`) still didn't bill through Billplz. Root cause was NOT the backend — `CreateGatewayBill::resolveProvider(1)` correctly returned `'billplz'` and a live sandbox Billplz bill created fine (http 200). The bug was in the **public page's gateway-detection flag**: `PublicHomeBuilder::build()` computed `$toyyibpayConfigured` by querying **only** the `toyyibpay` integration (`->where('provider', PROVIDER_TOYYIBPAY)->where('enabled', true)`). With Toyyibpay disabled + Billplz enabled, that flag was **false**, so `public-tenant/home.blade.php` (a) hid the "Pay online now" option (only shown when `$toyyibpayConfigured && $manualPaymentEnabled`) and (b) defaulted the Alpine `payMethod` to `'manual'` (`opts.toyyibpayConfigured ? 'gateway' : 'manual'`) — so guests only ever got the bank-transfer/manual path and never reached the Billplz gateway. **Fix**: `PublicHomeBuilder` now derives the flag from the **gateway-agnostic dispatcher** — `app(CreateGatewayBill::class)->resolveProvider($tenant->id)` (checks Toyyibpay **or** Billplz, the same resolver the booking POST bills through) → `$toyyibpayConfigured = provider !== null`, and passes a new `$gatewayName` ('Billplz'/'Toyyibpay') so the copy is accurate. Also de-hardcoded the "You'll be redirected to Toyyibpay" wording in `home.blade.php` (booking fine-print + fallback line) and `book-sent.blade.php` (derives the name from `$payment->gateway_provider`) — both with a `?? 'Toyyibpay'` null-safe fallback so other render paths (marketplace) can't error. The `$toyyibpayConfigured` variable name is kept (view + Alpine unchanged) but now means "an online gateway is configured". **Verified on prod** via the HTTP kernel rendering `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com/`: `resolveProvider(1)='billplz'`, page 200, `toyyibpayConfigured: true`, defaults to the gateway path, mentions "Billplz", and no longer says "redirected to Toyyibpay". Files: `app/Services/Public/PublicHomeBuilder.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`, `resources/views/public-tenant/book-sent.blade.php`. Deployed via scp → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`. **⚠️ Note for the host**: the Billplz integration is currently in **sandbox mode** (`is_sandbox=1`) — bills go to `billplz-sandbox.com` (test only; real customers can't actually pay). For live bookings, untick "Use sandbox (billplz-sandbox.com)" in `/dashboard/integrations/billplz` and re-test.

- **2026-07-05** — **Fix: sending an invoice via WhatsApp/email auto-cancelled the booking a few minutes later.** Root cause: `BookingDocumentController::invoicePayUrl()` (the pay link resolved when a host sends an invoice) **mints a fresh Toyyibpay deposit bill** for the outstanding amount → creates a `Payment(type=deposit, gateway_provider='toyyibpay')`. But `ProcessPaymentLifecycle::pendingUnpaidOnline()` identified an "abandoned online booking" purely by *"has a toyyibpay deposit payment"*, so attaching that pay-link retroactively made a **manual / phone / older** booking match the fee-auto-cancel query — and if its `fee_due_at` had already passed, the hourly `bookings:process-payment-lifecycle` cancelled it (freeing the dates + notifying the guest). This defeated the manual-payment design (manual bookings were meant to never auto-cancel). **Fix**: auto-cancel is now gated on booking *intent*, not on the presence of a gateway payment. The guest online pay-now flow (`PublicBookingController::store`, gateway branch) stamps `meta['fee_autocancel'] = true` on the booking; `ProcessPaymentLifecycle` now only chases/cancels bookings carrying that flag (new `feeAutocancelEligible()` guard in both the fee-chase and fee-cancel loops). Manual bookings, host-attached pay links ("send invoice"), and `payLink` never set the flag → never auto-cancelled. Also broadened the coarse prefilter to include Billplz deposit payments (was Toyyibpay-only). **Trade-off**: genuine online bookings created *before* this fix lack the flag, so they won't auto-cancel — the host can cancel those manually; all new online bookings self-heal. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`, `app/Console/Commands/ProcessPaymentLifecycle.php`. PHP lint clean; not runtime-verified locally (vendor/ absent). **Deploy**: scp the 2 files → `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (no migration, no asset build; the scheduler + `email` queue worker must be running as before).
- **2026-07-04** — **Fix: "View PDF" served a stale invoice/receipt (old template) — now always re-renders from the current template + branding.** A host reported the invoice PDF didn't reflect the redesigned template. Root cause: `BookingDocumentController` get-or-creates the `Invoice` record then `streamPdf()` served the **stored PDF file** from disk — so a document generated with the OLD template kept serving that stale file forever; the redesign only applied to brand-new documents. **Fix**: new `renderPdf(Invoice, Booking, ?Payment)` helper renders `pdf.invoice` fresh from the CURRENT template + live tenant branding (logo/bank/QR), **overwrites the stored file** (so it stays in sync), and returns the binary. `show()` (View PDF) now streams that fresh render; `send()` calls it before dispatching so the **email attachment + WhatsApp signed-URL** also carry the latest design. The invoice number + line-item data stay as-issued (snapshotted on the record) — only the design/branding refreshes. Threads `$payment` through so the receipt's paid-amount/method render correctly. **Verified on prod**: rendering booking 80's existing invoice (`WAF-INV-26-0012`, real data) via the authed route now returns the redesigned PDF (gradient header, letter-spaced name, stay strip, total band, "Thank You") — was the old layout. - **2026-07-04** — **Fix: booking detail page 500'd for every booking (`/dashboard/bookings/{id}`) — a literal `<x-…>` tag inside a CSS comment.** After the calendar-documents refactor, opening ANY booking threw `syntax error, unexpected end of file, expecting "endif"` from `show.blade.php`. Root cause: when I removed the `.bk-doc*` styles from show.blade I left a CSS comment reading `/* … live in the shared <x-booking.documents> component … */`. **Blade's component-tag compiler scans the entire template — including inside `<style>` blocks and CSS comments — and parsed that literal `<x-booking.documents>` (no self-close) as a real, unclosed component tag**, emitting an `if($component->shouldRender()):` with no matching `endif;` → the compiled PHP wouldn't parse. `php artisan view:cache` "succeeds" because it only *writes* the compiled file (no PHP-lint), so the break only surfaced at include time; under prod OPcache (`enable_file_override`) the broken compiled view kept being served even after a graceful `reload` (needed a full `systemctl restart php8.4-fpm`). Diagnosed by compiling show.blade with `blade.compiler->compileString()` + `php -l` on the output and bisecting (removing the component line fixed it) → traced to the comment. **Fix**: dropped the angle brackets in the comment (`<x-booking.documents>` → `booking.documents`). The two real usages (show.blade + calendar, both self-closed `<x-booking.documents … />`) were always fine. **Lesson: never write a literal `<x-component>` tag in Blade comments or `<style>`/text — Blade will try to compile it. Verify Blade changes by actually rendering/linting the compiled output, not just `view:cache` (which doesn't lint).** Verified: all 3 views compile to valid PHP locally; on prod, authenticated renders of `/dashboard/bookings/{75,80,90}` return **HTTP 200** (were 500). File: `resources/views/tenant/bookings/show.blade.php`. Deployed (scp + `view:cache` + `systemctl restart php8.4-fpm`).
