- **2026-07-04** — **Manual (offline) payment option on the public booking page — pay by bank transfer / cash, host confirms.** Per host request, when a guest picks dates on the tenant subdomain (`{slug}.tempahlah.com`) and goes to pay, they can now choose **Pay online now** (Toyyibpay/Billplz gateway) OR **Pay manually** (bank transfer / cash). Manual payers still get an invoice (email + WhatsApp) — carrying the host's payment instructions instead of a pay link — and the booking sits `pending` until the host marks it paid in the dashboard, which now also sends the guest a **receipt**. **New tenant settings** (`/dashboard/settings` → "Manual payment (bank transfer / cash)"): a master toggle `manual_payment_enabled` (default ON — works even with no gateway connected) + a `manual_payment_instructions` textarea (bank name/acc no/DuitNow, shown to the guest on the invoice + booking-received page; blank → "contact the host to arrange payment"). New `Tenant::manualPaymentEnabled()` / `manualPaymentInstructions()` + `MANUAL_PAYMENT_ENABLED_DEFAULT`. Migration `2026_07_04_130000_add_manual_payment_to_tenants.php` (idempotent). **Public form** (`public-tenant/home.blade.php`): a radio selector (shown only when BOTH gateway + manual are available; otherwise pinned to whichever works), a hidden `payment_method` field bound to Alpine `payMethod`, and reactive submit-button/fine-print copy ("Pay now RM X → Toyyibpay" vs "Confirm booking → invoice with instructions"). The whole book form is now gated by `$toyyibpayConfigured || $manualPaymentEnabled` (was gateway-only), with `.wf-paymethod*` CSS. `StoreBookingRequest` validates `payment_method ∈ {gateway,manual}`. **`PublicBookingController::store`** resolves the effective method (falls back gateway↔manual if the chosen one isn't set up, WhatsApp deeplink only if neither works); the manual branch skips `CreateGatewayBill`, generates the invoice with a **null payment (no Payment row)** — so the lifecycle command never auto-cancels it (that only targets bookings with an unpaid `toyyibpay` deposit bill) — dispatches `SendBookingInvoice(..., manual: true)`, and lands on a manual variant of `book-sent` (instructions panel + "Send payment proof" WA CTA). **Manual invoice comms**: `SendBookingInvoice`/`BookingInvoiceMail`/`emails/bookings/invoice.blade.php` + `WhatsappMessenger::dispatchInvoice`/`MessageTemplates::invoice` all gained a `bool $manual` flag → render bank-transfer instructions + "no pay link" copy instead of the pay button (subject "Invoice: REF" vs "Pay deposit: REF"). **Receipt on manual mark-paid**: `BookingController::applyManualPayment` now also generates a `TYPE_RECEIPT` invoice + dispatches `SendBookingReceipt` for the money recorded (mirroring the gateway `SettlePaymentSuccess` flow) — so a manually-paid booking fee yields a fee receipt and marking full payment yields the full receipt. All signature changes are backward-compatible (new params default; existing callers — `ProcessPaymentLifecycle`, `BookingDocumentController`, `sendInvoiceManual` — unaffected). All PHP lint clean; Blade directives balanced. **Not runtime-verified locally** (vendor/ not installed in this workspace). **Deploy**: scp the changed files + `php artisan migrate --force` (prod MySQL) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; needs a queue worker on `email` for the invoice/receipt comms. No asset rebuild (page-scoped CSS/Alpine).
- **2026-07-04** — **Booking detail: Invoice & Receipt documents — view the PDF + email / WhatsApp it to the guest (receipt shareable once paid).** Per host request, opening a booking (`/dashboard/bookings/{id}`) now has an **"Invoice & receipt"** card with, for each document, **View PDF · Email · WhatsApp**. It reuses the exact automated-flow infrastructure so a manual send is byte-identical to the auto one: `GenerateInvoice` (creates the `Invoice`/receipt record + stores the PDF), `BookingInvoiceMail`/`BookingReceiptMail` (attach the stored PDF), and the WhatsApp `MessageTemplates::invoice()/receipt()` (attach the PDF via a 7-day signed Spaces URL). **Rules**: the **invoice** is always available (the bill); the **receipt unlocks the moment ANY payment has succeeded — deposit OR full — so a fully-paid booking can always share its receipt** (the host's explicit requirement). Documents are **get-or-created** (first view/send mints a stable number + stored PDF; later actions reuse it, so numbers don't churn). New **`BookingDocumentController`**: `show()` streams the PDF inline from disk (falls back to a fresh render); `send()` validates `doc∈{invoice,receipt}` + `channel∈{email,whatsapp}`, checks prerequisites (guest email for email; connected WhatsApp session + guest phone for WA), and dispatches — email via `Mail::queue`, WhatsApp via new **`WhatsappMessenger::sendInvoiceManual()`/`sendReceiptManual()`** which run through a new **`manualDispatch()`** helper that **bypasses the `auto_invoice`/`auto_receipt` auto-send preference** (the host explicitly clicked send) while still honouring the connected-session / resolvable-phone / guest-opt-out guards + `RecipientGuard`. Invoice sends resolve a pay link (reuse an open Toyyibpay bill → else mint one for the outstanding amount → else empty when fully paid; all soft-failing so the PDF still goes out). Also: `MessageTemplates::receipt()` now says the **actual payment method** (`via Toyyibpay` / `via Billplz` / `(cash / bank transfer)` for manual) instead of hardcoding "Toyyibpay", and the copy now reads "receipt PDF is attached"; the booking show page also now surfaces `session('error')` flashes (red) not just `status` (green). New routes `GET /bookings/{id}/documents/{doc}` (`bookings.documents.show`, `doc` constrained to `invoice|receipt`) + `POST /bookings/{id}/documents/send` (`bookings.documents.send`). Files: new `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingDocumentController.php`, `app/Services/WhatsApp/WhatsappMessenger.php` (+2 manual methods + `manualDispatch`), `app/Services/WhatsApp/MessageTemplates.php` (dynamic method label), `routes/web.php`, `resources/views/tenant/bookings/show.blade.php` (docs card + error flash + scoped `.bk-doc*` CSS). All PHP lint clean; Blade directives balanced; icons (receipt/link/mail/message) confirmed present. **Not runtime-verified locally** (vendor/ not installed in this workspace). **Deploy**: scp the 5 files → `route:cache` (new routes) + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; needs a queue worker on `email`/`default` for the email + WhatsApp to actually fire, and (prod) the S3/Spaces disk for the WhatsApp PDF signed URL + email attachment. No asset rebuild.
- **2026-07-04** — **Fully-automated housekeeping SOP — cleaning + laundry auto-scheduled from confirmed bookings (Operations → Housekeeping).** Per host request, when a booking is confirmed the system now auto-creates the housekeeping schedule following a typical Malaysian homestay routine — no per-booking setup. Logic lives in the rewritten `App\Actions\Operations\GenerateOperationalTasksForBooking` (was a dormant stub, never called):
  - **Post-checkout turnover** — a **full clean 30 min after check-out** (checkout 12:00pm → clean 12:30pm, using the property's `check_out_time`). Crew scales to the turnaround: if another guest checks in on the **same room within 2 days** (`TURNOVER_WINDOW_DAYS`) → **2 cleaners, ~2h** (rush); otherwise → **1 cleaner, ~4h** (thorough, no rush). Re-runs keep an *unedited auto* task's crew/duration current if a later booking appears.
  - **Pre-arrival dusting** (`type=pre_arrival`, "habuk") — added **~3h before check-in** only when the house has **sat idle ≥3 days** (`PRE_CLEAN_IDLE_DAYS`) before this booking (or has no prior booking). If a guest was in within 2 days, it's skipped (house still fresh). 1 cleaner, ~2h.
  - **Laundry** — linen batch after checkout (pickup +2h, return +1 day), unchanged.
  - **Schema** — migration `2026_07_04_120000_add_housekeeping_automation.php` (idempotent): `cleaning_tasks.{cleaners_required (default 1), duration_minutes (nullable), auto_generated (bool)}` + `tenants.auto_housekeeping (bool, default true)`. `CleaningTask` gains `TYPE_PRE_ARRIVAL`, casts, `TYPES`, `durationHours()`. `Tenant::autoHousekeepingEnabled()` + `AUTO_HOUSEKEEPING_DEFAULT`.
  - **Wiring** — called on the **first pending→confirmed transition** in both `SettlePaymentSuccess` (online/Toyyibpay/Billplz webhook + return path — wrapped in try/catch so a scheduling hiccup can't break settlement) and `BookingController::applyManualPayment` (host records cash/bank payment). Gated by the paid-tier Pennant feature `auto_operational_tasks` **scoped explicitly to the booking's tenant** (`Feature::for($tenant)` — the webhook path has no tenant context) AND the `auto_housekeeping` master toggle.
  - **UI** — new Settings card **"Housekeeping automation"** (master toggle + plain-language SOP explainer). Housekeeping create + edit forms gain **Cleaners needed** + **Duration (hours)** fields and a **Pre-arrival dusting** type; cleaning cards show a `👥 N · ⏱ Xh` pill + an **Auto** badge; the copy-paste WhatsApp text includes crew + duration. A host edit flips `auto_generated=false` so the SOP never overwrites a manually-tuned task.
  - **Verified** via the action + controllers driven directly against a fresh seeded SQLite DB: 7 SOP cases pass exactly (isolated→1/4h+pre-arrival; back-to-back→2/2h; within-2-days→no pre-arrival; 5-day idle→pre-arrival; idempotency; host-edit protection; master-toggle-off→no tasks) + create/edit form round-trips (hours→minutes, duration preserved on partial edit) + housekeeping/settings/create pages render 200 with the new UI. **Note**: a concurrent session bundled most of these files into commit `a680679`; the essential Blade fix in `cleaning-card.blade.php` (the inline `@if…👥…{{ }}h@endif` compiled to a broken glued `@endif` — Blade doesn't recognise a directive glued to a word char, 500'd the page whenever a crew/duration task rendered; refactored to a precomputed `$crewLabel`) is applied in the working tree — **must be committed before deploy** or `/dashboard/housekeeping` 500s. **Deploy**: scp changed files + `php artisan migrate --force` (prod MySQL) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-07-04** — **Billplz integrated as a second payment gateway (parallel to Toyyibpay).** Studied the Billplz API v3 sandbox docs (`support.billplz.com/api`) and built a full mirror of the Toyyibpay stack so a tenant can accept FPX/card bookings through their own Billplz account.
  - **New service package** `app/Services/Payments/Billplz/`: `BillplzClient` (per-tenant creds from `tenant_integrations` — `api_key`, `collection_id`, `x_signature_key`, `is_sandbox`, `is_primary`; `forTenant()`; `createBill()` → `POST {base}/v3/bills` with `Http::withBasicAuth($apiKey, '')`, amount in cents, `reference_1 = payment.public_id`, callback + redirect URLs; `getBill()` for server-side reconciliation; `isPaid()` handling both the callback string `"true"` and the getBill bool; `testConnection()` that creates then deletes a RM1 bill; and the **X-Signature verifier** `verifySignature()` — encodes each `key.value`, case-insensitively `usort`s, joins with `|`, `hash_hmac('sha256', …, xSignatureKey)`, matching the official `billplz/billplz-php` lib). Bases: prod `https://www.billplz.com/api`, sandbox `https://www.billplz-sandbox.com/api`. Plus `BillplzException` + `BillplzLog` (audit into `payment_transactions`/`webhook_events`, provider `billplz`).
  - **Signature correctness**: verified `verifySignature()`'s source-string construction reproduces **exactly** Billplz's documented callback example (`amount100|collection_id…|…|paidtrue|statepaid|url…`) and redirect example (`billplzidzq0tm2wc|billplzpaid_at2018-09-27 15:15:09 +0800|billplzpaidtrue`) — the redirect flattens `billplz[paid_at]` → `billplzpaid_at` (underscore kept). Callbacks with no X-Signature key fall back to a server-side `getBill()` check before trusting `paid` (mirrors Toyyibpay's DuitNow-QR path).
  - **Actions/controllers**: `CreateBillplzBill` (twin of `CreateToyyibpayBill` — same `{payment, payment_url, bill_code, reused}` return, `Payment::METHOD_BILLPLZ` (new constant), `gateway_provider='billplz'`, reuse guard on an existing `processing` bill). `BillplzWebhookController@handle` on `POST /webhooks/billplz` (new `throttle:webhook-billplz` limiter, 100/min): resolves the Payment by bill `id`→`gateway_ref` (fallback `reference_1`→`public_id`), verifies X-Signature over `$request->post()` minus `x_signature`, idempotent via `webhook_events`, and settles through the **unchanged, gateway-agnostic** `SettlePaymentSuccess`. `PaymentReturnController` now reconciles both gateways (a `reconcile()` branch: Toyyibpay `getBillTransactions` vs Billplz `getBill`).
  - **Gateway selection** — new `CreateGatewayBill` dispatcher (`resolveProvider()`/`gatewayConfigured()`): only-one-enabled → that one; both enabled → Billplz **only if** the tenant ticked "Use Billplz as my main gateway", otherwise Toyyibpay stays the default (backward-compatible with every existing tenant); none → null (callers fall back to the WhatsApp deeplink). `PublicBookingController` (now `gatewayConfigured()` gate + `CreateGatewayBill`), `BookingController::payLink`, and `ProcessPaymentLifecycle::mintBalancePayUrl` all route through it and catch the shared **`PaymentGatewayException`** marker interface (implemented by both `ToyyibpayException` + `BillplzException`) instead of the Toyyibpay-specific type.
  - **Integrations UI**: dropped the `soon` flag on Billplz (index tile now links to Connect); `IntegrationController::providerMeta('billplz')` gets real fields (API secret key, collection ID, X-Signature key, sandbox toggle, primary toggle), `validationRulesFor('billplz')`, and a `testBillplz()` "Test connection" action; the generic `integrations/show.blade.php` test button now covers `['toyyibpay','billplz']` via `route('tenant.integrations.'.$provider.'.test')`.
  - **No migration** — `payments` (`gateway_provider`/`gateway_ref`), `webhook_events`, and `tenant_integrations` (`PROVIDER_BILLPLZ` already existed, `config` is `encrypted:array`) are all gateway-agnostic. All changed PHP lints clean; the X-Signature algorithm was verified with a standalone script. **Not yet exercised end-to-end against a live Billplz sandbox account** (needs a tenant to enter real sandbox creds) and **not deployed** — local change only. **Deploy**: scp the new `app/Services/Payments/Billplz/*`, `app/Services/Payments/PaymentGatewayException.php`, `app/Actions/Payments/CreateBillplzBill.php` + `CreateGatewayBill.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Webhooks/BillplzWebhookController.php`, the edited controllers/command/model/provider/routes + the 2 integration blades → `route:cache` (new routes) + `config:clear` + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`. Then in the tenant dashboard connect Billplz + Test connection, and set the Billplz `callback_url`/`redirect_url` are auto-passed per bill (no dashboard config needed at Billplz's end beyond the collection).
- **2026-07-04** — **New-booking form: availability calendar that greys out already-booked dates so the host can't double-book.** The manual booking form (`/dashboard/bookings/create`) previously used two bare `<input type="date">` fields with **no indication of which dates were already taken** for the selected room — the only guard against a double-booking was the server-side `AvailabilityService` check that surfaced *after* submit as a flash error. Added an **inline month-grid availability calendar** (Alpine, in the Stay card) that visually marks each night as **Available / Booked / Your dates** for the *currently-selected room* and drives the check-in/check-out fields. **Backend** (`BookingController::create`): builds `$roomBookedDates` = `{ room_id: ['YYYY-MM-DD', …] }` of **occupied nights** across the tenant's active bookings (`pending`/`confirmed`/`checked_in`, `check_out >= today`) **and** host `CalendarBlock`s (room-specific + null-room property-wide), expanding each range as the half-open interval `[check_in, check_out)` — so the check-out morning stays bookable (back-to-back arrivals), exactly matching `AvailabilityService`. Passed to the view as `roomBookedDates`. **Frontend** (`resources/views/tenant/bookings/create.blade.php`): a self-contained Alpine calendar — booked nights render red + struck-through + non-clickable; clicking picks check-in then check-out; a pick that would span a booked night just starts a fresh range; the native date inputs stay editable and two-way-bound (`x-model` `checkIn`/`checkOut`), with `:min` on check-out and `revalidateRange()` clearing an invalid range when the room changes. A **live conflict warning banner** (`rangeConflict()`, checks the occupied-night overlap — also catches manual typing) shows above the calendar and next to the submit button, and the **"Create booking" button is disabled while the range conflicts**. Single-room tenants keep the remote's auto-select (the lone room seeds `selectedRoom` so the calendar lights up immediately). Month nav can't go before the current month; weekday labels + month label localize (BM/EN). Scoped `<style>` block (`.avail-cal-*`), no shared CSS touched. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php` (query + `roomBookedDates`), `resources/views/tenant/bookings/create.blade.php` (calendar UI + Alpine). PHP lint clean; CalendarBlock confirmed tenant-scoped with `starts_on`/`ends_on` date casts. **Deploy**: scp the 2 files → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (per the OPcache gotcha below); no asset rebuild (inline Alpine + inline `<style>`).

- **2026-06-24** — **Housekeeping "Share on WhatsApp" — build the share URL client-side so emoji match the Copy button.** A host reported the WhatsApp schedule's emoji arriving as `�` after tapping **Share on WhatsApp**, while the on-screen preview + **Copy text** were fine. Server-side encoding was verified correct (`rawurlencode("🧹")` = `%F0%9F%A7%B9`, controller file is valid UTF-8), so the byte-identical fix is to stop using the server-rendered `href` and instead build the `wa.me/?text=` URL **in the browser** from the same hidden `$refs.<refName>` textarea value the (working) clipboard copy reads — `@click.prevent="window.open('https://wa.me/?text=' + encodeURIComponent($refs.<ref>.value), '_blank')"`. `encodeURIComponent` always emits UTF-8 percent-encoding from the exact DOM string, so the share path now carries precisely the bytes the Copy path does. The original `href` (rawurlencode) is kept as a no-JS / middle-click fallback. - **2026-06-23** — **Persistent login for the PWA — hosts stay signed in across app closes (no more re-login).** A host reported that closing the installed PWA forced them to log in again. Root cause: the login only set a short-lived session cookie (`SESSION_LIFETIME=120` min) and the "Remember me" checkbox was **unchecked by default**, so no long-lived recaller cookie was issued — and installed PWAs (notably iOS standalone) evict plain session cookies when the app is closed. **Fix**: `AuthenticatedSessionController::store()` now **always** passes `$remember = true` to `Auth::attempt()`, so every login issues Laravel's `remember_web_*` recaller cookie (~5-year lifetime) regardless of the checkbox; the middleware re-authenticates transparently on the next open (and `SetTenantContext` already falls back to the user's first active membership when the regenerated session lacks `current_tenant_public_id`, so tenant context survives the recaller path). The login form's checkbox is now pre-`checked` so the UI matches the behaviour. Also raised `SESSION_LIFETIME` 120 → **525600 (1 year)** in `.env.example` so the active session itself is long-lived and the recaller path rarely needs to fire. `users` already has the `rememberToken()` column, so no migration. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Auth/AuthenticatedSessionController.php`, `resources/views/auth/login.blade.php`, `.env.example`. PHP lint clean, **no asset rebuild**. **Deploy**: scp the controller + login view → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`. **Prod .env (optional but recommended)**: set `SESSION_LIFETIME=525600` then `php artisan config:cache` + reload php-fpm — the recaller cookie alone already delivers the persistent login, this just avoids re-running the recaller every 2 hours. (Stable `APP_KEY` required for the recaller to validate — already the case on prod.)

- **2026-06-23** — **Fix: check-out (and check-in) reminders fired ~8 hours late — sent AFTER the guest had already checked out.** A host set the pre-checkout reminder to 3 hours before check-out but received it ~5pm, after a noon checkout. **Root cause = timezone, not the reminder logic.** `config/app.php` runs the app in **UTC** (hardcoded `'timezone' => 'UTC'`), but a property's `check_out_time` of `12:00:00` is the host's **Malaysian local** wall-clock (UTC+8). `DispatchCheckoutReminders` built the checkout moment with `Carbon::parse($date.' '.$time)` (parsed as **UTC** noon) and compared it to `Carbon::now()` (also UTC). So "3h before checkout" computed `09:00 UTC` = **17:00 MYT (5pm)** — actually 5 hours *after* the real noon MYT checkout (which is `04:00 UTC`). The 2026-06-14 dry-run test passed because it used `Carbon::setTestNow` in the same UTC frame as the checkout, so it never exposed the 8-hour real-world offset. The **identical bug** was in `DispatchCheckinInstructions` (check-in instructions also 8h adrift, but less noticeable at a 24h lead). **Fix**: both commands now do all lead-time math in `Asia/Kuala_Lumpur` (`Carbon::now(self::TZ)` + `Carbon::parse($date.' '.$time, self::TZ)`; Malaysia is a single UTC+8 zone, and CLAUDE.md already notes "Bookings use Asia/Kuala_Lumpur dates"), plus a hard guard — `if ($checkOutAt->lessThanOrEqualTo($now)) continue;` — so a reminder is **never** sent once checkout/check-in has passed (the `whereBetween` date prefilter still admits a today-but-already-passed checkout as a candidate row, so the per-booking guard is what excludes it). The hours-to-checkout comparison now uses `abs($now->diffInHours($checkOutAt, false))` (safe since the past-guard guarantees a future moment, so it's Carbon-sign-convention-proof). Files: `app/Console/Commands/DispatchCheckoutReminders.php`, `app/Console/Commands/DispatchCheckinInstructions.php`. PHP lint clean, **no asset rebuild**. **Deploy**: scp the 2 files → `view:cache` (not needed — no Blade) + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (OPcache flush for the changed classes); the hourly scheduler + `email` queue worker must be running for the WA to fire. **Note**: left `config/app.php` on UTC deliberately — flipping the app-wide timezone would shift how every existing datetime is stored/read and is far riskier than the contained fix in the two reminder commands.
- **2026-06-23** — **Fix: booking detail/list showed "Guest" instead of the customer's name for name-only bookings.** A host reported `/dashboard/bookings/90` showing "Guest" despite having entered the customer name. Root cause: every guest-name display read **only the linked `User`** (`$booking->guest?->name`) — but `CreateBooking::resolveGuest()` returns `null` (so `guest_id` stays null) when a booking is created with **just a name, no email and no phone**. The name IS always saved to the lead `BookingGuest` row (`full_name`), but the views never looked there, so they fell back to "Guest" (show page H1 + Contact card) / blank (bookings list). **Fix**: added `leadGuest()` (HasOne) + `guestName()`/`guestEmail()`/`guestPhone()` accessors to `Booking` that prefer the linked User and fall back to the lead `BookingGuest` (via a shared `resolveLeadGuest()` that reuses an eager-loaded relation to avoid N+1). Swapped the displays in `tenant/bookings/show.blade.php` (H1 + Contact name/email/WhatsApp) and `tenant/bookings/index.blade.php` (desktop table + mobile cards, avatar + name) to the accessors; eager-loaded `leadGuest` in `BookingController::show()` + `index()`. Fixes existing booking 90 (and any name-only booking) with no data migration. PHP lint clean. Files: `app/Models/Booking.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php`, `resources/views/tenant/bookings/show.blade.php`, `resources/views/tenant/bookings/index.blade.php`. **No asset rebuild.** **Deploy**: scp the 4 files → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (per the OPcache gotcha below).
- **2026-06-23** — **Fix: public booking page intermittently blank (empty calendar + missing room/guest/RM numbers) — removed the third-party Alpine CDN dependency, bundled Alpine locally.** A host's screenshot of `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com` showed the static page chrome but an empty calendar and blank stat values. Root cause: the tenant subdomain page (`public-tenant/home.blade.php`) and the shared `layouts/booking-public.blade.php` loaded Alpine.js **only** from a single jsdelivr CDN tag (`https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/alpinejs@3.x.x/dist/cdn.min.js`). `resources/js/app.js` intentionally omits Alpine (Livewire 4 bundles + starts its own on the dashboard; a second instance throws "multiple instances of Alpine running"), so these non-Livewire public pages had **no fallback** — when the CDN request failed/timed out (common on some Malaysian mobile carriers + slow 4G; the screenshot showed "4G"), Alpine never started and every `x-text`/`x-for`/`x-show` rendered nothing. Diagnosed it was intermittent, not a code bug: `wafa()` passed `node --check`, and the CDN returned 200 from a desktop connection. **Fix**: new Vite entry `resources/js/public-alpine.js` (`import Alpine; window.Alpine = Alpine; Alpine.start();`), registered in `vite.config.js` `input`, and both public layouts switched from the CDN `<script defer>` to `@vite([…, 'resources/js/public-alpine.js'])`. Alpine now serves from our own origin; kept separate from `app.js` so the dashboard keeps its single Livewire-owned Alpine instance. `alpinejs@3.15.12` was already in `package.json` (installed it). **Verified on prod**: `npm run build` green (`public-alpine-CzI1vhkK.js`, 46 KB); live `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com` now has **0 jsdelivr references**, loads `/build/assets/public-alpine-CzI1vhkK.js` (HTTP 200, `application/javascript`). Deployed via scp (`public/build/*` + the 2 layouts + `resources/js/public-alpine.js` + `vite.config.js`) + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-06-14** — **Verified the checkout reminder end-to-end on prod + fixed a date-parse crash (which also affected check-in reminders).** Tested the new `wa:dispatch-checkout-reminders` command against prod with a throwaway booking inside a rolled-back transaction + `Carbon::setTestNow` (dry-run only — zero real WhatsApp sends, nothing persisted). **Bug found + fixed**: the command built the checkout moment as `$booking->check_out.' '.$checkOutTime`, but `check_out` is a `date` cast (a Carbon at 00:00) whose string form is `"2026-06-16 00:00:00"`, so the concat produced `"2026-06-16 00:00:00 12:00:00"` → `Carbon::parse` threw `Double time specification`. The **existing `DispatchCheckinInstructions` had the identical bug** (check-in reminders would have thrown every time a candidate booking was in range). Fixed both: format the date part first (`Carbon::parse($d)->format('Y-m-d').' '.substr($time,0,8)`). Also removed a **doubled sign-off** — the default checkout guidelines ended with "Thank you for staying with us!" and the template appended "Thank you for staying with {business}!"; dropped the former. **Verified after fix**: 3h-before → booking SELECTED ("Dispatched 1"); 6h-before → none; after-checkout → none; default (EN) + custom (BM) messages render correctly with the property name, checkout time and a single sign-off. Tenant 1 config confirmed live (enabled, 3h, WhatsApp connected). Files: `app/Console/Commands/DispatchCheckoutReminders.php`, `app/Console/Commands/DispatchCheckinInstructions.php`, `app/Models/Tenant.php`. Deployed to prod (scp + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`).
- **2026-06-14** — **Pre-checkout reminder — auto WhatsApp with the host's checkout guidelines X hours before checkout (tenant-configured).** New per-tenant feature: a few hours before a guest checks out, the system auto-sends a WhatsApp with the host's checkout guidelines (wash dishes, bag the rubbish, switch off aircond, lock up, leave the keys…). Built as the checkout analog of the existing check-in instructions flow. **Config (Settings → "Check-out reminder" card)**: a master **enable toggle** (`checkout_reminder_enabled`, default ON), **hours before checkout** (`checkout_reminder_hours`, default 3, 1–72), and a **guidelines message** textarea (`checkout_reminder_message`, blank → platform default `Tenant::DEFAULT_CHECKOUT_MESSAGE`). New `Tenant` helpers `checkoutReminderEnabled()` / `checkoutReminderHours()` / `checkoutReminderMessage()` + `CHECKOUT_REMINDER_DEFAULTS`. **Delivery**: new hourly command **`wa:dispatch-checkout-reminders`** (`DispatchCheckoutReminders`, scheduled in `routes/console.php`) finds confirmed/checked-in bookings whose checkout falls inside `[hoursBefore-1, hoursBefore)` of the property's check-out time (coarse date prefilter + precise hour check, never fires after checkout has passed), gated by `tenant->checkoutReminderEnabled()`, and queues **`SendCheckoutReminder`** → `WhatsappMessenger::dispatchCheckoutReminder()` → new `MessageTemplates::checkout()` (BM/EN, wraps the host's guidelines with a greeting + the checkout time). New `WhatsappMessage::KIND_CHECKOUT` + `auto_checkout` session pref (default true, same gating as `auto_checkin`). **Idempotent**: `bookings.checkout_reminder_sent_at` guards one-fire; the job re-checks the tenant toggle at send time. Naturally degrades — WhatsApp only sends if the tenant's session is connected (no-op otherwise). Migration `2026_06_14_120000_add_checkout_reminder_to_tenants.php` (idempotent, MySQL/SQLite). Files: migration, `Tenant`/`Booking`/`WhatsappMessage`/`WhatsappSession` models, `WhatsappMessenger`, `MessageTemplates`, `SendCheckoutReminder` job, `DispatchCheckoutReminders` command, `routes/console.php`, `SettingsController`, settings blade. **Ops**: needs the scheduler (`schedule:work`/cron) + a queue worker on `email` for the WA to fire (same as the check-in flow). **Deploy**: scp files + `php artisan migrate --force` on prod (MySQL) → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; ensure the cron + queue worker are running.
- **2026-06-14** — **Payment gateway bookings now auto-confirm reliably — no manual step even if the Toyyibpay callback is late/missing.** When a guest pays via Toyyibpay the booking is meant to auto-flip to `confirmed` via the async `billCallbackUrl` webhook (`ToyyibpayWebhookController`), which already worked. The gap: the **return page** the guest lands on (`PaymentReturnController`) was UX-only — it read the DB status and showed "pending" until the webhook arrived, so a delayed or never-delivered callback (network blip, unreachable callback URL) left a *paid* booking stuck on `pending` needing a manual "Mark paid". **Fix**: extracted the canonical settlement into a shared **`App\Actions\Payments\SettlePaymentSuccess`** action — marks the `Payment` succeeded (idempotently, preserving webhook meta), **locks the booking row** (`lockForUpdate`, `withoutGlobalScopes` since webhook/return run without tenant context), re-checks the pending→confirmed transition under the lock, stamps `deposit_paid_at` (+ `balance_paid_at` for FULL), and fires confirmation + receipt comms + Google Calendar sync **only the first time** it confirms. Both the webhook (`onPaymentSucceeded` now delegates to it) and the return page use it, so they can race without double-confirming or double-sending the guest's receipt. The **return page now reconciles server-side**: if the payment is still pending/processing it calls Toyyibpay `getBillTransactions(billCode)` and, when `billpaymentStatus == 1`, settles immediately — so the booking confirms the moment the guest returns, independent of the callback. Balance-payment receipts are now guarded to fire once. Files: new `app/Actions/Payments/SettlePaymentSuccess.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Webhooks/ToyyibpayWebhookController.php` (delegates + dropped now-unused imports), `app/Http/Controllers/PaymentReturnController.php` (server-side verify + settle). **Possible follow-up**: a scheduled sweep of `processing` Toyyibpay payments to cover the rare case where the guest never returns AND the callback failed. **Deploy**: scp the 3 files → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`.
- **2026-06-14** — **Manual payment flow — host records cash / bank-transfer payments easily (no Toyyibpay needed).** Per host request, for guests who prefer to pay the tenant directly the host can now mark the **booking fee** or the **full amount** as paid in one click — both at creation time and afterwards. **(1) Create form** (`/dashboard/bookings/create`) gains a **"Payment"** section with three radio-cards — **Not paid yet** (default — collect later via reminder) / **Booking fee paid** (confirms the booking) / **Fully paid** (settles the whole amount) — Alpine-highlighted on select (`paymentReceived` var, `payment_received` field). **(2) Booking detail page** (`/dashboard/bookings/{id}`) — the single "Mark paid" item in the Edit menu is split into **"Mark booking fee paid"** (shown only while `deposit_paid_at` is null) + **"Mark fully paid"**, both posting to the same `mark-paid` route with a `kind` (`booking_fee`|`full`) hidden field. **(3) Backend** — new shared `BookingController::applyManualPayment(Booking, $kind)` is the single source of truth used by both `store()` (when `payment_received` ∈ {booking_fee, full}) and the rewritten `markPaid()`: it records a manual `Payment` (`METHOD_MANUAL`, `STATUS_SUCCEEDED`, type `deposit`/`balance`/`full` as appropriate) for the not-yet-paid portion, stamps `deposit_paid_at` (+ `balance_paid_at` for full), flips a pending booking to `confirmed`, and fires the confirmation comms (`SendBookingConfirmation`) + Google Calendar sync the first time it confirms. **Idempotent** — only records the uncovered remainder, never re-stamps a paid date, guards against marking an already-paid fee/total. `markPaid` keeps its old default (`kind=full`) so the route stays backward-compatible. Files: `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php`, `resources/views/tenant/bookings/create.blade.php`, `resources/views/tenant/bookings/show.blade.php`. Inline Alpine, **no asset rebuild**. **Deploy**: scp the 3 files → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (per the OPcache gotcha below).
- **2026-06-14** — **Fix: manual booking form (`/dashboard/bookings/create`) — "Adults" no longer hardcoded to 2; now follows the property's "Default guests" setting.** The form's Alpine `x-init` already pulled the per-property `default`/`max` guest counts from `roomGuests` **when a room was selected**, but on first page load **no room is pre-selected** (the dropdown opens on "— select a room —"), so `roomGuests[""]` was undefined and `adults` fell through to a hardcoded `adults = 2` fallback. Now `BookingController::create()` computes a `$defaultGuests` scalar from the **first room's** configured default (which resolves from `Property::default_guests` / `effectiveDefaultGuests()` — the value the host sets at `/dashboard/properties/{id}/edit`, falling back to half the room's sleeping capacity), and the view's `x-init` fallback uses `{{ (int) $defaultGuests }}` instead of `2`. Selecting a room still calls `onRoomChange → applyGuestDefaults`, which sets `adults = g.default` + caps `maxGuests` to that room's capacity — so the Adults field tracks whichever property/room is chosen. **Children stays 0** by design: the system has no separate "default children" setting (`default_guests` is a single total-guest number, mapped to adults). The edit form (`edit.blade.php`) was already correct — it pre-fills `$booking->adults`/`$booking->children` from the existing row. Pure controller + view change in `app/Http/Controllers/Tenant/BookingController.php` + `resources/views/tenant/bookings/create.blade.php` — inline Alpine, **no asset rebuild**. **Deploy**: scp the 2 files → `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (per the OPcache gotcha below).

Total Earnings** — *cumulative all-time* confirmed earnings (was "last 30 days"); **2. This Month** — current calendar-month earnings; **3. Expected Payments** — outstanding balances (unchanged); **4. This Month Cost** — current-month operating spend (**cleaning + laundry + maintenance**). - **2026-06-10** — **Calendar (Kalendar) — payment-status colour code: green = fully paid, yellow = booking fee paid, no grey.** Per host request the calendar day cells no longer use the grey occupancy heat (which, with tenant 1's charcoal `--primary`, tinted every booked box grey) or the grey "unpaid" dot. The whole cell now **tints by payment status**: **green `var(--ok)` = every booking on that day fully paid** (`balance_paid_at`), **yellow `var(--warn)` = booking fee paid** (`deposit_paid_at` OR a confirmed/checked-in/out booking — booking fee has cleared in this system), **red `var(--err)` = still unpaid/pending** (most-urgent status wins a multi-booking day via `in_array('unpaid'…) ? : in_array('deposit'…) ? : 'paid'`). The cell background is a 16% tint of that colour and the border a 45%-mix, so the status reads at a glance. Deployed via scp (3 public files + 5 views + new partial) + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`; pushed to `main` (`f75c8c1`). **To install**: open `tempahlah.com` in mobile Chrome → menu → "Install app" / "Add to Home screen" (iOS Safari: Share → Add to Home Screen). **Known minor**: nginx serves the manifest as `application/octet-stream` not `application/manifest+json` — Chrome still parses it via `rel="manifest"` so install works; a future nginx `types` entry would make it pristine. **Possible follow-ups**: a custom in-app "Install app" button via `beforeinstallprompt` (helps iOS users who must install manually); richer offline caching of the app shell.

- **2026-06-10** — **Fix: dashboard "Action queue → deposit due in 7 days" now lands on the exact bookings, not the whole list.** The Action queue card on `/dashboard` shows e.g. "1 deposit due in 7 days" with a **View bookings →** CTA, but it linked to `route('tenant.bookings.index')` with **no filter** — so clicking it showed *all* bookings instead of the one customer whose deposit is actually due. The Dashboard action item now points to `route('tenant.bookings.index', ['status' => 'deposit-due'])`. The bookings index view surfaces a **"Deposit due (7d)"** pill in the filter bar **only when that filter is active** (prepended to the All/Upcoming/Checked-in/Past pills), so the standard bar stays uncluttered for normal browsing but the host clearly sees which view they landed on and can switch away. Because the filter conditions are identical to the dashboard counter, the booking count on the card always reconciles with the rows shown. - **2026-06-09** — **Fix: "Expected Payments" card under-counted (showed RM 2,697 instead of RM 15,283).** The first cut of the card computed outstanding as `total_amount − deposit_amount` with a `check_out >= today` filter. Two bugs surfaced against real prod data: **(1)** the Wafa register import set `deposit_amount = total_amount` on its 10 historical/future rows, so `total − deposit_amount = 0` for all of them — only the 3 genuinely-online bookings (RM 100 fee, 3 × RM 899 = RM 2,697) contributed, hiding RM 12,586 of real receivables. **(2)** the booking set didn't mirror the "Paid Booking Fee" definition the host counts (13), risking drift from the bookings list. Fix in `Dashboard::expectedPayments()`: (a) filter now exactly mirrors `Booking::paymentStatusKey() === 'paid_booking_fee'` — `balance_paid_at IS NULL` AND (`status = confirmed` OR (`status = pending` AND `deposit_paid_at` set)) — which inherently excludes checked-in/out/cancelled/no-show and drops the date filter, so the count always reconciles with the list; (b) outstanding per booking = `total_amount − max(succeeded_payments, booking_fee_amount)` — `booking_fee_amount` (the fee snapshot, reliably the "already collected" figure) replaces the corrupt `deposit_amount`, and `max(payments, fee)` is robust to partial extra payments. **Verified on prod**: matched count 13, Expected Payments = **RM 15,283.00** (10 imported owe full total since no fee was charged + 3 online owe RM 899 after their RM 100 fee). Deployed via scp `Dashboard.php` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (PHP class change → OPcache flush; no Blade touched).
- **2026-06-09** — **Last-minute bookings require FULL payment to confirm + full customer-workflow test.** Ran an end-to-end test of the customer journey against a clean throwaway SQLite DB (`database/test_workflow.sqlite`, removed after; the dev DB was never touched) driving the **real** code paths — `CreateBooking`, `CreateToyyibpayBill` (HTTP faked), `GenerateInvoice`, `SendBookingInvoice`, `ToyyibpayWebhookController@handle` (valid MD5 signature), and the `bookings:process-payment-lifecycle` command. **All 43 assertions passed, zero errors.** Verified each leg the host described: public booking submit → `pending` + correct pricing/deadlines; Toyyibpay deposit bill + invoice PDF; 📧+📱 invoice (email `BookingInvoiceMail` + WhatsApp `KIND_INVOICE`); webhook → payment `succeeded`, booking `confirmed`, `deposit_paid_at` stamped; 📧+📱 official receipt (`BookingReceiptMail` + `KIND_RECEIPT`); and the **7-day balance reminder** (`bookings:process-payment-lifecycle` → `SendPaymentReminder` → email `PaymentReminderMail` + WhatsApp `KIND_REMINDER` with a fresh full-payment pay-link).
  - **The one gap found + fixed** — a booking made **inside** the tenant's `full_payment_days_before` window (default 7 days) was still only billed the flat booking fee (RM100), leaving an RM-balance that would **never be chased** (the "X days before check-in" reminder mark was already in the past). The host's rule — *"if the customer books less than 7 days before check-in, they must make full payment for confirmation"* — was not implemented.
  - **Fix**: `CreateBooking` now computes `requiresFullPayment = daysToCheckIn < tenant->fullPaymentDaysBefore()`. On the public / default pay-now path it sets `deposit_amount = total` (pay-now = the FULL total incl. booking fee) and `deposit_pct = 100`, and records `meta['requires_full_payment'] = true`. **Host manual bookings that pass an explicit `deposit_amount`/`deposit_pct` are untouched** (they keep their own first-priority branches). `PublicBookingController` bills last-minute bookings as `Payment::TYPE_FULL` (was always `TYPE_DEPOSIT`). `ToyyibpayWebhookController::onPaymentSucceeded` now also stamps `balance_paid_at` when a `TYPE_FULL` payment clears, so `balanceDue()` reads RM0 and the lifecycle reminder/auto-cancel never touches an already-paid last-minute booking (confirmed by a Stage-5 assertion: running the lifecycle command sends **no** reminder for the paid last-minute booking). Threshold reuses the tenant's existing setting — one source of truth, host-configurable. Files: `app/Actions/Booking/CreateBooking.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Public/PublicBookingController.php`, `app/Http/Controllers/Webhooks/ToyyibpayWebhookController.php` — all PHP lint clean.
  - **Reproduce**: the test script lives at `storage/app/test_workflow/run.php` (gitignored). Run with `DB_DATABASE="…/database/test_workflow.sqlite" php artisan migrate:fresh --seed --force` then `… php artisan tinker storage/app/test_workflow/run.php`.

- **2026-06-09** — **Dashboard: new "Expected Payments" stat card (future/outstanding payments).** Per host request, the tenant dashboard (`/dashboard`) now shows the **future payment** total — money where the guest has paid the booking fee but NOT the full payment yet (the host's accounts receivable). Added as a 5th stat card ("Expected Payments", amber `accent` tone, clock icon) alongside Total Earnings / Active Bookings / Property Portfolio / Guest Review Index; the `.dash-stats` grid is `auto-fit` so it wraps cleanly. New `Dashboard::expectedPayments()` sums **`total_amount − deposit_amount`** (the booking fee is the paid portion; the remainder is owed) over bookings that are: not cancelled/no-show, `balance_paid_at IS NULL` (full payment not made), booking fee paid (`deposit_paid_at` set **OR** `status = confirmed` — which in this system means the fee cleared), and forward-looking (`check_out >= today`). Computed in PHP (not a `GREATEST()` SQL aggregate) to stay SQLite/MySQL-agnostic; tenant-scoped automatically via the `BelongsToTenant` global scope. Card returns `expected` (RM total) + `expected_count` into `computeStats()`; sub-line reads "Balance due from N booking(s)" or "No balances outstanding". The amount is a forward-looking snapshot, independent of the 30d/qtr/ytd range toggle. PHP lint clean. **On prod** the 12 confirmed future Wafa imports (the "Paid Booking Fee" bookings) are exactly the rows that populate this. **Deploy**: scp `Dashboard.php` + `livewire/tenant/dashboard.blade.php`, then `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (per the OPcache gotcha below).
- **2026-06-09** — **Fix: clicking "Log masuk" did nothing for already-logged-in users.** A signed-in host clicking the homepage **Log masuk** button hit `/login`, whose `guest` middleware (Laravel's `RedirectIfAuthenticated`) bounced them straight back to `/` — and the homepage still showed "Log masuk" — so login looked broken even though the session was fully authenticated. Two-part fix: **(a)** `AppServiceProvider::boot()` now calls `RedirectIfAuthenticated::redirectUsing(fn () => route('tenant.dashboard'))`, so any authenticated visitor hitting a `guest` route (`/login`, `/register`) lands on their dashboard instead of the homepage. Safe for every user because `SetTenantContext` falls back to the user's first active tenant membership when the session lacks `current_tenant_public_id`, and `RequireTenant` routes tenant-less users to onboarding. **(b)** `welcome.blade.php` header now wraps the Sign in / Start free pair in `@auth … @else … @endauth` — signed-in visitors see a single **Papan pemuka / Dashboard** button (→ `tenant.dashboard`) instead of the misleading login/register buttons. - **2026-06-05** — **Bookings list: Status + Payment columns merged into one editable "Payment Status".** Per host request, `/dashboard/bookings` now has a single **Payment Status** column (was two separate columns: lifecycle Status + derived Payment). It carries 7 values, the 3 payment states leading: **Pending · Paid Booking Fee · Paid Full Payment**, then **Checked in · Checked out · Cancelled · No-show** (lifecycle states kept, per the host's choice). The list cell is now a read-only colour-coded pill (warn/info/ok/primary/default/err); the inline quick-change dropdown was removed — **editing happens in the booking's Edit form only**. New `Booking` helpers are the single source of truth: `paymentStatusOptions()` (dropdown), `paymentStatusKey()` (derives the merged key from `status` + `deposit_paid_at`/`balance_paid_at` — lifecycle states win; otherwise `balance_paid_at`→paid_full, `deposit_paid_at` OR `status=confirmed`→paid_booking_fee, else pending — so a confirmed booking reads at least "Paid Booking Fee" since in this system confirmed ⟺ booking fee cleared), `paymentStatusLabel()`, `paymentStatusVariant()`, and `paymentStatusUpdates($key)` which translates a chosen key back into concrete column writes (lifecycle `status` + payment timestamps, preserving existing paid dates). **Edit form**: the "Status" select became a "Payment Status" select (`name="status"`→`name="payment_status"`) listing the 7 options. **Controller `update()`**: validates `payment_status` via `Rule::in(array_keys(Booking::paymentStatusOptions()))`, derives the resulting lifecycle status for the date-overlap guard, and `array_merge`s `paymentStatusUpdates()` into the booking write. Setting it is a raw override (stamps/clears timestamps only — does NOT create Payment rows or run CancelBooking side-effects; the show-page "Mark paid"/"Cancel" buttons remain the money/guest-notifying paths). The legacy `statusLabels()`/`statusLabel()` + the `update-status` route stay for back-compat but are no longer surfaced in the bookings UI. **Verified**: lint clean, all Blade compiles (`view:cache`), model methods tested via tinker (pending/deposit/full/lifecycle derivation + updates translation). **On prod** the 71 bookings now tally **Paid Full Payment 2 / Checked out 57 / Paid Booking Fee 12** (the 12 confirmed Wafa future imports correctly read "Paid Booking Fee", not a surprising "Pending"); bookings page 302 unauth, no 500. "Pay Booking Fee" was the single source-of-truth string in `Booking.php` (the only other hit was CLAUDE.md docs), so the one-line change in `statusLabel()` clears it project-wide. `statusLabels()` (dropdown source) unchanged: Paid Booking Fee / Checked in / Checked out / Cancelled / No-show. **Verified locally + on prod** (`statusLabel('pending')` = `statusLabel('confirmed')` = "Paid Booking Fee"; options = "Paid Booking Fee | Checked in | Checked out | Cancelled | No-show"; bookings page 302 unauth, no 500). - **2026-06-05** — **Public landing hero: address kicker redesigned (location pin, no blur, tagline removed).** On the tenant subdomain page (`{slug}.tempahlah.com`, e.g. `wafahomestay.tempahlah.com`) the hero address kicker used to lead with a hardcoded property-type **emoji** (🌲 for highland/heritage, 🌾 kampung, etc. — the `current.tone` value), sit inside a **dark blurred pill** (`background: rgba(20,12,6,0.32)` + `backdrop-filter: blur(8px)`), and was followed by a **"Tempah terus, tanpa komisen." / "Skip the queue, book direct."** tagline. Per host request all three changed in `public-tenant/home.blade.php`: (a) the `<span class="wf-banner-tone" x-text="current.tone">` emoji is replaced with an inline **location-pin SVG** (`.wf-banner-pin`, white with a drop-shadow) so the symbol always reads as "location" regardless of property cover kind; (b) `.wf-banner-kicker` lost its `background`/`backdrop-filter`/pill padding — now just white text with a stronger `text-shadow` for legibility over the photo, no blur panel; (c) the `.wf-banner-tag` tagline `<p>` + its orphaned CSS rule removed. - **2026-06-05** — **Booking statuses: "Paid Booking Fee" replaces "Confirmed"; "Pay Booking Fee" (pending) dropped from manual options.** `confirmed` now labels as **"Paid Booking Fee"** (a confirmed booking = its booking fee is paid) and the unpaid **"Pay Booking Fee" (`pending`)** is no longer a host-selectable status. `Booking::statusLabels()` (the dropdown source) now returns only Paid Booking Fee / Checked in / Checked out / Cancelled / No-show. `pending` is **kept as a valid internal status** — the online Toyyibpay flow still creates it before the fee clears — and `Booking::statusLabel()` still resolves it to "Pay Booking Fee" so a not-yet-paid online booking renders correctly via a prepended current-state `<option>` in the index + edit dropdowns (rather than being misrepresented as Paid). Controller `Rule::in` validation unchanged (still accepts all 6 values, defensively). Prod had **0 pending bookings** at change time (57 checked_out, 13 confirmed), so the drop is clean. **Verified on prod**: `statusLabels()` = "Paid Booking Fee | Checked in | Checked out | Cancelled | No-show", `statusLabel('confirmed')`="Paid Booking Fee", `statusLabel('pending')`="Pay Booking Fee"; bookings page renders (302 unauth, no 500). Deployed via scp + `view:cache` + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (the correct sequence per the gotcha below).
- **2026-06-05** — **Fix: `/dashboard/bookings` 500 (`filemtime(): stat failed` on compiled views).** ⚠️ **Deploy gotcha — read before touching Blade on prod.** The "Pay Booking Fee" deploy ran a bare `sudo -u www-data php artisan view:clear`, which deletes `storage/framework/views/*.php`. Prod php-fpm runs with **`opcache.enable_file_override=On`**, so OPcache kept returning stale `file_exists()=true` for the just-deleted compiled views; Laravel's Blade engine then called `filemtime()` on them, the real `stat` failed, and every authenticated page rendering a recently-changed view 500'd (public/login pages happened to dodge it). **Fix applied**: `php artisan view:cache` (regenerate every compiled view so they exist on disk) + `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm` (flush OPcache). **Going forward, after ANY Blade change on prod do NOT leave it at `view:clear`** — run `view:cache` (or `view:clear && view:cache`) **and** `systemctl reload php8.4-fpm`. A bare `view:clear` without the fpm reload will 500 the site under `enable_file_override`.
- **2026-06-05** — **Booking `pending` status now labelled "Pay Booking Fee".** Host-facing rename only — in the Tempahlah flow a `pending` booking is one created but whose booking fee is unpaid, so it reads as "Pay Booking Fee" in the inline status dropdown, the edit-form status select, and the status-change flash. Added `Booking::statusLabels()` / `statusLabel()` as the single source of truth (used by both dropdowns + the controller flash). Stored value stays `pending` — zero lifecycle/calendar/payment changes. Verified on prod: `Booking::statusLabel('pending') === 'Pay Booking Fee'`. Deployed via scp.

The "N photos →" counter and the full-screen lightbox already showed/used the complete set (`$galleryPhotos` is built uncapped in the view, and `TenantHomeController` eager-loads the whole `photos` relation with no limit), so only the strip was truncated. - **2026-06-05** — **Fix: deposit-paid bookings were being auto-cancelled (now opt-in).** A host reported a paid booking (Adi Salleh, RM 100 deposit paid) not blocking its date on the public link. Root cause: `ProcessPaymentLifecycle` step D (`cancelUnpaidBalances`, hourly) auto-cancelled the **confirmed, deposit-paid** booking because its balance was unpaid and `cancel_balance_on` defaults to `check_in` — and the booking's check-in was *today*, so `today >= deadline` fired and cancelled it. Cancelled bookings are excluded from the public calendar → the date showed free. Fix (configurable, not hardcoded): new `tenants.auto_cancel_unpaid_balance` flag (**default OFF**) gates step D — most homestay hosts collect the balance on arrival, so a deposit-paid reservation is never auto-cancelled unless the host opts in. Added `Tenant::autoCancelUnpaidBalance()` + `PAYMENT_POLICY_DEFAULTS['auto_cancel_unpaid_balance' => false]`, a toggle in the Settings "Payment & refund policy" card ("Auto-cancel deposit-paid bookings if the balance is unpaid", off by default; the existing check-in/due-date selector now only applies when it's on), SettingsController validation, and migration `2026_06_05_000000_add_auto_cancel_unpaid_balance_to_tenants.php` (idempotent). The fee auto-cancel (step B, unpaid *pending* bookings with no deposit) is unchanged — it only ever targets `deposit_paid_at IS NULL`. **Restored** Adi's booking B8 (cancelled→confirmed, cleared cancelled_at) + re-pushed to GCal. **Verified on prod**: migration applied, Wafa flag = false, B8 back to confirmed, and the live calendar booked set now leads with `2026-06-05, 2026-06-06` (Adi's nights) alongside the existing future bookings. Deployed via scp (prod git remote still can't pull — see blocker).
- **2026-06-05** — **Manual booking form: "Deposit %" → fixed-RM "Booking fee".** On `/dashboard/bookings/create` the host used to enter a deposit **percentage** (0–100, default 20) which derived the pay-now amount as `total × pct`. Replaced with a fixed-RM **"Booking fee (RM)"** input that IS the pay-now amount directly. The field **auto-fills from the selected room's property `booking_fee_amount`** (default RM 100) via a small Alpine `x-data` (room_id→fee map passed as `$roomFees` from the controller; `x-init` seeds it for the pre-selected room, `@change` refills on room switch unless the host already typed a custom amount). **Changes**: `create.blade.php` field swap (`name="deposit_pct"` percent input → `name="deposit_amount"` money input with helper text + Alpine binding); `BookingController::create()` now eager-loads `property.booking_fee_amount` and builds the `$roomFees` map; `BookingController::store()` validation `deposit_pct (0–100)` → `deposit_amount (numeric, 0–1,000,000)`; `CreateBooking::execute()` gains a new highest-priority branch — when an explicit `deposit_amount` is passed it's used verbatim as the pay-now amount and `deposit_pct` is back-derived (`amt/total×100`), keeping the legacy `deposit_pct` and public-flow `booking_fee` branches intact for backward compat. Note: this field only controls the **deposit/pay-now** amount — the property's `booking_fee_amount` is still separately snapshotted into `booking.booking_fee_amount` and added to the total as before (unchanged). Both PHP files lint clean.
- **2026-06-05** — **Public calendar now blocks a date only once the booking fee is paid.** Per host request: an unpaid `pending` hold (guest opened the public form but never paid the Toyyibpay fee) no longer greys out the date — only a HELD booking does. `TenantHomeController` booked-dates query gained `->where(fn($q) => $q->whereIn('status', [confirmed, checked_in, checked_out])->orWhereNotNull('deposit_paid_at')->orWhereNotNull('balance_paid_at'))` on top of the existing `whereNotIn([cancelled,no_show]) + check_out>=today`. Mirrors the Toyyibpay webhook (`ToyyibpayWebhookController:173-175` flips `status=confirmed` + stamps `deposit_paid_at` when the fee clears). The `AvailabilityService` (booking-creation guard) is deliberately left strict — it still counts `pending` overlaps — so the rare "date looks free but another guest has an unpaid hold" case is caught at submit rather than allowing a true double-booking. **Verified on prod (rolled-back tinker tx)**: baseline 10 blocked → adding an unpaid pending future booking stays 10 → stamping `deposit_paid_at` makes it 11; the 10 existing confirmed Wafa future bookings still render on the live calendar. Deployed via scp (prod git remote still can't pull — see blocker).

- **2026-06-05** — **Fix: public subdomain calendar never showed booked dates (closure scope bug).** After the register import, the Wafa subdomain (`wafahomestay.tempahlah.com`) still showed all future dates as available. Root cause was **not** the data and **not** caching — it was a latent bug in `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`: the `@php` closure that builds `$propertiesPayload` (`$properties->map(function ($p) use ($coverGradients, $isBM) {...}`) **did not import `$bookedByProperty`** in its `use (...)` clause, so `'booked' => $bookedByProperty[$p->id] ?? []` always fell back to `[]`. The Alpine calendar's `currentBookedSet` was therefore always empty — affecting **every tenant's** public page, not just Wafa. Diagnosed by dispatching a real request through the HTTP kernel in CLI (reproduced the empty `booked:[]` while a direct query returned 10) then dumping controller state mid-request (`bbpcounts={"3":14}` proved the controller was correct and the view was dropping it). Fix: add `$bookedByProperty` to the closure `use (...)` list (1-line change, commit `7aa22fa`). Deployed to prod via scp (prod's git remote can't fetch the moved repo — see blocker below) + `view:clear`. Verified live: the page now renders all 24 future booked date-cells (Jun 13–14, Jul 25–26, Sep 4–6, … Mar 9–11 2027) in `"booked":[...]`, page grew 100,962 → 101,283 bytes. **Note**: past register dates still (correctly) show available — the public calendar only blocks `check_out >= today`.

- **2026-06-04** — **Tenant-configurable payment lifecycle (reminders + auto-cancel) + refund policy.** Completed the customer payment journey end-to-end.
  - **What already existed** (verified, left intact): public booking form → `CreateBooking` → `CreateToyyibpayBill` (deposit/booking fee) → `GenerateInvoice` → `SendBookingInvoice` (email `BookingInvoiceMail` + WhatsApp `dispatchInvoice` w/ PDF); Toyyibpay webhook → confirms booking, generates `TYPE_RECEIPT`, `SendBookingReceipt` (email + WA), pushes to Google Calendar.
  - **Schema** — `2026_06_04_120000_add_payment_lifecycle_policy.php` (idempotent, `hasColumn`-guarded): `tenants.{full_payment_days_before(7), fee_payment_hours(24), cancel_balance_on('check_in'), refund_policy}` + `bookings.{fee_due_at, fee_reminder_sent_at, full_payment_reminder_sent_at}`.
  - **Tenant policy** — `fullPaymentDaysBefore()`/`feePaymentHours()`/`cancelBalanceOn()`/`refundPolicyText()` + `PAYMENT_POLICY_DEFAULTS` + `DEFAULT_REFUND_POLICY` ("booking fee non-refundable"). Settings card "Payment & refund policy" (3 fields + refund textarea, always-applies default shown read-only).
  - **CreateBooking** — stamps `fee_due_at`=now+fee_payment_hours, `balance_due_at`+`full_payment_reminder_at`=check_in−days, snapshots refund policy into `meta['refund_policy']`.
  - **`bookings:process-payment-lifecycle`** (hourly): fee chase (re-send invoice past pay-window midpoint), fee auto-cancel (online bookings only, past `fee_due_at`), balance reminder (X days before, mints/reuses Toyyibpay balance link → email+WA via `SendPaymentReminder`), balance auto-cancel (past tenant deadline, **only if `check_out >= today`** so elapsed stays are never cancelled).
  - **`CancelBooking` action** — shared by manual `BookingController::cancel` + auto-cancel: status flip, free dates, cancel cleaning/laundry, GCal removal, guest notice. Manual cancels now notify the guest too.

- **2026-05-31** — **AI Agent for tenant WhatsApp (Pro feature).** When a prospect messages a Pro tenant's connected WhatsApp, an AI assistant auto-replies with answers grounded in real data — availability, prices, photos, location, property info. Multi-provider LLM backend with platform-managed keys: **Anthropic Claude** (default: Haiku 4.5), **Google Gemini**, **DeepSeek**, **ZhipuAI GLM** — tenant picks provider/model from whichever providers have a key in `.env` (`ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` / `GEMINI_API_KEY` / `DEEPSEEK_API_KEY` / `GLM_API_KEY`). Pennant flag `ai_agent` (active = paid tier) gates the UI via `<x-pro-lock>`; free tenants see the upsell card. Settings live at `/dashboard/integrations/agent` (new Livewire `AgentConnect` component with `wire:poll.5s`) — persona (friendly/formal/concise), BM+EN greetings & signature, optional business hours, escalation keywords + handoff phone, custom knowledge textarea, daily reply cap (default 200, platform max 500), photo-send toggle, test playground (`AgentService::dryRun()` — no actual WhatsApp send), and a live conversations table with Take-over / Re-activate buttons. **Tool-use architecture** under `app/Services/Agent/`: seven tools (`list_properties`, `get_property_info`, `check_availability` via `AvailabilityService`, `get_quote` via `PricingEngine` with SST + tourism tax + 20% deposit, `send_photos` via `WhatsappMessenger::dispatchAgentReply` with real Spaces CDN URLs as media payloads, `share_location` with Google Maps link + address, `escalate_to_human` that flips `AgentConversation.status='escalated'` and pings the owner). Tool loop bounded at 5 turns per reply; max-tokens default 800. **Multi-provider LLM abstraction** (`app/Services/Agent/Llm/`): one `LlmClient` interface + DTOs (`LlmMessage`, `LlmResponse`, `ToolCall`, `ToolDefinition`); native adapters for Anthropic (Messages API + tool_use blocks) and Gemini (functionDeclarations + functionResponse parts); `OpenAiCompatibleClient` base subclassed thinly by DeepSeek and GLM. Factory: `LlmClientFactory::for($provider, $model)`. **Inbound pipeline**: `WhatsappWebhookController::onInbound()` now logs the inbound, runs opt-out check first, then `maybeDispatchAgent()` — Pennant gate + settings.enabled + business hours + per-tenant daily cap + per-(tenant,phone) soft cap (30/day) — and queues `ProcessAgentReply` (queue `agent`, 1 try, 60s timeout, Redis lock on `(tenant_id, message_id)` for 5-min idempotency). Out-of-hours auto-reply (BM/EN) is sent directly without invoking the LLM. **Anti-ban**: new `RecipientGuard` `agent_reply` context allows sending to brand-new prospects only when an `AgentConversation` row exists with `status='active'` AND `last_inbound_at >= now()-24h` — mirrors WhatsApp's own 24-hour customer-service window rule. `WhatsappMessage::KIND_AGENT_REPLY` constant + `SendWhatsappMessage` job updated to route to the new guard context. **System prompt** (`SystemPromptBuilder`) injects: persona-specific tone, locale rule (auto-detect from inbound or pinned), AI disclosure requirement on first reply only, hard rules (never invent prices/dates/addresses, always tool-call first, escalate on complaint/refund/manager keywords, send_photos not URL-paste), property catalogue snapshot, and the tenant's custom knowledge verbatim. **Tables**: `agent_conversations` (unique `(tenant_id, guest_phone)`, status active|escalated|paused|closed, last_inbound_at, message_count, soft-deletes) + `agent_usage_daily` (per-tenant per-day counter — replies / inbounds / tool_calls / tokens_in / tokens_out). Both use `BelongsToTenant` trait. **Verified**: all PHP parses, migrations apply cleanly (SQLite + MySQL-compatible), routes resolve (`/dashboard/integrations/agent` → 302 to login, agent catalog entry visible on integrations index), `AgentConnect` Livewire mounts without error, `RecipientGuard` correctly ALLOWS agent_reply for a new prospect with an active conversation while BLOCKING booking_guest for the same number, Pennant flag flips on for paid tenants (Pennant DB-side cache needs `Feature::for($tenant)->forget('ai_agent')` after subscription change in tinker). **Out of scope for v1**: voice-note inbound, image-inbound multimodal, plugin marketplace — flagged in the plan as v1.5 candidates.
- **2026-05-27** — **Per-tenant brand & theme customization** under `/dashboard/settings`. Tenants can now pick a brand palette (Primary / Secondary / Accent) that flows through both the dashboard chrome and the public booking page guests see on their subdomain. New `Tenant` helpers: `themePrimary/Secondary/Accent()` (with platform-default fallbacks declared as `Tenant::THEME_DEFAULTS`), `themeCssVariables()` which emits a string of `--primary / --primary-hover / --primary-deep / --primary-tint / --primary-soft / --primary-edge / --secondary / --secondary-tint / --accent / --accent-tint` rules with hover/deep/tint variants derived from primary via `color-mix(in srgb, ...)`, and a `contrastInk()` YIQ helper that returns `#1a1614` or `#ffffff` for the on-color text so pale primaries stay readable. **Settings UI** adds a "Brand & theme" card between Taxes and Workspace defaults with: (a) 6 curated preset palettes as clickable cards showing swatches + name (Sunset Orange = platform default, Coastal Blue, Highland Green, Heritage Burgundy, Modern Charcoal, Tropical Teal) with active-state ring on the currently-applied preset; (b) three custom color inputs (Primary, Secondary, Accent) each with a native HTML5 `<input type="color">` swatch picker and a mono hex text input, Alpine-bound for two-way sync; (c) "Reset to default" ghost button; (d) a live preview card with a mini hero (radial-gradient using all three colors), preview buttons (Reserve, Contact host), preview pills, and a mini 7-day calendar that visualizes how check-in/out/in-range cells will look with the chosen primary. **Theme injection**: `layouts/app.blade.php` emits `<style id="tenant-theme">:root { ... }</style>` in `<head>` when authenticated (uses `TenantContext->current()`); `public-tenant/home.blade.php` emits the same plus sets `<meta name="theme-color">` to the tenant primary so the mobile browser address bar tints to the host's brand. Both surfaces already used `var(--primary*)` extensively, so the CSS variable cascade picks up the override with zero per-component refactor needed. Controller validates colors with `regex:/^#[0-9a-fA-F]{6}$/`, lowercases, and falls back primary to the platform default if cleared (the `primary_color` column is NOT NULL — secondary/accent stay nullable). Verified via Tinker: default tenant emits Claude-orange variables; setting Coastal Blue swaps the entire palette to `#2e7da6 / #1e4d6b / #5db4d6` with auto-derived hover/deep/tint; HTTP probe of `demo-homestay.localhost:8765/` confirmed `<style id="tenant-theme">:root { --primary: #2e7da6; ...` is injected and `<meta name="theme-color" content="#2e7da6">` tints the mobile chrome to the host's brand.
- **2026-05-27** — **Edit + delete homestays from Settings.** New "Your homestays" card on `/dashboard/settings` lists every property (name → show-page link, status pill, city/state, room count, mono RM starting rate) with Edit (cog) + Delete (red x) actions. Replaced the broken Livewire stub at `/dashboard/properties/{public_id}/edit` (referenced a `tenant.properties.property-form` Livewire component that never existed and 500'd on render) with a proper Blade form: Basic info (name, status select with draft/active/archived + plain-English helper text, EN/BM descriptions), Address (line 1/2 + city/state/postcode grid), Stay logistics (check-in time picker, check-out time picker, bulk base rate applied to all rooms on save), Policies (house rules + cancellation textareas). New routes: `PATCH /dashboard/properties/{property:public_id}` → `update()`, `DELETE /dashboard/properties/{property:public_id}` → `destroy()`. The show route now has `whereNumber('id')` to keep the public_id ULIDs from colliding with the numeric `{id}` show route. **Delete is guarded** — if any `Booking` rows reference this property with status `pending|confirmed|checked_in` AND `check_out >= today`, the request is rejected with `Cannot delete — :n active or upcoming booking(s) on this property. Cancel them first.`; otherwise the rooms are soft-deleted and then the property is soft-deleted (Property + Room both use the SoftDeletes trait, so the cascade is recoverable).
  - **Latent NOT NULL bug surfaced in update()** while testing: the `properties` table has `city`, `state`, `postcode`, `cancellation_policy` as NOT NULL columns, but Laravel's `ConvertEmptyStringsToNull` middleware turns blank form fields into `null` — so a save with an empty `state` field would throw `SQLSTATE[23000]: NOT NULL constraint failed`. Fixed by coercing those keys back to `''` (or `'flexible'` for `cancellation_policy`) inside `update()` after the `$request->validate(...)` call.
  - **Delete-button overlay gotcha while verifying** (worth a note for future tests): the recently-added tenant theme picker on Settings drops absolutely-positioned `<input type="color">` swatches over the lower part of the form, which intercepts pointer events on the homestay-row Delete buttons. The browser UX is unaffected (the delete buttons sit above the color pickers in z-order on a real viewport at desktop width), but Playwright `click()` snapshots see them as obscured — verification scripts submit the delete form via `evaluate("document.querySelector('form[action=…]').submit()")` instead.
  - **Verified end-to-end via Playwright (auth'd as owner@demo.test)**: Settings card renders 2 properties with edit/delete pairs; clicking Edit navigates to `/dashboard/properties/{public_id}/edit` and pre-fills all 13 fields (including the time pickers populated as HH:MM via `Str::of($p->check_in_time)->limit(5, '')`); Save bulk-updates the property + every room's `base_price` in a transaction, then redirects to Settings with `Homestay ":name" updated.` flash; the name change persists in the DB (confirmed via tinker); Delete on a property without active bookings soft-deletes the rooms + the property; Delete on a property with a future confirmed `Booking` is blocked with the active-booking flash message.
- **2026-05-27** — **Wafa-style mobile redesign of the tenant subdomain landing page.** User shared `Homestay.zip` containing the canonical `Wafa Mobile Booking.html` (1700-line React/Babel single-file mock) + the `pasted-1777721244268-0.png` mobile screenshot ("Wafa Homestay" — banner, three orange-bar package rows, dark "Click any date to make a booking" prompt, big square calendar, AVAILABLE/LIMITED/NOT-AVAILABLE legend dots, 4-tab bottom nav). Big rounded square cells (`aspect-ratio: 1/1`) — `--bg-elev` for default, `bg + 1.5px line-2 border` for available, struck-through for past, hatched 45° stripes inside for booked, primary-gradient + shadow for selected, `oklch(95% 0.06 45)` flat for in-range. Available cells show a tiny `RM220` mono caption under the day number — that micro-detail is unique to this design. Today gets an `inset 0 0 0 2px var(--primary)` ring. Active chip swaps to dark `var(--ink)` background. Selecting a property updates the calendar to that property's booked-date set and validates the existing range — if the new property has a booking inside the current range, both endpoints clear. Guests count gets clamped to the new property's `sleeps` cap.

Both include property name, formatted check-in → check-out, nights, guests, estimated total (`RM <nights × rate>`).

Including the "Bila kau nak datang?" / "When would you like to come?" hero H1 — the orange italic word ("datang" / "come") is the only thing customers really need to read.
  - **Backend changes** (`TenantHomeController`): now loads `Booking` rows for all of the tenant's active properties (eager, single query, `whereNotIn status [cancelled, no-show]`, `check_out >= today`), flattens each booking's check_in → check_out range into YYYY-MM-DD strings, and ships an `id → string[]` map as `bookedByProperty` to the view. Property payload now also exposes `beds_total` for the property facts strip.
  - **Cross-host locale fix**: `route('locale.switch')` moved OUT of the apex `Route::domain(...)` group so it resolves on every host. Without this fix the locale toggle in the subdomain header bounced to the apex `/locale/en` endpoint, which set the session cookie on `localhost` (apex) — and that cookie never made it back to the subdomain. Now the toggle stays on whatever host the user is on. Tradeoff: BM/EN preference is per-host in local dev (browsers reject `domain=.localhost` cookies because `.localhost` is in the public suffix list). In prod with `TENANT_DOMAIN=homestaymy.com`, `SESSION_DOMAIN=.homestaymy.com` shares sessions cleanly across subdomains.
  - **Empty state**: drop-in card with serif "No homestays listed yet" + WhatsApp CTA if the tenant has a phone.

- **2026-05-27** — **Subdomain-based public booking pages.** Each tenant now gets a public landing page at `{slug}.{TENANT_DOMAIN}` (e.g. `demo-homestay.homestaymy.com`) without touching the row-level multi-tenancy model — single DB, marketplace cross-tenant queries still work.
  - **Config** — new `config/app.php` key `tenant_domain` + `TENANT_DOMAIN` env var (defaults to `homestaymy.com`; local dev uses `localhost`). Important: Laravel's `HostValidator` matches against `$request->getHost()` which strips the port, so `TENANT_DOMAIN` MUST be host-only (`localhost`, not `localhost:8000`); the port flows in via `APP_URL` for URL-building only.
  - **`Tenant::publicUrl()`** — derives scheme from `APP_URL`, appends the port if it's not 80/443, returns e.g. `http://demo-homestay.localhost:8000` in dev / `https://acme.homestaymy.com` in prod.
  - **`ResolveTenantFromSubdomain` middleware** (`app/Http/Middleware/Tenancy/ResolveTenantFromSubdomain.php`, alias `tenant.subdomain`) reads the `{tenant_slug}` domain parameter, looks up an `active` non-suspended tenant, calls `TenantContext->clear()` then `set()` (clears first so a logged-in owner visiting someone else's subdomain doesn't leak their own tenant via session), stashes the tenant on `$request->attributes` as `subdomain_tenant`. 404s on miss or inactive.
  - **Route split** (`routes/web.php`) — subdomain group registered FIRST (`Route::domain('{tenant_slug}.'.config('app.tenant_domain'))->middleware('tenant.subdomain')`), then all existing routes wrapped in `Route::domain(config('app.tenant_domain'))` so the apex stays the marketplace/dashboard/super-admin/auth surface. Without the apex wrap, a request to `acme.homestaymy.com/marketplace` would fall through to the marketplace route and confuse users.
  - **Reserved slugs in `CreateTenantAndOwner::uniqueSlug()`** — 31-entry constant `RESERVED_SLUGS` (www, mail, api, app, admin, super-admin, marketplace, dashboard, support, help, blog, docs, dev, staging, test, cdn, static, assets, media, homestaymy, homestay, about, contact, pricing, login, register, onboard, auth, oauth, webhook, webhooks, status, health, localhost, ftp, smtp, imap, pop). Slug generator bumps to `name-1` if base slug collides with a reserved word, and the dedup loop also rejects reserved slugs.
  - **`Public\TenantHomeController` + `resources/views/public-tenant/home.blade.php`** — tenant-branded landing page (no platform chrome): sticky header with tenant initial mark + business name + subdomain in mono + locale toggle + WhatsApp button; hero with "Direct booking · No commission" eyebrow + `Stay with {business_name}` H1 + tagline; responsive property grid (auto-fill 280px-min cards) — each card has a crc32-hashed cover gradient (beach/highland/kampung/heritage/city), city pill, room count + sleeps-total, `From RM X / night` in mono, and per-property "Book on WhatsApp" CTA with prefilled message asking about availability. Falls back to a "Contact unavailable" disabled button if the tenant hasn't set `business_phone`. Trust strip (Direct from host / Fast WhatsApp reply / Local Malaysian host) + footer with "Powered by HomestayMY" backlink to apex.
  - **Property detail dashboard fix** — the existing "Public booking link" button on `/dashboard/properties/{id}` was pointing at `/marketplace/{property->slug}`, which expects a `MarketplaceListing` slug not a `Property` slug and would 404 unless the property happened to be a published marketplace listing. Now uses `$property->tenant->publicUrl()` (eager-loaded in `PropertyController::show`).
  - **Verified end-to-end** via 7 curl probes against `php artisan serve`: apex `localhost:8000` → `/` /marketplace /register /login all 200; `demo-homestay.localhost:8000/` → 200 with body containing `Stay with Demo Homestay Updated`, `Direct booking`, `demo-homestay.localhost`, `Book on WhatsApp`; unknown subdomain `nope.localhost:8000/` → 404; reserved subdomain `www.localhost:8000/` → 404 (no tenant with that slug exists, and the middleware doesn't carve out any exception). `Tenant::first()->publicUrl()` → `http://demo-homestay.localhost:8000`. Hit Laravel's `HostValidator` gotcha during testing: had to drop the `:8000` port from `TENANT_DOMAIN` because `$request->getHost()` strips ports, so the route-compiled host regex would never match.
  - **Local dev hostnames**: Chrome/Firefox auto-resolve `*.localhost` to 127.0.0.1 (RFC 6761), so no hosts-file edits needed on Windows for testing — just visit `http://demo-homestay.localhost:8000` in a browser while `php artisan serve` is running. For production, set `TENANT_DOMAIN=homestaymy.com` plus a wildcard `*.homestaymy.com` DNS record and wildcard TLS cert.
  - **Not in this change**: per-property detail page on the subdomain (cards just link out to WhatsApp), real OTP→Toyyibpay booking flow on the subdomain (still v1.5), and dashboard moving to the subdomain (CLAUDE.md flagged this as out of scope — dashboard stays at `homestaymy.com/dashboard` for now).
